LUK 14:16 Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Vanyi ndǝ saya ɗa kǝra wu yiwu ja tsǝmiya nji aga sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝr mini dǝgalǝu, kǝ ji nggari nji gangǝu.
LUK 14:17 Ənggǝra pǝcir mini kǝ ɗa, kǝ ji sǝwa mafa nyi aga ja maˈyi ja nda nar nyi anǝ nji kǝra ji ngga, ‘Anda mau, arya a fuwar nji kalar sau wu lagu!’
LUK 14:18 Ama kǝ patǝkura nda dzǝgwa na sǝra ɗa nanda aˈyi sǝni shili mai. Ndǝ tanggǝrma na, ‘Dzǝgwa ɗǝlbiya fa nga yau, a ɗar tsaˈa ya mai ya nda lari. Usi mǝliya ɗa mba ɗǝfu.’
LUK 14:19 Kǝ vanyi ndǝ na, ‘Dzǝgwa ɗǝlbiya nga yi thla zǝwa pamǝpamǝ tǝfu, ar lagu nga yi kabangǝkǝ aga ya nda dzǝguya thlǝr nga nda, yu kǝdi ngau, nǝ ɗa lagu.’
LUK 14:20 Kǝ vanyi ndǝ ɓǝra na, ‘Dzǝgwa hǝ mala nga yau, agabangǝ na ya sǝni uya lagu shili mai.’
LUK 14:21 “Kǝ mafa kǝ sha shili ji sa nar nyi anǝ thlagǝri ki nyi sǝˈyar kǝ ndǝ na kau. Kǝ hu ɗa thlagǝri ki nyi ndzǝ gagaɗau, ji dzǝgwa na anǝ mafa nyi, ‘Maˈyi a ndu mǝlmǝˈyar kau kukusa, ga nu lagu dǝgal ǝnga lagu kushu ga nggari ɗa nji tǝtǝ dǝnama, ǝnga nji kukurɓǝu, ǝnga lǝfǝˈyar, ǝnga nji tǝtǝ dzau, ga shili ǝnga nda ǝnggau.’
LUK 14:22 Ənggǝrna, mafa nyi a shiliri ji na, ‘Thlagǝu, sǝra gǝ na patǝ a mǝliya ri nji, ama tsu vi gangǝu kǝra gǝra nyau.’
LUK 14:23 Kǝ thlagǝri ki ɓǝra nar nyi anǝ mafa nyi, ‘Ɓǝra maˈyi a biyar ya mǝlmǝ a ndar lagu dǝgalˈyar ǝnga kusha nyi ga nggari kalar ndǝra gǝ lari aga ki ɗa sa nyau.
LUK 14:24 Ya nar hyi, alaga zǝma njira nji ngga tanggǝrma ta a nda uya nda ɗar sǝ kǝ nji mǝliya aga mini kǝ mai.’ ”
LUK 14:25 Vanyi pǝci nji gangǝu a vǝr nu Yesu, kǝ ji shabiya dzǝ ji na anǝ nda,
LUK 14:26 “Kalar ndǝra shili aga ja nu ɗa, ma naja aˈyi cabiya ɗa yiwukur a ndiya anǝ dǝnyi, ǝnga mǝnyi, ǝnga mala nyi, ǝnga wazha nyi, ǝnga zamǝ nyiˈyar ǝnga kwamǝ nyiˈyar, ǝkkǝˈyi piya ja ǝnga kǝrnyi mai, naja sǝni ɗa zǝmbǝlma ɗa mai.
LUK 14:27 Kalar ndǝra gǝra hǝri wu dladlakǝ nyi, ja dzǝgwa nu ɗa, aˈyi ja kyaga ɗa nǝɗa mai.
LUK 14:28 “Kǝja karapǝ, ma zǝma hyu yiwu ja hǝriya umbwa dzǝgamǝ a dǝmǝlmau, aˈyi ju nggya kwatahǝu, ja tsambiya sǝra hǝri kǝ wu mbari, aga ja tsamiya tara sǝra ara ja a sǝni kuɗǝna hǝra nyi wa?
LUK 14:29 Ma naja aˈyi mǝl abangǝ mai, ma hǝri kǝ taˈyi wu lagura ghar gǝnna, patǝr njira wu nda tǝrabiya wu lagu ta ndu nda nggushi nyi,
LUK 14:30 nda dzǝgwa na, ‘Lari ndǝ kǝ ji dzǝguya hǝri ama naji sǝni kuɗǝna mai.’
LUK 14:31 “Abangǝ tsu ma tǝl kǝra ǝnga njir pa nyi dubu kumou, ju yiwu ja hǝ pa a nda nǝ tǝl kǝra ǝnga njir pa nyi dubu mǝthlǝ kumunyi, aˈyi ju nggya kwatahǝu, ja tsamiya tara dǝnama nǝ pana nji kǝ aˈyi ara ja wa?
LUK 14:32 Ma ji lari abǝr naja sǝni mbari mai, tsu nda naɗǝ ju sǝwa njir sǝ nyiˈyar aga nda ɓasǝwa nda nggya jamǝu.
LUK 14:33 Abangau nga nyi tsu ma ndǝra aˈyi piyari sǝra ara ja patǝ mai, naja sǝni ɗa zǝmbǝlma ɗa mai.”
LUK 14:34 “Unau sǝ mǝsahǝu ngau, Ama ma unǝ caɓǝnakǝr, abar nga ju sǝn shabiya kǝrnyi a shila?
LUK 14:35 Tsu ja sǝn ɗa mǝnahǝ mai, alaga aga gwaɓa, kǝl ba nja pǝna wacu. Ndǝra ǝnga himi ngga, ja nggari.”
LUK 15:1 Ənggǝra njir tsǝm budau ǝnga alenyi “njir bikau” A vǝr shili aga nda ngga highiɓǝ nǝ Yesu,
LUK 15:2 kǝ njir Farisi ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar dzǝguya jiga miya nda vǝr na, “Lari gǝyi! Ndǝ kǝ a shabiya ri ja kǝrnyi bazhiya njir bikau, ǝkkǝˈyi sǝr sǝm nga ju sǝm ǝnga nda.”
LUK 15:3 Kǝ Yesu nar nda najaka karapau:
LUK 15:4 “Nja na zǝma hyi ǝnga tǝmahǝu gharu, kǝ zǝma nyi sanakǝr, aˈyi ju piyari ǝdlǝkumunyi apǝ ǝdlau ar vir ɓǝlari nda, ja maˈyi a nda gal kǝra sa kǝ wa?
LUK 15:5 Maja nǝr nyi ri, hu ɗa ja wu pida, ja dzǝgwa fǝri nyi ar papadla ja,
LUK 15:6 ja hǝri nyi a ndu ki, ja dzǝgwa ngga bazhi nyiˈyar ǝnga njira ju nggya ǝnga nda, ju na anǝ nda, ‘Dlǝwa ɗa mau ǝnga caguli ara a nǝr yau tǝmahǝu ɗa ta sa ta!’
LUK 15:7 Ya vǝr na anǝ hyi, abangau nga nju caguli a dǝmǝlmau ma ndǝ zǝmǝ tubi, a ndiya nji cicau ǝdlǝkumunyi apǝ ǝdlau, kǝra gǝra ɓǝra yiwu tubi.”
LUK 15:8 “Nja na tsu, mala ǝnga kwaɓa nyi kumou, kǝ zǝma nyi sa, mi nga hyu nggani ju nda mǝla? Aˈyi ju mbǝbiya uˈu wu pitǝlla ja dzǝgwa tsǝkǝbiya ki kǝ ǝnga hangǝkal kǝl ji nǝr wa?
LUK 15:9 Maja nǝr kwaɓa kau, ju ngga bazhi nyiˈyar ǝnga tǝwul nyiˈyar, ju na, ‘Dlǝwa ɗa mau ǝnga caguli, ara a nǝr yau kwaɓa ɗa kǝra sa ta.’
LUK 15:10 Abangǝ tsu yu nar hyi, sǝr caguli ngau anǝ waladiˈyar nǝ Hyal ma ndǝ zǝmǝ ndǝr bikau tubi.”
LUK 15:11 Kǝ Yesu dumwa ǝnga ndǝr ji na, “Vanyi ndǝ aˈyi ɗǝɗǝmǝu kǝra ǝnga wazha mǝthlǝu.
LUK 15:12 Zǝr kǝra kushu wu pama nda na anǝ dǝrnda, ‘Tada, nǝ ɗa nji kabangǝkǝ sǝra wu ɗa nǝ ɗa ma ga tǝri.’ Kǝ dǝnyi tǝkǝya nda sǝr fa ki.
LUK 15:13 Ayukuɗa pida kushu, kǝ zǝr kǝ faˈari sǝra ɗar nǝ nyi patǝu, ba ji piyari ki. Kǝ ji maˈyi a ndu vanyi mǝlmǝ kǝra a biyar ya ˈyiˈyir nda. A ndǝna kǝ ji tsǝya sǝra ara ja patǝ a ndu nggya nǝ pǝpǝltǝkur.
LUK 15:14 Ayukuɗa a tsiyari ja sǝra ara ja patǝu, kǝ wuɓau ɗǝmwaˈyi gagaɗau shili wu mǝlmǝ kau, naja tsu a gwar ja wu ɓwaɓwatǝ ara tsu sǝ nyi aˈyi mai.
LUK 15:15 Kǝ ji maˈyi a nda gal sǝr mǝl ara ndǝr mǝlmǝ kau, kǝ ndǝ kǝ sǝwa nyi a nda ɓǝla fǝshiu nyi.
LUK 15:16 Ju gal sǝr sǝm fǝshiu kǝ aga ja sǝmku, ama ndǝr nǝ nyi aˈyi mai.
LUK 15:17 Ənggǝra ji shili wu hangǝkal nyi, kǝ ji na, ‘Kǝja njir mǝl thlǝr anǝ dǝɗa a vǝr tǝtǝl ǝnga sǝr sǝm, nayau ǝtsu a vir tau ǝnga wuɓau ǝnggau!
LUK 15:18 Yu hyaˈari yu sha a ndara dǝɗa ya nda nar nyi, “Tada, a mǝliya ri yau bikau anǝ Hyal, ǝnga anǝ ngau.
LUK 15:19 Nayi ɓǝra ɗa tsaˈa nja ɓǝra ngga ɗa ǝnga zǝr ngǝ mai. Fiya ɗa ya ɗa ǝnggǝr pathlǝu wu pama njir mǝl thlǝr ngau.” ’
LUK 15:20 Kǝ ji hyaˈari ji maˈyi a ndara dǝnyi. “Ma tsu ja naɗǝu, kǝ dǝnyi tsamǝ ri nyi. Kǝ dǝnyi tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya ja, ji dzǝgwa hyaˈari ǝnga hwi, ji nda mbari zǝr nyi, ji dzǝgwa mbunggǝr nyi dzau.
LUK 15:21 Kǝ zǝr nyi na, ‘Tada, a mǝliya ri yi bikau anǝ Hyal ǝnga anǝ ngau. Nayi ɓǝra ɗa tsaˈa nja ɓǝra ngga ɗa ǝnga zǝr ngǝ mai.’
LUK 15:22 Ama kǝ dǝnyi nggari mafa nyiˈyar, ji na, ‘Ənga kusa! Shila mau ǝnga lǝgutǝ mǝnahǝu, hya har nyi. Har nya mau shishiˈwu ǝnga ɓiɓi,
LUK 15:23 nja ɓǝra dla ǝnga thla nggǝnggǝthlǝ ta aga nja tsǝya, aga mǝna sǝm, mǝna caguli.
LUK 15:24 Arya zǝr ɗa kǝ ɗǝɗǝmǝ tǝtǝ nga ja ama kabangǝkǝ a ɗar ja aˈyi ǝnga pi. Ɗǝɗǝmǝ sasa nga ja, ama kabangǝkǝ a nǝr nyir nji.’ Kǝ ndǝ gu caguli gagaɗau.
LUK 15:25 “Wu pǝci kabangǝkau, zǝr dǝgal nyi kǝra maˈyi a gwa tagǝu, a vǝr si nga ja. Ənggǝra ji ɗa lǝhǝu, ba ji nggari nja vǝr tsa kangga, ǝnga nja vǝr fǝl.
LUK 15:26 Kǝ ji nggari mafa ki kau, ji yiwa nyi sǝra a vǝr ɗa.”
LUK 15:27 “Kǝ mafa kǝ na, ‘Mǝshikǝr ngǝ ta ngǝ shili, ca ngǝ dǝr hyi mǝliya nji tsǝya thla nggǝnggǝthlǝ ta ara zamǝ ngau sha shili wu ki jamǝu.’ ”
LUK 15:28 “Ama kǝ hu ɗa zamǝ nyi kǝ ndzǝ gagaɗau, kǝ ji nggǝl ara vu ki. Kǝ dǝrnda biya ji biya sǝsǝkuya nyi kǝr aga ja vu ki.
LUK 15:29 Ama kǝ ji shaɗǝwa nyi anǝ dǝnyi ji na, ‘Lari gǝyi, wu patǝr faˈyar kau, ya vǝr mǝl thlǝr ǝnggǝr mafa, nayi saya nggǝl ara mǝl sǝra gǝ na mai, alaga abangau, nagǝ saya mbari alaga zǝr ku aga ya ngga bazhir ˈwa ɗaˈyar aga ˈya tsǝya ˈya sǝm mai!
LUK 15:30 Ama ǝnggǝra zǝr ngǝ kǝ sha shili, ndǝra maˈyi ka nda tsǝya gǝnna ngau wu sǝsukur, kǝ gǝ dzǝgwa tsǝya nyi thla ta kǝra ndiya ǝnga nggǝnggǝthlau.’
LUK 15:31 Kǝ dǝnyi na anǝ nyi, ‘Zǝr ɗa, alaga nuwa nga gǝ ǝnga yau, patǝr sǝra ara yau, nǝ ngǝ ngau.
LUK 15:32 A ɗar tsaˈa mǝna caguli ǝnga huɗǝ pipida, ara zamǝ ngǝ kǝ a tǝri, kǝ ji ɓǝra sha shili ǝnga pi, ndǝ sasa nga ja, ama kabangǝkǝ a nǝr nyir nji.’ ”
LUK 16:1 Yesu na anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar, “Nji sayi mǝliya vanyi ndǝr bǝrba kǝra nǝ nyi kari nyi anǝ ndǝr dlǝwa nyi aga ja tsamǝ anǝ nyi. Wu yukuɗa nyi, kǝ nji shili ǝnga ɗahǝu anǝ nyi ǝnggǝra ndǝr dlǝwa nyi a vǝr ndza kari nyi.
LUK 16:2 Kǝ thlagǝri ki kǝ ngga ndǝr dlǝwa nyi, ji na anǝ nyi, ‘Mi nga ya vǝr nggari ar kǝra gǝ ka? Shili ga nar ɗa ar kǝra sǝra gǝ mǝlna, ara tsu gu nda nggya ndǝr dlǝwa ɗa mai.’
LUK 16:3 Kǝ ndǝr dlǝwa nyi kǝ na wu ɗǝfuwa ja, ‘Thlagǝri ki ɗa wu nda kǝdlǝ na ɗa wu thlǝr, mi ya dzǝgwa mǝla? Kǝja na ya sǝni zǝwa mai, sǝli tsu wu tǝ ɗa ara kǝdiyau.
LUK 16:4 Ənghǝng! A sǝni yi sǝra ya mǝl, aga nja nda dlǝwuri ɗa a vu kir nda, ma ji kǝdlǝ na ɗa wu thlǝr ɗa.’
LUK 16:5 “Kǝ ji ngga patǝr njira thlagǝri ki nyi a vǝr nu nda mǝl. Ji yiwa ndǝ tanggǝrma ji na, ‘Yiɗau ngǝ thlagǝri ki ɗa a vǝr nu nga?’
LUK 16:6 Ji na, ‘Tǝm nǝr mal gharu.’ “Kǝ ndǝr dlǝwa nyi kǝ na, ‘Hǝri lǝkakaɗǝ ngau, ǝnga kusa, ga tsǝfǝri tǝm tǝfu kumunyi.’
LUK 16:7 Kǝ ji nar nyi anǝ vanyi ndau, ‘Kari nagǝ tsu, yiɗau nga nju nu nga?’ Naja tsu kǝ ji na, ‘Kayiwa uhi gharu ngau.’ Ndǝr dlǝwa nyi kǝ na, ‘Hǝri lǝkakaɗǝ ngau, ga mǝliya ja ɗa buhu cisu kumunyi.’
LUK 16:8 “Kǝ thlagǝri ki ndǝr dlǝwa kǝra gǝra jirkur kǝ faliya nyi ara ji cabiya tsǝtsǝlkur. Arya njir najaka pǝci, a sǝni mǝl thlǝr ǝnga tsǝtsǝlkur nda a ndiya njir lagu mbǝmbǝl.”
LUK 16:9 Yesu dumwa ji na, “Ya vǝr na anǝ hyi, hya mǝl thlǝr ǝnga gǝnnar hyi aga hya uya bazhi anǝ kǝrhyi. Lagu kǝ ngǝ ma thlǝr gǝnnar hyi a taˈyi ri, nju sa dlǝwuri hyi a vu ki nǝ kǝra gǝra kuɗau.
LUK 16:10 Ma ndǝra nju sǝn fiyafǝ ǝnga ja wu sǝ kushu, nju sǝn fiyafǝ ǝnga ja wu sǝ dǝgal tsu. Ma ndǝ kǝra nji gǝra sǝn fiyafǝ ǝnga ja wu sǝ kushu, nju sǝn fiyafǝ ǝnga ja wu sǝ dǝgal tsu mai.
LUK 16:11 Ma nahyi aˈyi mǝl thlǝr kǝra tsaˈa miya ɗǝfu ǝnga gǝnna nǝ duniya mai, wa ngǝ nda fǝr kǝr ǝnga hyi ja nǝ hyi gǝnna nǝ jirkura?
LUK 16:12 Ma tsu nahyi aˈyi mǝl thlǝr tsaˈa miya ɗǝfu ǝnga gǝnna ndǝ mai, wa nga nda nǝ hyi nǝr hya gǝnna?”
LUK 16:13 “Ndǝr sǝn mafakur anǝ thlagǝr ki pamǝpamǝ mǝthlǝ aˈyi mai, ara ju nda yiwu vanyi ba ja piyari vanyi ǝnga ju nda hǝya kǝr anǝ vanyi ba ja diɗana vanyi. Nahya sǝn daɓǝri nu Hyal ǝnga gal gǝnna mai.”
LUK 16:14 Njir Farisi njir yiwu gǝnna ngau, ǝnggǝra ndǝ nggari sǝra Yesu na ba ndǝ tsǝrauna nyi.
LUK 16:15 Ama kǝ Yesu na anǝ nda, “Nahyi ngǝ njir yiwu hya canǝ nyi anǝ nji abǝr nji cici nga hyi. Ama Hyal ju sǝni ɗǝfuwa hyi. Sǝra nju lǝ dǝgalkur anǝ nda, nanda ngǝ didiɗi wu mwar Hyal.”
LUK 16:16 “Kǝl ta Yahwana ndǝr mǝl Baɓǝtizǝma shili, highiɓǝ nǝ dlaɗǝ nǝ lagu Musa ǝnga nǝ nabiˈyar ca ngǝ ǝnga nju mǝl thlǝr ǝni. Ama dzǝguya ǝnga Yahwana ndǝr mǝl Baɓǝtizǝma, ǝnggǝra nji tǝtǝlna ndǝshigu mǝsahǝu nǝ tǝlkur Hyal, kalar ndau a vǝr gal lagu aga ja ɗa a gwa.
LUK 16:17 Dǝmǝlmau ǝnga gyuˈyi a sǝni sanakǝr, a ndiya sǝ ǝnggǝr camwaɗi wu ndǝr zǝmǝ sara wu dlaɗǝ nǝ lagu Musa a tǝɗau a gyuˈyi.
LUK 16:18 Ndǝra kǝdlǝna mala nyi, kǝ ji hǝr vanyi mala, ndǝr dlǝnga mala ngau. Ənga tsu sal kǝra hǝri mala kǝra sal nyi kǝdlǝna ndǝr dlǝnga mala nga ja.”
LUK 16:19 “Vanyi ndǝr gǝnna aˈyi kǝra wu ha kari nǝ gǝnna gangǝu pamǝpamǝu, ǝnga ju sǝm sǝr sǝm mǝsahǝu kalar pǝci.
LUK 16:20 A biya miya ki nyi, vanyi ndǝr kǝdi aˈyi kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Liyazaru, ǝnga dza ja patǝ ǝnga mbǝlgǝu. Nju shili ǝnga ja, nja sa pina nyi ǝna kalar pǝci.
LUK 16:21 Naja tsu ǝnga huɗǝ pipida ma ji sǝni uya alaga sǝra tǝɗau sara dar vir sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝ ndǝr gǝnna kau, patǝ ǝkkǝˈyi hya wu sa naɗǝ mbǝlgǝ nyi kau.”
LUK 16:22 “Pǝci shili ba ndǝr kǝdi kǝ tau, kǝ waladiˈyar hǝri nyi ka nda fiya nyi ar vir nggya mǝnahǝu ǝnga Ibrahimu. Ətsu ba ndǝr gǝnna kǝ tau ba nji haɗǝna nyi.
LUK 16:23 Ji thlǝwa kǝrnyi wu uˈur kǝtsa, ja vǝr sa ɓwaɓwatǝu. Ənggǝra ji hyaˈanakǝr a dǝmǝlmau, kǝ ji lari Ibrahimu naɗǝ nanda ǝnga Liyazaru.
LUK 16:24 Kǝ ji ngga nyi, ji na, ‘Tada Ibrahimu, tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya yau, ga sǝwa Liyazaru aga ja fuwa zǝr tsa ja a gwu ˈyimi aga ja fǝri ar kyara yau ya nggari shishiˈwu, arya ya vir lari ɓwaɓwatǝ wu uˈu kau!’
LUK 16:25 “Ama kǝ Ibrahimu na, ‘Zǝr ɗa, ga ɗǝngari ja, pǝci kǝra gu duniya, nagǝ ǝnga sǝ mǝnahǝu papatǝu, ama Liyazaru nǝ nyi a lari ja ɓwaɓwatǝu. Ama kabangǝkǝ pǝcir nggari mǝsahǝkur nyi ngau, ama nagau wu ɓwaɓwatǝ nga ngau.
LUK 16:26 Kǝ ma mai, wu pama ˈya ǝkkǝˈyi hyi kaˈu dǝgal ǝnga dzǝgamǝ aˈyi, kǝra nji mǝliya ara nja sara vǝlna sara ndara hyi a shili ngau, alaga sara ngau a ndara hyi.’
LUK 16:27 Kǝ ndǝr gǝnna kǝ na, ‘Tada, ma abangǝ ja, yu kǝdi ngau, sǝwa nyi a ndu ki dǝɗa,
LUK 16:28 arya zamǝɗaˈyar aˈyi tǝfu, ja maˈyi ja nda kughiya nda, a sara nda ɓǝra shili ngǝ ǝtsu, a shili wu ɓwaɓwatǝu.’
LUK 16:29 “Ibrahimu shaɗǝwa nyi, ‘Zamǝ ngǝˈyar aˈyi nda ǝnga highiɓǝ nǝ Musa ǝnga tsǝfǝ nǝ nabiˈyar, nda sǝ himi sǝra ndu na.’
LUK 16:30 Kǝ ndǝr gǝnna shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, ‘Awau, tada Ibrahimu, ma ndǝ hyaˈari sara vir tau ji sha ndara nda, ndu tubi.’
LUK 16:31 Ama kǝ Ibrahimu na, ‘Ma tsu nanda aˈyi nggari highiɓǝ Musa ǝnga tsǝfǝ nabiˈyar kǝ mai, alaga vanyi ndǝ hyaˈari sara vir tau, nanda sa sǝ himi anǝ nyi mai.’ ”
LUK 17:1 Yesu na anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar, “Sǝra wu daɓaga mǝliya nji nda mǝliya bikau aˈyi cumu. Ama sǝr tǝhuɗǝ anǝ ndǝra ju shili lagu nyi.
LUK 17:2 Kuji anǝ nyi, nja mbiya bǝra ar fǝlanga ja, ba nja vakuwa nyi a gwar dǝl dǝgal a ndiya ja mǝliya zǝmǝ wu wazha yiɗiɗǝˈyar kǝ njir nu ɗa mǝliya bikau.
LUK 17:3 Hya tsamǝ sǝra hya mǝl ja. “Ma zamǝ ngau mǝliya ngǝ bikau, ga kughiya nyi, ma ji na a tubir yau, tǝfǝbiya nyi.
LUK 17:4 Ma ji mǝliya ngǝ bikau pamǝpamǝ mǝɗǝfǝ wu pǝkǝ pathlǝu, kǝ ji ɓǝra sha shili ja vǝr na, ‘A mǝliya ngǝ ri yi bikau yafa ɗa,’ ba ga tǝfǝbiya nyi.”
LUK 17:5 Kǝ cama sǝsǝˈyar kǝ na anǝ Thlagǝu, “Cakǝri mbǝrsar ˈya ja ɗa ǝnga dǝnama!”
LUK 17:6 Kǝ Thlagǝ shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Ma mbǝrsa hyi aˈyi ǝnggǝr culi bǝla, gu sǝni na anǝ wu dǝgal kau, ‘Kucina kǝr ǝnggau ga ciya kǝr a gu tsadau,’ ju nda mǝl sǝra gǝ na.”
LUK 17:7 “Ma mafa ngǝ si sara a gwar vi zǝwa ǝnga sara vir ɓǝla, gu nda na anǝ nyi, ‘Usi ǝnga si! A ndau ga nggya, ga sǝm sǝr sǝm ya?’
LUK 17:8 Awau, ngu nda na anǝ nyi, ‘Mǝliya ɗa sǝr sǝm nǝ wagǝu kwatahǝu, ga dzǝgwa tsǝrpǝri kǝrngau ba ga hǝri ɗa a shili ya sǝm ya sa, kadivira ga dzǝgwa sǝm ga sa nǝ ngau’
LUK 17:9 Gu nda na usi anǝ mafa ngau ara ji mǝliya sǝra tsaˈa ja mǝl ya?
LUK 17:10 Abangǝ nga hyi tsu, ma hya mǝliya ri sǝra thlagǝr kir hyi nar hyi hya mǝl, hyu nda na, ‘Naˈya mafa ngǝ wacu. A mǝliya ri ˈya sǝra nju yiwu ˈya mǝl.’ ”
LUK 17:11 Ənggǝra Yesu mbari lagu ja vǝr maˈyi a vu Urshalima, ndǝ dzǝgwa ɓau wu kǝl kǝra wu pama Samariya ǝnga Galili.
LUK 17:12 Ənggǝra ja vǝr vu mǝlmau, kǝ njir pibi kumo thlǝwa nyi. Ndǝ taˈyi tuwara tsalǝu,
LUK 17:13 ndǝ dzǝgwa ngga ǝnga ɗahǝu dǝgalǝu, “Yesu ndǝ dǝgalǝu! Ga tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya ˈya!”
LUK 17:14 Ənggǝra Yesu lari nda, kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Ma ˈya mau hya nda canǝ nyi kǝrhyi anǝ pubu.” Kǝ ndǝ maˈyi, ar lagu ba ndǝ ɗa jamǝu.
LUK 17:15 Pathlǝ wu pama nda, lari abǝr a ɗar ja jamǝu, kǝ ji sha shili, ja vǝr fal Hyal ǝnga ɗahǝu dǝnama gagaɗau.
LUK 17:16 Ji ɓǝliya undi a dumwar Yesu, ja vǝr usa nyi. Naja tsu ndǝr Samariya ngau ndǝra nji diɗana.
LUK 17:17 Kǝ Yesu yiwa, “Aˈyi nji kumo nga nji mǝliya jamǝ wa? Əmani ngǝ alenyi nji ǝdlǝ ka?
LUK 17:18 Mi ngǝ ɗa kǝl mǝthlǝpi kǝ ngǝ sha shili ja sa cabiya usaku nyi anǝ Hyala?”
LUK 17:19 Yesu dzǝgwa na anǝ nyi, “Hyaˈari ga maˈyi sǝ ngau, mbǝrsa ngau a mǝliya ngǝr jamǝu.”
LUK 17:20 Alenyi njir Farisi yiwa Yesu pǝci kǝra tǝlkur Hyal wu nda shili, kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Shiliri tǝlkur Hyal aˈyi ǝnga li ǝnga nju nda tsamiya mai,
LUK 17:21 ndǝr nda na tsu, ‘Kǝja ja,’ ǝnga ‘Wa ta ja,’ aˈyi mai, arya tǝlkur Hyal wu pama hyi nga ja.”
LUK 17:22 Kǝ Yesu dzǝgwa na anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar, “Pǝci a vǝr shili kǝra gu nda yiwu ga lari zǝma pǝci nǝ Zǝr Ndau, ama na ga nda lari mai.
LUK 17:23 Nju nda na anǝ hyi, ‘Wa ta ja a ndǝna,’ ǝnga tsu ‘Kǝja ja ǝnggau.’ Ama hya sara maˈyi hya nda tsamǝ nyi mai.
LUK 17:24 Ənggǝr sǝm nǝ par kǝra wu cabiya mbǝl nyi ar kuɗiyar mǝlmǝ baˈanǝ vanyi kuɗiyar mǝlmǝ kǝra kalar ndau wu lari, abangǝ shiliri Zǝr Ndau wu nda ɗa.
LUK 17:25 Ama tanggǝrma kǝl ji lari ɓwaɓwatǝ gagaɗau kwatahǝu ǝnga tsu nji kabangǝkǝ nda piyari nyi.
LUK 17:26 Ənggǝra ji ɗa ar pǝcir Nǝhu, abangǝ nga nyi wu nda ɗa ar pǝcir shilǝr Zǝr Ndau.
LUK 17:27 Nji nggya kǝl sǝm sǝr sǝm ǝnga sa sǝ sasa, ndu faˈa mathlǝkǝˈyi ǝnga ndu lǝ kuˈyi anǝ shili, baˈanǝ shili ar pǝci kǝra Nǝhu gwu kwambwal dǝgal ta ari. Kǝl ta dǝl shida ba ji kuɗǝna nji patǝu.
LUK 17:28 “Abangǝ nga nyi ɗa tsu ar pǝcir Lotu. Nji kǝl sǝm, ǝnga sa, ndu ɗǝl ǝnga ɗǝlna, alenyi nji kǝl thlǝka sǝ pamǝpamǝ ǝnga hǝr ki.
LUK 17:29 Ama pǝci kǝra Lotu piyari Sodomu, kǝ uˈu ǝnga hakil uˈu shida sara dǝmǝlmau ba ji dlǝna nda patǝu.
LUK 17:30 “Tangǝ ǝnggǝr ta nga nyi wu nda ɗa ar pǝcir shilǝr Zǝr Ndau.
LUK 17:31 Ar pǝci ta, ndǝra a dar kǝra umbwa, ja sara gya ja vu ki aga vuwa hǝ sǝ mai, ara ja sara sana pǝci.” “Ndǝra a gwa tagǝ tsu, ja sara sha a su ki aga sa hǝ kar ha nyi mai.
LUK 17:32 Hya ɗǝngari sǝra ɗa ǝnga mala Lotu!
LUK 17:33 Kalar ndǝra wu yiwu piya ja, ju nda tini. Ndǝra gǝra yiwu piya ja arya yau, ju nda uya.
LUK 17:34 Yu nar hyi ja, pǝci kǝra sǝ kǝ wu nda ɗa, nji mǝthlǝ a vǝr pida ar sǝr pida zǝmǝ ba nja hǝri zǝmǝ ba nja piyari vanyi.
LUK 17:35 Mathlǝkǝˈyi mǝthlǝ a vǝr au ar ɓǝra, ba nja hǝri zǝmǝ ba nja piyari vanyi.”
LUK 17:37 Kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar yiwa nyi, ndǝ na, “Thlagǝu, ǝman na?” Kǝ ji shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Ma vi kǝra sǝ tǝtǝ ari ǝna ngǝ kwadǝgǝu wu daɓau.”
LUK 18:1 Yesu nar nyi najaka karapǝ anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar aga ja highiɓǝri nda aga nda dumwa ǝnga ndǝr anǝ Hyal parangǝ, a sara nda hǝɗa mai.
LUK 18:2 Ji na, “Wu vanyi mǝlmǝ vanyi ndǝr pathla aˈyi kǝra gǝra hivǝr Hyal ǝnga kǝra gǝra tal nji.
LUK 18:3 Wu mǝlmǝ kǝ vanyi malatǝsal aˈyi kǝra a vǝr shili parangǝ ǝgya ndǝr pathla ja vǝr kǝdi nyi ju na, ‘Dlǝwari ɗa ga nǝ ɗa sǝra tsaˈa aga nǝ ɗa a dumwar dawa ɗa.’
LUK 18:4 Tanggǝrma ba ji nggǝl, ama wu yukuɗǝ kǝ ji na wu ɗǝfuwa ja, ‘Alaga kǝ aˈyi yu hivǝr Hyal mai, nayi tsu wu tal nji mai,
LUK 18:5 ama ara ǝnggǝra mala kǝ ɓwanǝ ɗa kǝr ǝnga shili ar kǝr ar kǝr, yu nǝ nyi sǝra ju yiwu kau, a sara gangǝkura shili nyi kǝ a nda nǝ ɗa hǝɗa!’ ”
LUK 18:6 Kǝ Thlagǝ na, “Nggara mǝ ja sǝra ndǝr pathla kǝra gǝra jirkur kǝ na!
LUK 18:7 Kǝ hyi nggani, Hyal a yiwu nda nǝ nyi sǝra tsaˈa anǝ nji nyi kǝra ji ɗǝmbiya kǝra wu tiwi anǝ nyi vuˈyi ǝnga puci sǝra ndu kǝdi wa? Naja ˈyi wu nda dlǝwari nda ǝnga kusa wa?
LUK 18:8 Yu na anǝ hyi, ju nda nǝ nda sǝ tsaˈa kǝra ndu kǝdi kukusa. Ama ma Zǝr Ndau wu nda sha shili, wu sa thlǝwa ja njir mbǝrsa wu duniya kǝ ya?”
LUK 18:9 Yesu na najaka karapǝ anǝ njira hǝri Kǝrnda abǝr nji tsapǝu nga nda, nda dzǝgwa diɗana alenyi nji.
LUK 18:10 Ji na, “Nji sayi mǝliya nji mǝthlǝ kǝra maˈyi a gwu ki Hyal aga nda gwa ndǝr ǝnga Hyal. Pathlǝ wu pama nda ndǝr Farisi, ǝnga vanyi ndǝ kǝ ndǝr tsǝm budau.
LUK 18:11 “Kǝ ndǝr Farisi hyaˈari ji taˈyau, ji dzǝguya ndǝr anǝ Hyal ja vǝr na, ‘Hyal, a usa ngǝ ri yau ara nayau aˈyi ǝnggǝr alenyi nji mai, njir hǝl, njir dlǝrbau, nji sǝsu. Nayi tsu aˈyi ǝnggǝr ndǝr dlǝwu budǝ kǝ mai.
LUK 18:12 Yu hǝ zǝmǝtsini mǝthlǝ wu sugu, yu hǝbiya pathlǝu wu sǝ kumo patǝ kǝra yi uya.’
LUK 18:13 “Ama kǝ ndǝr dlǝwu budǝ kǝ taˈyu naɗǝu, naja aˈyi ɗa tsaˈa ja hyaˈana liya ja a dǝmǝlmǝ mai, kǝ ji cabiya tǝtǝwakur nyi, ja vǝr na, ‘Hyal, tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya yau, nayi ndǝr bikau!’ ”
LUK 18:14 Yesu na, “Yi wu na nǝ hyi, ndǝr tsǝm budau, ji sha a ndu ki nyi gǝra bikau wu mwar Hyal, aˈyi ǝnggǝr ndǝr Farisi mai. Arya kalar ndǝra hǝri kǝrnyi, nju nda hǝya nyi. Ama ndǝra hǝya kǝrnyi, nju nda hyaˈana nyi.”
LUK 18:15 Alenyi nji shili ǝnga wazha aga Yesu a fǝnggǝr nda barka. Ənggǝra zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar lari abangau, ba ndǝ tsa ar kǝra nda.
LUK 18:16 Ama kǝ Yesu ngga wazha, ji na, “Piyara mau wazha yiɗǝɗǝ nda shili ǝgya yau. Hya sara ka nda mai. Arya, tǝlkur Hyal anǝ nji ǝnggǝr nanda nga nyi.
LUK 18:17 Ənga jiri yu na anǝ hyi, kǝmir ndǝra gǝra dlǝwuri tǝlkur Hyal ǝnggǝra zǝr kushu wu dlǝwu, naji wu sǝn vwagwa mai.”
LUK 18:18 Vanyi ndǝr tǝɗǝmwa nǝ Yahudiya yiwa Yesu ji na, “Malǝmǝ, ndǝ mǝnahǝu, mi nga ya mǝl ya uya pi gǝra kuɗa?”
LUK 18:19 Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Ara mi gu ngga ɗa ndǝ mǝnaha? Ndǝ mǝnahǝ aˈyi mai kǝl Hyal wacu.
LUK 18:20 A sǝni gau sǝra dlaɗau cabiya, ‘Ga sara tsa ndǝ mai. Ga sara mǝl sǝsukur mai. Ga sara hǝl mai. Ga sara thla fati ar kǝra ndǝ mai. Ga sara dlǝrbǝ ndǝ mai. Ga gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli anǝ dǝngǝ ǝnga mǝngau.’ ”
LUK 18:21 Kǝ zǝr baduwari ta na anǝ nyi, “A ɓǝlar yi sǝˈyar kǝ patǝ tsu yi zǝr kushu. Mi ngǝ sǝra hya?”
LUK 18:22 Yesu nar nyi, “Sǝ zǝm wacu ngǝ hyau anǝ ngau, ma gu yiwu ga ɗa ndǝ tsapǝu, ga maˈyi ga nda ɗǝlna patǝr sǝra ara gau, ba ga tǝkǝna gǝnna nyi anǝ nji ɗaɗali, gu uya akkǝri a dǝmǝlmau. Ba ga dzǝgwa shili aga ga sa nu ɗa.”
LUK 18:23 Ənggǝra ji nggari abangau kǝ zǝr baduwari kǝ ndalǝr bama, kǝ ji maˈyi ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzau, ara naja ndǝr bǝrba gagaɗau.
LUK 18:24 Ənggǝra Yesu lari ɗǝfuwa ja a ndzǝ ri, kǝ ji na, “Wu nda ɗa dzadzau gagaɗau anǝ njir gǝnna nda gwu tǝlkur Hyal!
LUK 18:25 Arya wu nda ɗa ɓatsǝ anǝ dlǝgwam ja tǝrabiya wu liya libǝra, a ndiya ndǝr gǝnna ja vu tǝlkur Hyal.”
LUK 18:26 Njira nggari ndǝr kǝ ndǝ yiwa nyi, ndǝ na, “Ma abangǝ nga nyi, wa ngu sǝn uya mbǝɗa?”
LUK 18:27 Yesu na, “Sǝra gǝra sǝn ɗa ngau, anǝ ndau, ama anǝ Hyal ɓatsu.”
LUK 18:28 Kǝ Biturusu shaɗǝwa, ji na, “Kǝja ˈya piyari sǝ patǝ ˈyi nu ngau.”
LUK 18:29 Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Wu sǝn yau abangǝ, yu nar hyi jirkura nyi tsu, kalar ndǝra piyari ki ǝnga zamǝˈyar, ǝnga kwamǝˈyar, ǝnga tada ǝnga ama ba ǝkkǝˈyi wazha ǝnga fa arya tǝlkur Hyal
LUK 18:30 ju nda uya gangǝu a adabanga sǝˈyar kǝ ji piyari ǝnggau wu duniya kau, wu duniya kǝra wu shili kǝ tsu pi kǝra kuɗau.”
LUK 18:31 Kǝ Yesu hǝri zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ a ndar batiti, ji na anǝ nda, “Kǝja, mǝn wu mai a vu Urshalima, vi kǝra sǝra nabiˈyar tsǝfǝri ar kǝra Zǝr Ndau wu nda nyabiya dzau.
LUK 18:32 Nju nda lǝri nyi anǝ njira aˈyi njir Yahudiya mai, aga nda diɗana nyi, nda nǝ nyi ɓwaɓwatǝu, nda dzǝgwa tǝfǝri nyi tuli.
LUK 18:33 Ndu nda dǝgǝ nyi ǝnga wuɗa, nda tsǝya nyi, ama pida makǝrkura nyi ba ja hyaˈari sara vir tau.”
LUK 18:34 Ama zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar nggabiya sǝ kǝ Yesu na kǝ mai. Ɗǝɗǝwa ngǝ sǝra ndǝr kǝ cabiya anǝ nda, ca ngǝ ɗa nandǝ sǝni nggabiya mai.
LUK 18:35 Ənggǝra Yesu dla lǝhǝu wu dzǝri Yariko, kǝ ja ndǝ lǝfau a vǝr nggya ar thlǝr pa lagu, ja kǝdiyau.
LUK 18:36 Ənggǝra ji nggari nji gangǝu a vǝr tǝrabiya, kǝ ji yiwa sau ji na, “Mi nga vǝr ɗa?”
LUK 18:37 Kǝ ndǝ na anǝ nyi, abǝr, “Yesu ndǝr Nazǝratu nga vǝr tǝrabiya.”
LUK 18:38 Kǝ ji hyaˈana ɗahǝu ji na, “Yesu! Zǝr Dawuda! Tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya yau!”
LUK 18:39 Njira a dumwa ndǝ kughi anǝ nyi aga ja haɗiya miya ja. Ama kǝ ji ɓǝra hyaˈana ɗahǝu gagaɗau ja vǝr na, “Na gǝ, Zǝr Dawuda, tǝhuɗǝ ǝgya yau!”
LUK 18:40 Kǝ Yesu taˈyau, ji na, “Shila mau ǝnga ja ǝnggau.” Ənggǝra ji shili lǝhǝu, Yesu yiwa nyi,
LUK 18:41 “Mi nga gu yiwu ya mǝliya nga?” Kǝ lǝfǝ kǝ shaɗǝwa, ji na, “Thlagǝu, ya yiwu ya lari sau.”
LUK 18:42 Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Lari sau! Mbǝrsa ngau a pahǝnari liya gau.”
LUK 18:43 Aga zǝmǝ kǝ liya ja lari sau, kǝ ji nu Yesu, ja vǝr dlǝvǝ Hyal. Ənggǝra nji lari sǝ kǝ ɗa kau, kǝ ndǝ patǝ fal Hyal.
LUK 19:1 Yesu vu Yariko, ja vǝr tǝrabiya wu hu ɗa mǝlma nyi,
LUK 19:2 kǝ ja vanyi ndǝ dǝgal nǝ njir tsǝm budau, kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Zakka. Naja tsu ndǝr gǝnna,
LUK 19:3 ji ɗa aga ja lari tara wa ngǝ Yesu, ama naji sǝni lari nyi mai ara naja ndǝ tashu, ǝnga tsu nji gangǝ gagaɗau.
LUK 19:4 Agabangǝ kǝ ji maˈyi a dumwa ǝnga hwi, kǝ ji thlǝwa wu bǝla kǝ ji dagwa, aga ja lari nyi, arya Yesu wu nda tǝrabiya lagu ta.
LUK 19:5 Ənggǝra Yesu thlǝwa vi ta, kǝ ji hyaˈanakǝr a dǝmǝlmau ji na, “Zakka, kusa ga shida! Əshina yu ɗa mǝthlǝpi wu ki ngau.”
LUK 19:6 Zakka gya ǝnga kusa, ji dlǝwuri nyi ǝnga huɗǝ pipida.
LUK 19:7 Ənggǝra nji lari abangau, kǝ ndǝ mbari ngwungwuni, nda vǝr na, “Kǝja! Wu ki ndǝr bikǝ nga ji ɗa mǝthlǝpi.”
LUK 19:8 Kǝ Zakka hyaˈari aˈyi taˈyau, ji na anǝ Thlagǝu, “Nggari, ndǝ dǝgal, yu tǝkǝya sǝra ara yau bwata mǝthlǝu, ba ya tǝkǝna pathla nyi anǝ nji tǝtǝ dǝnama. Patǝkura njira nyi dlǝrbǝri, yu nda shabiya nda sǝr nda aga foɗǝu.”
LUK 19:9 Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Əshina ma, mbǝɗau a shiliri wu ki kau, naja ma culi Ibrahimu ngau.
LUK 19:10 Arya Zǝr Ndau ji shili aga sa gal nji sasa, ǝnga ja sa canǝ nda lagur mbǝɗau.”
LUK 19:11 Tsu nda vǝr sǝ himi sǝˈyar kau, kǝ Yesu dumwa ǝnga na vanyi karapǝ anǝ nda, ara a ɗar lǝhǝu wu dzǝri Urshalima, ǝnga nja vǝr ɗǝnga abǝr tǝlkur Hyal wu cabiya dzǝ aga zǝmǝu.
LUK 19:12 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Nji sayi mǝliya vanyi ndǝ dǝgal kǝra maˈyi a ndu vanyi mǝlmǝ naɗǝ aga nja fiya nyi tǝl ja dzǝgwa sha shili.
LUK 19:13 Kadivira ja mai, ji ngga kumo wu pama mafa nyiˈyar, ji nǝ nda pam papathlǝ ji dzǝgwa na anǝ nda, ‘Shafǝli mau ǝni kǝl yi sha shili.’
LUK 19:14 Njir mǝlmǝ nyi wu yiwu nyi mai. Agabangau, kǝ ndǝ sǝwa cama ayukuɗa ji mai a ndu mǝlmǝ ta abǝr, ‘Naˈyu yiwu ndǝ kǝ ja ɗa tǝl ar kǝra ˈya mai.’
LUK 19:15 “Kǝ nji fiya ndǝ kǝ tǝl, ji dzǝgwa sha shili wu ki. Ənggǝra ji shili kǝ ji sǝwa nja nggari nyi mafa nyiˈyar ta, aga ja sǝni nubwa kǝra ndǝ uya ar kǝra sǝra ji nǝ nda.
LUK 19:16 Ndǝ tanggǝrma shili ji na, ‘Thlagǝu, a uyari yau nubwa pam kumo a dar kǝra pam pathlǝu ta gǝ nǝ ɗa ta.’
LUK 19:17 Kǝ thlagǝri ki kǝ na anǝ nyi, ‘Usi mafa tsapǝu ndǝr mǝl thlǝr tsaˈa miya ɗǝfu! Gǝ mǝl thlǝr ngau, tsaˈa miya ɗǝfu ǝnga sǝ kushu kǝra nji nǝ ngau, yu mǝliya ga sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra mǝlmǝ pamǝpamǝ kumou.’
LUK 19:18 Mafa nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi shili ji na, ‘Thlagǝu, a uyari yau nubwa pamǝ tǝfu a dar kǝra pamǝ zǝmǝ ta gǝ nǝ ɗa ta.’
LUK 19:19 Thlagǝr ki nyi shaɗǝwa anǝ ndǝ kau, ‘Gǝ wu sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra mǝlmǝ pamǝpamǝ tǝfu.’
LUK 19:20 “Kǝ vanyi mafa shili ji na, ‘Thlagǝu, kǝ ja pamǝ zǝmǝ ngau. Yi pǝɗiya wu kukuzhal, yi ɗǝwana.
LUK 19:21 Ara yu hivǝr ngau, arya na gǝ ndǝ dzadzau ngau. Kǝja ga fa sǝra kǝra nǝ gau, gu gǝm tsu sǝra gǝ kǝra thlǝka na.’
LUK 19:22 Kǝ ji na anǝ nyi, ‘Nagǝ mafa ɗǝmwaˈyi hangǝkal, yu mǝliya ngǝ numa ǝnga sǝra biya sara wu miya gau! Əngwar gau nayi ndǝra nji kǝra sǝni hangǝkal nyi, ndǝr fa sǝ nji kurthlǝu ǝnga yiwu gǝm ar vi kǝra yi kǝra thlǝka na.
LUK 19:23 Tsaˈa nga nyi, ama mi ngǝ ɗa nagǝ fiya gǝnna ɗa ar vi fǝ gǝnna maya, aga maˈyi shili ya uya akkǝri ar kǝri mai ya?’
LUK 19:24 “Kǝ ji na anǝ nji ta taˈyi ǝkkǝˈyi ja, ‘Dlǝwura mau gǝnna dubu pathlǝu kǝra ara ja kau, ba hya nǝ nyi anǝ ndǝra ǝnga dubu kumou.’
LUK 19:25 Ama kǝ ndǝ shaɗǝwa nyi, ndǝ na, ‘Thlagǝu, pamǝ kumo nga ara ja.’
LUK 19:26 Ji shaɗǝwa, ji na, ‘Yi wu nar hyi, ndǝra aˈyi ǝnga sau nju nda cakǝri nyi. Ndǝra kǝra aˈyi ǝnga sau, alaga sǝ kushu kǝra aˈyi ara ja nju nda dlǝwuri.
LUK 19:27 Njira dawa ɗa kau, nji kǝra gǝra yiwu ya ɗa tǝl ar kǝra nda kau, faˈari nda mau a shili nja tsǝya nda wu mwa ɗa.’ ”
LUK 19:28 Ənggǝra ji nana abangau, kǝ ji dumwa a vu Urshalima.
LUK 19:29 Ənggǝra Yesu ǝnga zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar vu mǝlmǝ Bethfaji ǝnga Bethlani, mǝlmǝ kǝra lǝhǝu wu dzǝr Urshalima, kǝra a dar kǝra mǝ zaitunu. Kǝ Yesu sǝwa zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar mǝthlǝu,
LUK 19:30 Ji na anǝ nda, “Maˈya mau a vu zǝr mǝlmǝ kǝ a ndumwar hyi kau, ǝnggǝra hyi vwau, hyu vuwa thlǝwa zǝr kwara mbamba ar sǝˈyi, kǝra nji gǝra saya dari, hya pǝlna nyi hya hǝr ɗa a shili.
LUK 19:31 Ma nji yiwa hyi, ‘Mi ngǝ ɗa hyu mǝl abanga?’ Kǝl ba hya na, ‘Thlagǝ ngu yiwu ja mǝl thlǝr ǝni.’ ”
LUK 19:32 Njira nji sǝwa, ndǝ maˈyi, kǝ ndǝ thlǝwa kalar sau ǝnggǝra Yesu nar nda ta.
LUK 19:33 Nda vǝr pǝl nyi ja, kǝ thlagǝri kwara nyi na anǝ nda, “Aga mi nga hyu pǝl nya?”
LUK 19:34 Kǝ ndǝ na, “Thlagǝ ngu yiwu ja mǝl thlǝr ǝni.”
LUK 19:35 Kǝ ndǝ hǝri nyi a shila nǝ Yesu. Ənggǝra ndǝ fǝr lǝgutǝr nda a dar kwara nyi, kǝ ndǝ dlǝwari Yesu ndǝ fǝri nyi a dar ya kwara nyi.
LUK 19:36 Ənggǝra ja vǝr ɓau, kǝ nji dzǝgwa sǝya lǝgutǝr nda a gyar lagu.
LUK 19:37 Ənggǝra ji shili lǝhǝu wu dzǝri Urshalima, mǝ tsa ga vi kǝra lagu sa gya ar dza gar nǝ wur Zaitunu, kǝ daɓǝr zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar gangǝu daɓau nda vǝr usa Hyal, nda vǝr fal nyi tsu ǝnga ɗahǝu ǝnga dǝnama arya sǝ dǝdǝgur pamǝpamǝ kǝra ndǝ lari.
LUK 19:38 Nda vǝr na! “Barka a nggyar anǝ tǝl kǝra wu dla wu thlǝmǝr Thlagǝu! Jamǝkur a nggyari a dǝmǝlmau, ǝnga kadakadarkur anǝ Hyal!”
LUK 19:39 Kǝ alenyi njir Farisi kǝra wu pama nda na anǝ nyi, “Malǝmǝ, ga kughi anǝ zǝmbǝlma ngǝˈyar nda nggya zǝmǝu!”
LUK 19:40 Ji shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Ya nar hyi,” “alaga ndǝ bǝgau, tsǝka ˈyar kǝ ǝnga kǝr nda ndu wau.”
LUK 19:41 Ənggǝra ji shili lǝhǝu gagaɗau, ji tsamiya vu Urshalima, kǝ ji tiwi anǝ nyi.
LUK 19:42 Ji na, “Kara nggǝrau, ma ja hyi nda sǝni sǝra wu nǝ hyi nggya jamǝu! Ama kǝ ja a ɗar ɗǝɗǝwa ara hyi.
LUK 19:43 Pǝci a vǝr shili kǝra dawar hyu nda zǝwar hyu masǝmǝ nda dzǝgwa pa ǝnga hyi. Sojar nda ngu nda zǝwar hyi.
LUK 19:44 Ndu nda hǝradlǝna ngau ǝnga nja dlǝna njira a gwa patǝu. Nandǝ wu nda piyari tsǝka zǝmǝ ar kǝra kuvwa nyi mai. Sǝˈyar kǝ wu nda ɗa ǝnga hyi ara nahyi aˈyi sǝnbiya abǝr Hyal shili aga mbǝɗa hyi mai.”
LUK 19:45 Kǝ Yesu vu ki Hyal ji vuwa kǝdlǝbiya njira vǝr ɗǝl ǝnga ɗǝlna sǝ a vuna patǝu,
LUK 19:46 ji na anǝ nda, “Tsǝtsǝfǝ nga nyi, “ ‘Nju ngga ki ɗa ǝnga vir kǝdi Hyal,’ ama kǝja hya shabiyari ji ɗa vir ɗǝwa njir ɗalagu.”
LUK 19:47 Parangǝ ja vǝr highiɓau wu ki Hyal. Ama pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar, ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar, ǝnga nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmǝ ndu gal lagu kǝra nda daɓaga tsǝya nyi ari.
LUK 19:48 Ama nandǝ uya lagu kǝra nda sǝni tsǝya nyi mai, ara ndǝr nyi a uyari vi wu ɗǝfuwa nji, ǝnga nandǝ wu yiwu ndǝr zǝmǝ a tǝɗau a gyiwu ˈyi mai.
LUK 20:1 Vanyi pǝci Yesu gwu ki Hyal ja vǝr highiɓau, ja vǝr tǝtǝlna ndǝshigu mǝsahǝu anǝ nji, kǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar, malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar ǝnga njira nggurǝm shili ara ja. Ndǝ sa yiwa nyi,
LUK 20:2 “Ənga dǝnama wa nga gu mǝl sǝˈyar ka? Wa ngǝ nǝ ngǝ dǝnama nǝ mǝl sǝˈyar ka?”
LUK 20:3 Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Nayi ma yu yiwari hyi. Nar ɗa mau,
LUK 20:4 dǝnama kǝra Yahwana mǝl baɓǝtizǝma ǝni, Hyal ngǝ nǝ nyi ǝndǝga ndau?”
LUK 20:5 Kǝ ndǝ ndǝr wu pama nda, ndǝ na, “Ma mǝn na, ‘Sara ara Hyal nga nyi dla,’ ju nda na, ‘Mi ngǝ ɗa nahyi hǝnggǝri ǝnga ja mai ya?’
LUK 20:6 Ma tsu mǝn na, ‘Sara ara nji,’ gangǝkura nji kǝ ndu nda vavaka mǝn ǝnga tsǝka, arya patǝkura nda a hǝnggǝri abǝr Yahwana nabi nga ja.”
LUK 20:7 Agabangǝ kǝ ndǝ na anǝ nyi, “Naˈya sǝni vi kǝra dǝnama nyi dla sara ri mai.”
LUK 20:8 Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nda, “Nayi ma, nayi wu na anǝ hyi, tara ǝnga dǝnama wa nga yu mǝl sǝˈyar kǝ mai.”
LUK 20:9 Kǝ Yesu nar nyi najaka karapǝ anǝ nji, ji na, “Nggara mau vanyi karapau, Vanyi thlagǝr fa aˈyi kǝra thlǝkana fa wur inabi. Ji zǝwari fa kǝ wu masǝmǝ, ǝnga ji labiya kaˈu nǝ ɓǝci ˈyimir wur inabi. Kǝ ji liya dzaˈwu nǝ ɓǝla fa. Kǝ ji tǝtǝkǝna fa anǝ njir zǝwa, ba ji maˈyi a nda gǝ ndau.
LUK 20:10 Ənggǝra pǝcir fwahǝu ɗa, kǝ ji sǝwa mafa nyi a nda nǝ njira hǝ fa, aga ja dlǝwuri nyi akkǝri nyi nǝ inabi sara wu fa wur inabi nyi. Ama kǝ njira hǝri fa kǝ dǝgǝna mafa kau, ka dzǝgwa sǝwa nyi ǝnga tsi kurthlǝu.
LUK 20:11 Kǝ ji ɓǝra sǝwa vanyi mafa nyi, ama kǝ ndǝ ɓǝra dǝgǝna nyi ka hǝna sǝli nyi, ndǝ dzǝgwa shabiya nyi ǝnga tsi kurthlǝu.
LUK 20:12 Kǝ ji ɓǝra sǝwa mafa nǝ makǝrkura nyi, kǝ ndǝ uya nyi ǝnga mbǝlgǝu, ndǝ vakana nyi a biya.
LUK 20:13 “Kabangǝkau, ndǝ kǝ thlagǝri fa inabi kǝ na, ‘Mi nga ya mǝla? Yu sǝwa zǝr ɗa kǝ zǝmǝ kǝ yu yiwu kau, tara ba nda gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli.’
LUK 20:14 “Ama ǝnggǝra njir hǝ fa kǝ lari nyi, kǝ ndǝ na wu pama nda, ǝnghǝng! ‘Kǝja ndǝr faˈa ki nyi. Mǝna tsǝya nyi, ba sǝr faˈa ki nyi kǝ patǝ a ɗa nǝr mǝn.’
LUK 20:15 Kǝ ndǝ tsǝya nyi ka vakana nyi a biyar ya kǝr ki. “Kabangǝkau, mi nga hyu nggani thlagǝri fa kǝ wu nda mǝl ǝnga njir hǝ fa ka?
LUK 20:16 Ju nda shili ja sa dlǝna patǝr njir hǝ fa kau, ba ja dzǝgwa nǝ nyi fa anǝ nji pamǝ tsu.” Ənggǝra nji kǝ nggari abangau kǝ ndǝ na, “Hyal ja tsana!”
LUK 20:17 Ama kǝ Yesu tsamǝ nda kǝ ji yiwa, “Mi ngǝ sǝ kǝ cabiya wu ndǝr Hyal kǝra tsǝtsǝfa? “ ‘Tsǝka kǝra njir hǝr diɗana ca ngǝ ɗa tsǝka ɓǝlkǝr.’
LUK 20:18 Kalar ndǝra tǝɗau a gyar tsǝka kau, ju ɓǝɓǝl, ama ndǝra tsǝka kǝ tǝɗǝ a gyar ja, ju ǝya dzǝ huhutǝu.”
LUK 20:19 Ənggau ngǝ malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar ǝnga pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ndu yiwu nda mbari Yesu, arya ndǝ sǝnbiya abǝr karapǝ kǝ ji lǝ kǝ ar kǝra nda nga nyi, ama kǝ hivǝr mbar nda ara dlamir nji.
LUK 20:20 Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa gal lagu, ndǝ kina alenyi nji aga nda ɗa ǝnggǝr nji tsapǝu, nji jiri. Ndǝ dzǝgwa sǝwa nda a ndǝgya Yesu aga nda ngǝ ya nyi lǝbam ǝnga sǝra ndu yiwa nyi, aga nda uya nda nǝ nyi Yesu anǝ ndǝr pathla kǝra ǝnga dǝnama nǝr ˈyiˈyir Roma.
LUK 20:21 Nji kǝ nji sǝwa kǝ na anǝ Yesu, “Malǝmǝ, ˈyi wu sǝni abǝr ndǝr ngau ǝnga highiɓǝ ngau jiri nga nyi, ˈyi wu sǝni tsu na gu ca pamǝpamǝkur mai, ama gu highiɓǝ sǝra jiri nǝ lagu Hyal anǝ nji patǝu.
LUK 20:22 Wu ɗǝnga ngau, a ɗar tsaˈa ˈya ki budau anǝ tǝl Kayisaru ǝndǝga awau?”
LUK 20:23 Ama Yesu a sǝnbiya tsǝtsǝlkur nda, kǝ ji na anǝ nda,
LUK 20:24 “Canǝ ɗa mau kwaɓa. Bama wa ǝnga thlǝmǝr wa nga ri ka?”
LUK 20:25 Ndǝ shaɗǝwa nyi, “Nǝ Tǝl Kayisaru ngau.” Kǝ ji nar nda, “Ma abangau, hya nǝ nyi anǝ tǝl Kayisaru sǝra nǝ nyi, ba hya nǝ nyi anǝ Hyal sǝra nǝ Hyal.”
LUK 20:26 Ənggau kǝ ndǝ tini mbari nyi ǝnga ndǝr wu mwar nji. Kǝ ndǝ nggya zǝmǝu, ara shaɗǝwa nyi ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ nda.
LUK 20:27 Kǝja alenyi njir Sadusi, njira na abǝr hyaˈari sara vir tau aˈyi mai, ndǝ dla ǝgya Yesu, ndǝ na,
LUK 20:28 “Malǝmǝ, Musa tsǝfǝri ˈya najaka dlaɗau abǝr, ‘Ma ndǝ tau ji piyari mala nyi kǝra gǝra wazha, a kyau zamǝ nyi a hǝri mala kǝ aga ja uya wazha anǝ zamǝ nyi.’
LUK 20:29 Nji sayi mǝliya alenyi nji nanda mǝɗǝfau, nanda patǝ zamǝ nga nda. Kǝ dǝgala nda hǝri mala ba ji tau kǝra yabiya zǝr.
LUK 20:30 Kǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi hǝri mala kau.
LUK 20:31 Nǝ makǝrkura nyi abangau. Kǝ ɗa patǝkura nda mǝɗǝfǝ hǝri mala kau, ama ba ndǝ tǝ patǝ gǝra ya ǝnga mala kau.
LUK 20:32 Wu yukuɗa nyi, mala kǝ ma ba ji tau.
LUK 20:33 Kabangǝkǝ ya, pǝcir hyaˈari sara vir tau, mala wa nga ju nda ɗa? Arya patǝkura nda a hǝri nyi ri nda aga mala.”
LUK 20:34 Yesu na anǝ nda, “Nji kabangǝkǝ kǝl hǝ dzǝ nga ndu hau wu pamǝu,
LUK 20:35 ama njira wu nda ɗa tsaˈa aga hyaˈari sara vir tau nga ndu vu tǝlkur Hyal wu pǝci ta, nandǝ wu hǝ dzǝ mai.
LUK 20:36 Ndu nda ɗa ǝnggǝr waladiˈyar, nandǝ wu ɓǝra tǝ mai. Ndu nda ɗa wazha Hyal ara a hyaˈari nda sara vir tau.
LUK 20:37 Musa ǝnga kǝrnyi a cabiyari ar babal abǝr njira tau ndu nda hyaˈari ǝnga pi. Wu ndǝr ar kǝra kǝdlǝl kǝra mbari uˈu, ji ndǝr ar kǝra Thlagǝ abǝr naja ngǝ, ‘Hyal nǝ Ibrahimu ǝnga Ishaku ǝnga nǝ Yakubu.’
LUK 20:38 Naja aˈyi Hyal nǝ nji tǝtǝ mai ama nǝ njira ǝnga pi. Anǝ nyi kalar ndau ǝnga pi nga ja.”
LUK 20:39 Kǝ alenyi malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar ndǝ ndǝr ndǝ na, “Malǝmǝ, a nabiyar gǝ kakalǝu!”
LUK 20:40 Ənggau nandǝ ɓǝra uya dǝnama nǝ yiwa nyi vanyi sǝ mai.
LUK 20:41 Yesu yiwa nda ji na, “Abari nga nju sǝni na abǝr Kǝrsiti zǝr Dawuda?
LUK 20:42 Dawuda ǝnga kǝrnyi na wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ Zabura: “ ‘Thlagǝ na anǝ Thlagǝ ɗa, Nggya lagu mazǝma yau,
LUK 20:43 kǝl yi fiya dawa ngau ǝgya kiɗa hiya gau.” ’
LUK 20:44 Dawuda ji na anǝ Kǝrsiti ‘Thlagǝu.’ Ya abari nga ja sǝni na anǝ nyi zǝr nya?”
LUK 20:45 Ənggǝra nji patǝ a vǝr sǝ himi nyi, kǝ ji nar nyi anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar abǝr,
LUK 20:46 “Hya hangǝkal ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar. Ndu yiwu nda ɓau wu pama nji wu kar ha nggunggurǝm ǝnga nja dzǝgwa usa nda ar sugu. Ndu yiwu tsu nja nǝ nda vir nggya tsapǝ wu umbwa daɓǝ dzǝ njir Yahudiya, ǝnga vir nggya nǝ kadakadarkur ar vir mini.
LUK 20:47 Nanda ngǝ njir sǝm kari nǝ mathlǝkǝˈyi tǝsal, nda dzǝgwa ndǝr ǝnga Hyal tugu aga nja lari abǝr aˈyi nda. Jiri, nanda ngu nda lari ɓwaɓwatǝ gagaɗau a ndiya nji patǝu.”
LUK 21:1 Yesu hyaˈanakǝr kǝ ji lari alenyi njir gǝnna a vǝr fǝ gǝnnar nda a gwu cala tsǝm sau a gwu ki Hyal.
LUK 21:2 Kǝ ji lari vanyi malatǝsal kǝra sǝ nyi aˈyi mai ji shili ǝnga kwaɓa nyi mǝthlǝ kǝ ji puwa a gwu cala.
LUK 21:3 Kǝ Yesu na, “Jiri, nga yu na anǝ hyi,” “sǝra mala tǝtǝ dǝnama kǝ fuwa, a ndiya nǝ nji kǝ patǝu.
LUK 21:4 Arya patǝkura nda ndǝ fuwa sara wu gangǝkura nda ǝni, ama naja ǝnga tukur kǝra ja ǝni, kǝ ji fuwa sǝra ju nggya aga nyi patǝu.”
LUK 21:5 Alenyi zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar dzǝguya ndǝr ar kǝra ki Hyal, ǝnga culi tsǝka mǝnahǝu kǝra nji hǝri ǝni, ǝnga sǝr ɓathlǝ umbwa mǝmǝnahǝ kǝra nji nǝ nyi anǝ Hyal. Ama kǝ Yesu na,
LUK 21:6 “Ma aga sǝˈyar kǝ hyu tsamǝ kau, pǝci wu shili nahyi wu nda thlǝwa tsǝka zǝmǝ ar kǝra kuvwa nyi mai, kalar zǝma nyi nju nda vakana a gyiwu ˈyi.”
LUK 21:7 Ndǝ yiwa nyi, “Malǝmǝ,” nar ˈya, “ǝnuwa ngǝ pǝci kǝra sǝˈyar kǝ wu nda ɗar kǝra, ǝnga mi ngu nda ɗa mǝtsamǝ nǝ shili nga, ǝnga kuɗiyar najaka duniya?”
LUK 21:8 Kǝ ji shaɗǝwa nda, “Hya nggya hya tsamǝ ǝnga hangǝkal nja sara nggutana hyi. Arya nji gangǝu wu nda shili wu thlǝmǝ ɗa, ndu na ǝnga kǝrnda, ‘Nayi ngǝ Kǝrsiti,’ ǝnga, ‘Pǝci a ɗar lǝhǝu.’ Hya sara nu nda mai.
LUK 21:9 Hya sara hivǝr mai, ma hyi nggari ar kǝra papa ǝnga ndǝr ǝngwa ǝngwa ar kǝra papa, hangǝkalǝr hyi ja sara hyaˈari mai. Kǝl ma sǝˈyar kǝ nyabiya dzau, ama tsu kuɗǝr duniya naɗǝu. ”
LUK 21:10 Ji dumwa ǝnga na, “ˈYiˈyi wu dlǝɗǝ ˈyiˈyi, ǝnga tǝlkur wu nda par tǝlkur.
LUK 21:11 Wuɓau ǝnga kǝnggǝɗǝr ˈyiˈyi wu nda ɗarkǝr ar vi pamǝpamǝ gangǝu, ǝnga shilǝgǝˈyar pamǝpamǝ ar kalar vi pamǝpamǝu. Nju nda lari sǝr lǝ hivǝr ǝnga sǝr dǝdǝgurˈyar sara dǝmǝlmau.
LUK 21:12 “Ama kadivira sǝˈyar kǝ ɗa, nju nda mbari hyi nja nǝ hyi ɓwaɓwatǝu. Nju hǝri hyi a ndu umbwa daɓǝ dzǝ njir Yahudiya aga nja thlana hyi numa, nja ɓǝra fuwa hyu fursǝna. Nju hǝri hyi a dumwar tǝlˈyar ǝnga nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmǝ arya thlǝmǝ ɗa aga nda ɓǝra thlana hyi numa.
LUK 21:13 Sǝˈyar kǝ ngu nda nǝ hyi lagu nǝ tǝtǝlna ndǝshigu mǝsahǝu ar kǝra yau.
LUK 21:14 Agabangǝ hya fǝr kǝr ǝni tsu kaɗǝu abǝr nahyi wu nda ɓwakǝr ǝnggǝra hyu nda hǝbiya kǝrhyi mai.
LUK 21:15 Arya yu nda nǝ hyi sǝr na ǝnga sǝnbiya aga alaga zǝma dawar hyi a sǝni nda shabiya ndǝr hyi ǝnga kǝpalna sǝra hyu na mai.
LUK 21:16 Əkkǝˈyi dǝr hyi, ǝnga zamǝri hyi, ǝnga nji gǝ hyi, ǝnga bazhir hiˈyar wu nda lǝri hyi anǝ nji, ǝnga nju nda tsǝya alenyi nju pama hyi.
LUK 21:17 Patǝkura nju nda yiwu shishir dza hyi mai arya thlǝmǝ ɗa.
LUK 21:18 Ama shishir kǝra hyi zǝmǝ wu nda sa mai.
LUK 21:19 Ma hyu sǝni cinapi hyu uya mbǝɗau.
LUK 21:20 “Ma hyi lari sojaˈyar zǝwar Urshalima, hya sǝni abǝr pǝcir kuɗǝ nyi a ɗar lǝhǝu.
LUK 21:21 Kǝ njira wu ˈyiˈyir Yahudi, nda hwi a du mau. Njira wu hu ɗa mǝlmǝ nda biya, njira a biyar ya mǝlmǝ nda sara vu hu ɗa mǝlmǝ mai.
LUK 21:22 Arya pǝci kǝ pǝcir pathla ngau, a ɗar tsaˈa nja nyabiya sǝra tsǝtsǝfau wu ndǝr Hyal.
LUK 21:23 Sǝr tǝhuɗǝ anǝ mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra ǝnga huɗǝu ǝnga kǝra a vǝr lǝ uˈwa ar pǝci ta! Ara ɓwaɓwatǝ ɗǝmwaˈyi wu nda vu ˈyiˈyi kau, ǝtsu huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal wu nda gya ar kǝra nji kau.
LUK 21:24 Nju nda tsǝya alenyi nja vǝr pa, nju nda mbari alenyi nji nja maˈyi ǝnga nda a ndu mafakur a ndu alenyi ˈyiˈyi. Njira aˈyi njir Yahudiya mai ndu nda sǝmku Urshalima, kǝl pǝcir nda nyabiya dzau.”
LUK 21:25 “Nji wu nda lari sǝ pamǝpamǝ nǝ lǝ hivǝr ar pǝci, ǝnga hya, ǝnga shashilga. Wu duniya tsu nju nda gwu ɓwaɓwatǝ ǝnga hivǝr ara par ˈyimi ar tsadau.
LUK 21:26 Nju nda shavǝr ara hivǝr ǝnggǝra nda vǝr ɗǝnga ar kǝra sǝra a vǝr shili wu duniya, arya pǝci, hya ǝnga shashilgaˈyar nju nda kǝnggǝɗǝr nda.
LUK 21:27 Wu pǝci ta nju lari Zǝr Ndau ju shili wu dlama ǝnga dǝnama ǝnga kadakadarkur.
LUK 21:28 Ma sǝˈyar kǝ a dzǝguyar ɗa, hya hyaˈari hya taˈyau ǝnga jirkur hyi ara pǝcir mbǝɗǝr hyi a ɗar lǝhǝu.”
LUK 21:29 Kǝ ji nar nda najaka karapau, “Tsamiya mau wur ɓǝla ǝnga alenyi wuˈyar.
LUK 21:30 Ma ndǝ dzǝguya thlǝ hyali, nahyi ǝnga kǝrhyi, hya sǝni abǝr biyargwa a shiliri.
LUK 21:31 Abangǝ tsu, ma hya lar sǝˈyar kǝ a ɗari, hya nggya ǝnga sǝni abǝr tǝlkur Hyal a ɗar lǝhǝu.”
LUK 21:32 “Yu nar hyi jirkura nyi, najaka zamanǝu, aˈyi wu tǝrabiya mai, kǝl sǝˈyar kǝ patǝ nyabiya dzau.
LUK 21:33 Dǝmǝlmau ǝnga gyiwu ˈyi wu nda tǝrabiya, ama ndǝr ɗa nǝ nyi wu tǝɗau a gyiwu ˈyi mai.”
LUK 21:34 “Hya hangǝkal ǝnga kǝrhyi. Hya sara piyari sǝm ǝnga sa sǝ sasa, ǝnga ɓwaɓwatǝ nǝ nggya biya duniya ja sara hǝna hangǝkalǝr hyi mai. A sara pǝci kǝ a shili ar kǝra hyi ǝnga kǝra sǝnkur hyi
LUK 21:35 ǝnggǝr lǝbam. Ara wu nda shili ar kǝra nji patǝ kǝra wu duniya pǝci ta.
LUK 21:36 Hya nggya ǝnga fǝr kǝr, hya ndǝr ǝnga Hyal parangǝ aga hya uya dǝnama nǝ tǝrabiya wu sǝˈyar kǝ nda ɗa kǝ aga ja daɓaga ɗa hya taˈyau wu mwar Zǝr Ndau.”
LUK 21:37 Kalar pǝci, Yesu a vǝr dumwa ǝnga highiɓau wu ki Hyal, ama ma wagǝu ɗa ba ja maˈyi a ndar vi kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Gar mǝ Zaitunu ba ja pida a dǝna.
LUK 21:38 Kaɗǝ kalar mudlǝ nji patǝ tsu ndu shili ǝgya ja nda sa sǝ himi nyi wu ki Hyal.
LUK 22:1 Pǝcir mǝl lardur nǝr njir Yahudiya ǝnga macikǝl kǝra gǝra thlǝlam, kǝra nja ngga ǝnga lardur vǝlna a ɗar lǝhǝu,
LUK 22:2 kabangǝkǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar nda vǝr gal lagu ǝnga dabar kǝra nda daɓaga tsǝya Yesu, ama hivǝr a vǝr tǝ nda ara nji.
LUK 22:3 Kǝ Shatan gwu ɗǝfuwa Yahuda, kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Isikarayoti pathlǝu wu pama zǝmbǝlma nyi kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu.
LUK 22:4 Kǝ Yahuda maˈyi a ndǝgya pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga dǝgal njir ɓǝla ki Hyal aga ja nda nar nda ǝnggǝra ju sǝni pǝlna nyi pǝzhi anǝ Yesu.
LUK 22:5 Kǝ ɗa sǝr caguli anǝ nda, ndǝ hǝnggǝri ndu nǝ nyi gǝnna.
LUK 22:6 Yahuda tsu a hǝnggǝri ja ǝnga sǝra ndǝ na, ja vǝr gal lagu mǝnahǝu kǝra ja sǝni pǝlna nyi pǝzhi anǝ Yesu kǝra ja gǝra sǝni.
LUK 22:7 Kǝ pǝcir lardur nǝr macikǝl kǝra gǝra thlǝlam shili, kǝra ɗa ca ngǝ pǝcir thla gamǝ nǝr lardur nǝr vǝlna.
LUK 22:8 Yesu sǝwa Biturusu ǝnga Yahwana, ja vǝr na, “Maˈyi mau hya nda mǝliya mǝn vir sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝ vǝlna aga mǝna sǝm.”
LUK 22:9 Kǝ ndǝ yiwa nyi ndǝ na, “Əmani nga gu yiwu ˈya pabǝra?”
LUK 22:10 Ji na anǝ nda, “Ənggǝra hyu vu hu ɗa mǝlmau, ndǝ sal a vǝr hǝ tǝm ǝnga ˈyimi wu thlǝwa hyi. Nu nya mau a ndu ki kǝra ju nda vuwa gwa.
LUK 22:11 Hya nar nyi anǝ thlagǝr ki kau, ‘Malǝmǝr ˈya ngǝ sǝwa ˈya aga ˈya nar ngau, “Əmani ngǝ umbwa dlǝwu mǝthlǝpi kǝra nayi ǝnga zǝmbǝlma ɗaˈyar wu nda sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝr vǝlbiya a gwa?” ’
LUK 22:12 Ju nda canǝ hyi umbwa kǝra a dar kǝra umbwa kǝra dǝgal kǝra nja mǝliya ri. Ənggau hya mǝliya kalar sau, aga sǝm sǝr sǝm.”
LUK 22:13 Kǝ ndǝ maˈyi ndǝ nda thlǝwa kalar sau ǝnggǝra Yesu nar nda ta, kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa mǝliya vir sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝr lardur nǝ vǝlna.
LUK 22:14 Ənggǝra pǝci ɗa, kǝ Yesu ǝnga cama sǝsǝ nyiˈyar nggya aga nda sǝm sǝr sǝm.
LUK 22:15 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “A yiwur yau gagaɗau aga ya sǝm lardur nǝr vǝlbiya kǝ ǝnga hyi kadivira ya dzǝgwa lar ɓwaɓwatǝu!
LUK 22:16 Arya yu nar hyi, nayi tsu ɓǝra sǝm sǝ kǝ ǝnga hyi mai kǝl ma jirkura nyi nyabiya dzǝ wu tǝlkur Hyal.”
LUK 22:17 Kǝ ji hǝri kyakiwa, kǝ ji usari Hyal ji na, “Hǝra mau hya tǝkǝya wu pama hyi.
LUK 22:18 Ya vǝr na anǝ hyi abǝr, tsu yu ɓǝra sa ˈyimir yayar wur inabi mai, kǝl ma tǝlkur Hyal shili.”
LUK 22:19 Abangau, kǝ ji hǝri macikǝl, kǝ ji lǝr usaku anǝ Hyal, ba ji ɓǝɓǝlǝwa, kǝ ji nǝ nyi anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar, ju na, “Dlǝwura mau hya sǝm, naja kǝ kumǝr dza yi ngau, hya mǝl abangau aga ɗǝngari ǝnga yau.”
LUK 22:20 Abangǝ tsu, ayukuɗa sǝr sǝm nǝ wagǝu, kǝ ji hǝri kyakiwa ta, ji na, “Kyakiwa kǝ ca ngǝ alkawal mbamba mafǝliyangǝ kǝra Hyal mǝliya ǝnga mashi ɗa kǝra nju nda pǝna arya hyi.
LUK 22:21 Ama kǝja tsa ndǝra wu nda thlǝna hiyau wu cala ǝnga yau!
LUK 22:22 Zǝr Ndau wu nda tau ǝnggǝra Hyal nana, ama sǝr tǝhuɗǝ anǝ ndǝ kǝ pǝlna nyi pǝzhi kau!”
LUK 22:23 Kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar dzǝguya yiwa wu pama nda, tara wa ngu nda mǝl sǝ kau.
LUK 22:24 Abangau kǝ kǝpal hyaˈari wu pama zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar abǝr tara wa ngu dǝgal wu pama nda.
LUK 22:25 Yesu na anǝ nda, “Tǝlˈyar nǝr duniya vǝr cina njira ǝgya kiɗa nda, ǝnga tsu njira wu sǝm dǝgalkur wu na abǝr nanda ngǝ, ‘Njir dlǝwa nji.’
LUK 22:26 Ama ja sara ɗa abangau wu pama hyi mai. Ndǝra dǝgal wu pama hyi ja ɗa ǝnggǝr ndǝra ndiya ǝnga kushu, ndǝr sǝm tǝlkur tsu ja ɗa ǝnggǝr ndǝr mǝl thlǝr.
LUK 22:27 Wa nga ndiya ǝnga dǝgala, ndǝra nggya vǝr sǝm sǝr sǝm ǝndǝga ndǝra hǝri sǝr sǝm a shili? Aˈyi ndǝra vǝr sǝm wa? Ama nayau wu pama hyi ǝnggǝr ndǝr mǝl thlǝr anǝ hyi.
LUK 22:28 “Nahyi ngǝ njira nggya ǝnga yau wu patǝr ɓwaɓwatǝ kǝra yi lari.
LUK 22:29 Ənggǝra dǝɗa caɗǝbiya ɗa aga ya sǝm tǝlkur, abangǝ nga ya vǝr nǝ hyi tsu,
LUK 22:30 abangǝ nga hyu nda sǝm, hya sa ǝnga yu tǝlkur ɗa. Ətsu hyu nda nggya ar vir sǝm tǝlkur, hya dzǝgwa sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra culi kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ nǝ Izirayila.
LUK 22:31 “Simanu, Simanu, Shatan a dlǝwuri ja dǝnama aga ja dzǝbiya hyi patǝu, ja tǝkǝbiya hyi ǝnga yau ǝnggǝra ndǝr zǝwa wu tǝkǝ uhi ǝnga cacangǝ.
LUK 22:32 Ama a kǝdi ri yi Hyal anǝ ngau, Simanu, a sara mbǝrsa ngau a tǝwa mai. Ayukuɗa ma ga sha ara shili ǝgya yau, ga sa cakǝri nyi dǝnama anǝ zamǝ ngǝˈyar.”
LUK 22:33 Simanu shaɗǝwa, ji na, “Thlagǝu, a pabǝri yi kǝrɗa aga ya maˈyi a vu fursǝna nga gau, alaga tǝ ma.”
LUK 22:34 Yesu shaɗǝwa, “Biturusu, yu nar ngau, kadivira vǝgǝm nda wau ǝshina ǝvuˈyi, gu nda na, na ga sǝni ɗa mai ar kǝr ar kǝr makǝru!”
LUK 22:35 Kǝ Yesu yiwa nda, “Ənggǝra yi sǝwa hyi gǝra pǝrki, gǝra mbala ǝnga ɓiɓi, a tini ri hyi sǝ ya?” Əngwar nda, “Awau.”
LUK 22:36 Kǝ ji dzǝgwa na anǝ nda, “Ama kabangǝkau, ma gǝ ǝnga pǝrki, ga hǝri, ǝnga mbǝl ɓǝ tsu, ma tsu katsakǝr aˈyi ara ngǝ mai, ɗǝlna lǝgutǝ ha ngau ga ɗǝlbiya zǝmǝ ǝni.
LUK 22:37 Yu nar hyi abǝr sǝ kǝ tsǝtsǝfǝ kǝ abǝr, ‘Nji jigabiya nyi wu pama njir bikau,’ ya nar hyi a ɗar kakalǝ sǝˈyar kǝ nda nyabiya dzǝ ar kǝra yau. Jiri, patǝr sǝra tsǝtsǝfau ar kǝra yau a vǝr nyabiya dzǝ samǝu.”
LUK 22:38 Zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar na, “Thlagǝu, tsamiya, kǝ ja katsakǝr mǝthlǝu.” Yesu na, “Tsaˈa abangau.”
LUK 22:39 Yesu piyari vi ta ji maˈyi a ndu mǝ zaitunu ǝnggǝra ji tsǝliya, kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar nu nyi.
LUK 22:40 Ənggǝra ndǝ thlǝwa vi ta, kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Hya kǝdi Hyal hya sara tǝɗau a gu dzau.”
LUK 22:41 Kǝ ji ɓana dzǝ tsalǝu sara wu dzǝri nda, ji ɓǝliya undi ju kǝdi Hyal,
LUK 22:42 “Tada, ma gu yiwu, hǝna ɗa ɓwaɓwatǝ kau, ama aˈyi sǝra yu yiwu mai, ama sǝra gu yiwu bǝgǝ ja ɗa.”
LUK 22:43 Kǝ waladi sara dǝmǝlmau shida ǝgya ja, ja vǝr fǝ ɗǝfu anǝ nyi.
LUK 22:44 Ənggǝra Yesu wu ɓwaɓwatǝ gagaɗau, kǝ ji dumwa ǝnga kǝdi Hyal ǝnga jirkur, ka dzǝgwa ɗa vitǝku kǝra a vǝr biya sara wu dza ja ǝnggǝr mashi nga vǝr tǝɗau a gyiwu ˈyi.
LUK 22:45 Yesu hyaˈari sara a vǝr kǝdi Hyal, ji sha a ndǝra zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar, ba ji thlǝwa nda wu ghanyi, ara hǝhǝɗakura nda ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzau.
LUK 22:46 Ji yiwa nda, “Mi ngǝ ɗa hyu ghanya? Hyara mau, hya kǝdi Hyal, hya sara tǝɗau a gu dzau.”
LUK 22:47 Tsu ja vǝr ndǝr kǝ dlamir nji shili, Yahuda, pathlǝu wu pama kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu, naja ngǝ dumwa anǝ nda. Ji shili ǝgya Yesu aga ja bǝrpǝ nyi,
LUK 22:48 ama kǝ Yesu yiwa nyi, “Yahuda, ǝnga bǝrpǝ dzǝ nga ga pǝl pǝzhi anǝ Zǝr Ndǝ ya?”
LUK 22:49 Ənggǝra njir nu Yesu lari sǝkǝ a vǝr yiwu ja ɗa kau, kǝ ndǝ na, “Thlagǝu, ˈya mǝl thlǝr ǝnga katsakǝr ˈya ya?”
LUK 22:50 Pathlǝ wu pama zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar thlana himi nǝ mazǝma nǝ mafa nǝ pubu kǝra ndiya ǝnga dǝgal ǝnga katsakǝr.
LUK 22:51 Ama kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa, “Tsaˈa abangau!” Kǝ ji tsǝkwari himiya ndǝ kǝ ba ji mǝliya nyi jamǝu.
LUK 22:52 Yesu ndǝr anǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar, ǝnga dǝgal nǝ ɓǝla ki Hyal ǝnga nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmau, njira dla aga mba nyi. Ji na, “Nayi ngǝ ndǝr tǝɗǝmwa anǝ njir gwaɗǝvi ya, ǝnga hyi sǝbiya katsakǝr ǝnga zǝwa aga hya sa mba ɗa ya?
LUK 22:53 Parangǝu ya vǝr nggya ǝkkǝˈyi hyu Ki Hyal ya vǝr highiɓau, ama nahyi sayi mbar ɗa mai. Sǝˈyar kǝ ɗa patǝ aga sǝra nabiˈyar tsǝfǝri a nyabiya dzau.”
LUK 22:54 Ndǝ mbari Yesu ndǝ maˈyi ǝnga ja a vu ki pubu kǝra ndiya ǝnga dǝgalǝu. Biturusu nu nyi ama naɗǝ wu yukuɗǝ nyi.
LUK 22:55 Alenyi nji mbǝbiya uˈu ar hada vir thla sau, nda vǝr ɗaha uˈu, kǝ Biturusu shili ji sa nggya wu pama nda.
LUK 22:56 Kǝ mafa zǝr kwa lari nyi a vǝr nggya wu pama nda a miya uˈu. Kǝ ji tsamǝ du liya ja, kǝ ji na, “Ndǝ kǝ tsu ǝnga Yesu nga ja.”
LUK 22:57 Ama kǝ ji kǝpalna. Əngwar ja, “Mala, nayi wu sǝni nyi mai.”
LUK 22:58 Ɓǝliya sar kushu kǝ vanyi ndǝ lari nyi ji na, “Na ngǝ ma pathlǝu wu pama nda.” Kǝ Biturusu shaɗǝwa, ji na, “Ndau, nayi ǝkkǝˈyi ja mai.”
LUK 22:59 Ayukuɗa ǝnggǝr saka pathlǝu kǝ vanyi ndǝ hyaˈana ɗahǝ ji na, “Gǝra kǝpal a gwa ndǝ kǝ ma nanda ngau, arya naja ndǝr Galili.”
LUK 22:60 Biturusu shaɗǝwa nyi, “Ndau, nayi wu sǝni sǝra gu ndǝr ar kǝri kǝ mai!” Ənggǝra ja tsu a vǝr ndǝr, kǝ vǝgǝm wau.
LUK 22:61 Kǝ Thlagǝ shabiya dzǝ ja vǝr tsamǝ Biturusu gǝra hǝna li. Ənggau kǝ Biturusu ɗǝngari ndǝr kǝra Yesu nar nyi, abǝr, “Divira vǝgǝmǝ a wau, gu kǝpalna sǝn ɗa ar kǝr ar kǝr makǝru.” Kǝ ji hwi a biya, ji biya tiwi ǝnga sǝlǝm gagaɗau.
LUK 22:62 Kǝ ji maˈyi a biya ji biya tiwi gagaɗau.
LUK 22:63 Njira nji fiya aga ɓǝla Yesu ndǝ dzǝgwa nggushi nǝ diɗa nyi ǝnga ndǝ dǝgǝ nyi.
LUK 22:64 Ndǝ mbiya liya ja nda dzǝgwa yiwa nyi, “Nar ˈya, tara wa ngu dǝgǝ ngǝ kau?”
LUK 22:65 Ndǝ ɓǝra nar nyi alenyi ndǝr pamǝpamǝ nǝ diɗa nyi.
LUK 22:66 Ənggǝra vi kuɗau, nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmau, ǝnga pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar ndǝ kaɓau, nji dzǝgwa hǝri Yesu a shili wu mwar nda.
LUK 22:67 Ndǝ na anǝ nyi, “Ma nagǝ ngǝ Kǝrsiti, nar ˈya.” Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, “Ma yi nar hyi, nahyi wu nda hǝnggǝri ɗa mai,
LUK 22:68 ma tsu yi nda yiwari hyi, nahyi wu nda shaɗǝwa ɗa mai.
LUK 22:69 Ama mbari kabangǝkau, Zǝr Ndau wu nda nggya ar tsi mazǝm nǝ Hyal kǝra ǝnga dǝnama.”
LUK 22:70 Patǝu nda ndǝ yiwa nyi, “Abǝr nagǝ ngǝ zǝr Hyal ya?” Ji shaɗǝwa, ji na, “A nabiyar hyi kakalǝu, nayi ngau.”
LUK 22:71 Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa naja, “Sakida mani nga mǝn ɓǝra gala? A nggari mǝn sara wu miya ja ǝnga kǝrnyi.”
LUK 23:1 Patǝkura nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmǝ Yahudiya lǝbiya Yesu a ndǝgya Bilatusu.
LUK 23:2 Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa gǝm nyi nda vǝr na, “Naˈyi thlǝwa ndǝ kǝ ja vǝr yiwu ja sana njir ˈya, ǝnga ja vǝr na anǝ nda nda sara ki budau anǝ Kayisaru mai. Əngwar ja naja ngǝ Kǝrsiti, kǝra tǝl.”
LUK 23:3 Kǝ Bilatusu yiwa nyi, ji na, “Nagǝ ngǝ tǝl nǝ njir Yahudiya ya?” Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Ənggǝra gǝ na kau.”
LUK 23:4 Kǝ Bilatusu nar nyi anǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga dlamir nji abǝr, “Nayi nǝ ɗa, nayi thlǝwa ndǝ kǝ mǝliya sǝ ɗǝmwaˈyi mai.”
LUK 23:5 Ndǝ ciɗǝ nyi ǝnga ndǝr nda vǝr na abǝr, “Ənga highiɓǝ nyi nga ji hyaˈana hangǝkala nju ˈyiˈyir Yahudi. Ji dzǝguya sǝ kǝ wu Galili, kǝ ja tsu a shiliri ja ǝnggau.”
LUK 23:6 Ənggǝra Bilatusu nggari abangau, kǝ ji yiwa nda, ji na, “Naja ndǝr Galili ya?”
LUK 23:7 Ənggǝra ji nggari abǝr Yesu sara wu vi kǝra Hirudusu a vǝr sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝri nga ji dla, kǝ ji sǝwa nyi a ndara Hirudusu, arya wu pǝci ta naja Hirudusu ma wu Urshalima nga ja.
LUK 23:8 Ənggǝra Hirudusu lari Yesu kǝ hu ɗa ja pida, arya a sǝkari ja vǝr gal lagu kǝra ja lari Yesu, ara a nggari ja sǝ ar kǝra Yesu, ju cim Yesu a mǝliya nyi sǝ dǝdǝgur.
LUK 23:9 Hirudusu yiwa nyi yiwa sau pamǝpamǝ gangǝu, ama Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi mai.
LUK 23:10 Kǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga malǝmǝ dlaɗǝˈyar shili a dumwa nda vǝr fa hya ja ǝnga ndǝr ɗǝmwaˈyu.
LUK 23:11 Hirudusu ǝnga soja nyiˈyar ndǝ diɗana Yesu, ndǝ nggǝl nyi, kǝ ndǝ har nyi nggamndǝ dǝgalǝu, ndǝ dzǝgwa ɓǝra shabiya nyi a ndara Bilatusu.
LUK 23:12 Ar pǝci kǝ ngǝ Hirudusu ǝnga Bilatusu dzǝgwa ɗa bazhi, ara ɗǝɗǝmǝu dawa nga nda.
LUK 23:13 Bilatusu nggari pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga nji dǝdǝgal nǝ mǝlmǝ ǝnga nji patǝu,
LUK 23:14 ba ji na anǝ nda, “Hi hǝri ɗa ndǝ kǝ a shili, abǝr ja vǝr hya hangǝkala nji. Kabangǝkǝ a yubiya nyir yau wu dzǝri hyi patǝu, ama nayi thlǝwa sǝ kǝ hyu vazǝ nyi ǝni kǝ mai.
LUK 23:15 Abangǝ tsu ngǝ Hirudusu. Ca ngǝ ɗa ji ɓǝra shabiya nyi a shila nǝ mǝn. A cabiyari sǝ aˈyi ndǝ kǝ mǝliya kǝra ɗa tsaˈa nja tsǝya nyi mai.
LUK 23:16 Agabangǝ yu nda nǝ nyi wuɗa ba ya sǝya nyi.”
LUK 23:17 Kabangǝkau, wu lardur nǝ vǝlbiya kau, a ɗar tsaˈa anǝ Bilatusu, ja sǝya nda ndǝr fursǝna pathlǝ kǝra ndu yiwu.
LUK 23:18 Ama patǝkura nda hyaˈana ɗahǝ aga zǝmǝ ndǝ na, “Maˈya mau, ǝnga ja, hya sǝya ˈya Barabasu!”
LUK 23:19 (Nji mbiya Barabasu wu fursǝna ara hya hangǝkala nji ǝnga tsa ndau.)
LUK 23:20 Bilatusu ɓǝra ndǝr anǝ nda, arya ju yiwu ja sǝya Yesu.
LUK 23:21 Ama kǝ ndǝ nggya kǝl hya ɗahǝu, “Dlakǝya nyi nji! Dlakǝya nyi nji!”
LUK 23:22 Bilatusu ɓǝra ndǝr anǝ nda nǝ makǝrkura nyi, “Ara mi ya? Wa thlǝmǝ sǝ ɗǝmwaˈyi kǝra ndǝ kǝ mǝliya? Nayi nǝ ɗa, nayi thlǝwa nyi ǝnga bikau kǝra ɗa tsaˈa nja tsǝya nyi mai. Yu sǝwa nja nǝ nyi wuɗa, ba nja sǝya nyi.”
LUK 23:23 Ama kǝ ndǝ taˈyi nǝr nda abǝr kǝl nji dlakǝya nyi. Wu yukuɗu ba ndǝ ndiya dǝnama nyi.
LUK 23:24 Kǝ Bilatusu mǝliya ǝnggǝra ndu yiwu.
LUK 23:25 Kǝ ji sǝya nda ndǝ kǝ ndu yiwu kau, ndǝra nji fuwa wu fursǝna ara hya hangǝkala nji ǝnga tsa ndau. Kǝ ji nǝ nda Yesu aga nda mǝl sǝra ndu yiwu ǝnga ja.
LUK 23:26 Ənggǝra sojaˈyar a vǝr maˈyi ǝnga Yesu, Kǝ ndǝ ɓau ǝnga vanyi ndau nja ngga ǝnga Simanu, ndǝr Sayirini, ja vǝr si sara wu miya tagǝu. Ndǝ taˈyina nyi, ndǝ fǝri nyi wu dladlakau ar kǝra ja, ji dzǝgwa nu Yesu ǝni wu yukuɗu.
LUK 23:27 Nji gangǝ gagaɗau a vǝr nu nyi, wu pama nda alenyi mathlǝkǝˈyi aˈyi kǝra a vǝr tiwi, nda vǝr wau ar kǝra ja.
LUK 23:28 Kǝ Yesu shabiya dzǝ a nda kǝra nda, ji na, “Mathlǝkǝˈyi nǝ Urshalima! A sara hya tiwi ar kǝra yi mai, ama hya tiwi ar kǝra kǝrhyi ǝnga wazhar hyi.
LUK 23:29 Arya pǝci a vǝr shili kǝra nju sa na, ‘Sǝr caguli ngau anǝ mathlǝkǝˈyi ciri, njira gǝra vǝr ya, ǝnga njira gǝra sayi mbiya wazha Kǝrnda wu yi.’
LUK 23:30 A sa ɗa wu pǝci kau, “ ‘Nji wu nda na anǝ mau, “Dla mau a gyar kǝra ˈya!” Ənga anǝ garˈyar, “Mbuya ˈya!” ’
LUK 23:31 “Ma nji mǝl abangau anǝ wu nyanyaɓǝu, abari nga nyi wu nda ɗa anǝ wu uˈula?”
LUK 23:32 Nji ɗǝmwaˈyi mǝthlǝ nji lǝbiya nda tsu aga nja tsǝya nda ǝnga Yesu.
LUK 23:33 Ənggǝra ndǝ shili ar vi kǝra nja ngga ǝnga “papangǝkǝr,” kǝ nji dlakǝya nyi a ndǝna, ǝnga nji ɗǝmwaˈyi mǝthlǝ ta, pathlǝu lagu mazǝma ja ǝnga pathlǝu lagu matsala ja.
LUK 23:34 Kǝ Yesu na, “Tada, tǝfǝbiya nda, arya nanda sǝni sǝra nda vǝr mǝl mai.” Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa tǝtǝkǝna kar ha nyi wu lagur tǝɗǝ shiˈwu.
LUK 23:35 Nji gangǝu taˈyi nda vǝr tsamǝ ǝnggǝra nji dǝdǝgal a vǝr diɗa nyi, nda vǝr na, “Ji mbǝɗana alenyi nji, kabangǝkǝ ja mbǝɗana kǝrnyi, ma naja ngǝ Kǝrsiti kǝra Hyal caɗǝbiya.”
LUK 23:36 Sojaˈyar tsu ndǝ diɗana nyi lagur nǝ nyi ˈyimir wur inabi kǝra ɗar mwamwalu.
LUK 23:37 Nda vǝr na anǝ nyi, “Ma nagǝ ngǝ tǝl nǝ Yahudiya, ga mbǝɗana kǝrngau!”
LUK 23:38 Adabanga ja ndǝ tsǝfǝri vanyi tsǝfǝ kǝra na, “NDƏ KƏ NGƏ TƏL NƏ NJIR YAHUDIYA.”
LUK 23:39 Pathlǝ wu pama nji ɗǝmwaˈyi kǝra nji dlakǝya ǝnga ja na ndǝr didiɗi anǝ nyi, “Aˈyi nagǝ ngǝ Kǝrsiti ndangǝ wa? Mbǝɗana kǝrngau ǝnga ˈya!”
LUK 23:40 Ama kǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi kughi anǝ kuvwa nyi ji na, “Aˈyi gu hivǝr Hyal wa? Na ngǝ kǝra nji thlana hyi numa zǝmǝ ǝnga ja.
LUK 23:41 Nama nǝr ma, tsaˈa ngǝ sǝra nja vǝr mǝl anǝ ma ara sǝra mǝ mǝliya. Ama ndǝ kǝ nǝ nyi, mi ngǝ bikǝ nya?”
LUK 23:42 Kǝ ji na, “Yesu, ga ɗǝngari ɗa ma gǝ vu tǝlkur ngau!”
LUK 23:43 Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Ya nar ngau jirkura nyi, ǝshina gu nda nggya ǝnga yau a du zarna.”
LUK 23:44 Ma pǝci taˈyikǝr, kǝ kuthlǝu haɗiya patǝkura ˈyiˈyi, baˈa ndu saka makǝr nǝ wagǝu,
LUK 23:45 ara ǝnggǝra pǝci nggǝl ara mbǝl. Kadǝmbul kǝra a gwu ki Hyal tǝwa kǝr pamǝpamǝ mǝthlǝu.
LUK 23:46 Yesu hyaˈana ɗahǝu ǝnga dǝnama ji na, “Tada, a vu pǝla gǝ nga yi fiya piya yau.” Ənggǝra ji nana abangau, ba ji sǝna pi nǝ tau.
LUK 23:47 Ənggǝra soja dǝgal kǝra a ndǝna wu pǝci kǝ lari sǝ kǝ ɗa kau, kǝ ji fal Hyal ja vǝr na, “Pakatǝu, ndǝ kǝ ndǝ gǝra bikǝ ngau.”
LUK 23:48 Ənggǝra njira daɓau aga tsamǝ sǝ tsatsamǝ, lari sǝ kǝ ɗarkǝr kau, kǝ ndǝ sha a ndu ki nda vǝr thlǝ nggǝrau ara huɗǝ ndzǝndzau.
LUK 23:49 Patǝkura njira sǝni Yesu, ǝnga mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra nu nyi sara wu ˈyiˈyi Galili, ndǝ taˈyi tsalǝu nda vǝr tsamǝ nyi.
LUK 23:50 Kabangǝkau, vanyi ndau aˈyi kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Yusufu, naja pathlǝu wu pama nji dǝdǝgal nǝ njir Yahudiya, naja ndǝ mǝnahǝu ǝnga ndǝ jiri,
LUK 23:51 naja tsu aˈyi hǝnggǝri ǝnga sǝra nji mbiya ǝnga sǝra nji mǝl mai. Ji shili sara wu mǝlmǝ Arimatiya wu ˈyiˈyir Yahudiya. Naja tsu ja vǝr sǝkǝ shilir tǝlkur Hyal.
LUK 23:52 Kǝ ji maˈyi a ndara Bilatusu aga ja nda kǝdi nja nǝ nyi dza Yesu.
LUK 23:53 Kǝ ji hǝya dza ja nyi sara dar wu, ji pǝɗiya wu paˈwa, ji dzǝgwa fuwa nyi a gu hu kǝra nji labiya a vu mau, hu kǝ nji sayi haɗǝna ndau a gwa mai.
LUK 23:54 Pǝcir fǝ sau wu lagu ngau, a hyiri kushu nja vu pǝcir Ɓǝlsar.
LUK 23:55 Mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra nu Yesu sara wu Galili maˈyi ǝnga Yusufu aga nda lari hu kau, ǝnga ǝnggǝra nju nda fǝ dza Yesu.
LUK 23:56 Ndǝ dzǝgwa sha a ndu ki, ndǝ nda uya sǝ kisǝu ǝnga mal ɓǝsau. Kǝ ndǝ sǝbiya hǝɗa pǝcir Ɓǝlsar, ǝnggǝra dlaɗǝ nǝ lagu Musa nar nda.
LUK 24:1 Umudlǝ kaɗǝu pǝci tanggǝrma nǝ sugu mathlǝkǝˈyi ya nyi hyaˈari ndǝ hǝri sǝ kisǝu kǝra ndǝ mǝliya, ndǝ maˈyi ǝni a ndar hu.
LUK 24:2 Kǝ ndǝ thlǝwa a jahǝnari nji tsǝka kǝra a miya huwa nyi.
LUK 24:3 Ndǝ gu hu kau, ama nandǝ lari dza Thlagǝ Yesu mai.
LUK 24:4 Ma tsu nda vǝr ɗǝnga sǝkǝ ɗa kau, kukuthlǝ kǝ ja nji mǝthlǝ tataˈyu lǝhǝu wu dzǝri nda, wu kari pǝr tǝ pwahǝu a vǝr mbǝl.
LUK 24:5 Nyinyau ǝnga hivǝr, kǝ mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝ uzhau ǝnga kǝra nda a gyiwu ˈyi. Kǝ nja nyi na anǝ nda, “Ara mi nga hya gal ndǝra ǝnga pi wu pama nji tǝta?
LUK 24:6 Aˈyi ja ngǝ mai, a hyaˈari ja. Hya ɗǝngari sǝra ji na anǝ hyi tsu ja ǝnga hyu Galili.
LUK 24:7 Ji na, ‘Pakatǝ nǝ nyi nju nǝ nyi Zǝr Ndau a ndu tsa njir bikau, ndu dlakǝya nyi, pǝcir pida makǝrkura nyi ju hyaˈari ǝnga pi.’ ”
LUK 24:8 Ənggau kǝ ndǝ ɗǝngari sǝra ji na.
LUK 24:9 Ənggǝra ndǝ sha shili sara ndǝr huwa nyi, kǝ ndǝ nar nyi anǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar kumo a sǝrtangǝ ta ǝnga alenyi nji sǝˈyar kǝ ɗa kǝ patǝu.
LUK 24:10 Mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra na sǝˈyar kǝ anǝ cama sǝsǝˈyar kau, nanda ngǝ, Maryamu Magǝdaliya ǝnga Yuwana, ǝnga Maryamu miya Yakubu, ǝnga alenyi mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra nda ǝni.
LUK 24:11 Ama nandǝ hǝnggǝri sǝra mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝ na mai, ara ma ndu nggani jiri aˈyi wu ndǝr kǝ mai.
LUK 24:12 Ama kǝ Biturusu, hyaˈari maɗu ǝnga hwi a ndar huwa nyi, ji nda uzhau, ji tsambiya hu ɗa huwa nyi, kǝl paˈwa kǝra nji pǝɗiya nyi a gwa ca ngǝ baˈa ar dza huwa nyi. Kǝ ji sha a ndu ki ja vǝr ɗǝnga sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝ ɗa kau.
LUK 24:13 Pǝci ta tsu njir nu Yesu aˈyi mǝthlǝ kǝra a vǝr maˈyi a ndu mǝlmǝ kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Imawusu, kǝra naɗǝkura nyi wu ɗa miyal mǝɗǝfǝ sara wu Urshalima.
LUK 24:14 Nda vǝr ndǝr wu pama nda ar kǝra sǝˈyar kǝ ɗarkǝr kau.
LUK 24:15 Ənggǝra nda vǝr ndǝr wu pamǝ nda nda vǝr thla sǝmana, kǝ Yesu ǝnga kǝrnyi lǝhǝn nda, ja vǝr ɓǝ ǝnga nda,
LUK 24:16 a lari nyir nda, ama nandǝ tsamǝ ri nyi mai.
LUK 24:17 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Wa thlǝmǝ najaka sǝmana hya vǝr thla wu pama hya, hya vǝr ɓa?” Kǝ ndǝ taˈyi zǝmǝu, ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzau.
LUK 24:18 Pathlǝ wu pama nda, kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Kǝliyopasu, yiwa nyi, ji na, “Na gǝ mǝthlǝpi wu Urshalima, kǝra na ngǝ sǝnbiya sǝra ɗarkǝr wu pidaˈyar kǝ mai ya?”
LUK 24:19 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Sǝr mi ˈyar ara?” Kǝ ndǝ na anǝ nyi, “Sǝra ɗa ǝnga Yesu ndǝr Nazǝratu. Naja nabi, kǝra ǝnga dǝnama wu sǝra ju na ǝnga mǝl wu mwar Hyal ǝnga nji patǝu,
LUK 24:20 kǝ pubu dǝdǝgalˈyar ǝnga nji dǝdǝgal nǝr mǝn lǝri nyi aga nja tsǝya nyi, kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa dlakǝya nyi ar wu dladlakau.
LUK 24:21 Ɗǝɗǝmǝ ˈyi wu nggani abǝr naja ngu sa mbǝɗana njir Izirayila! Ama kǝ ja ǝshina ngǝ pida makǝrkura nyi ǝnggǝra sǝ kǝ ɗarkǝr.
LUK 24:22 Kǝl kǝ zhizhi nyi mai, alenyi mathlǝkǝˈyi kǝra wu pama ˈya nar ˈya sǝ dǝdǝgur. Ara ndǝ maˈyi a ndar huwa nyi ǝmudlǝ kaɗǝu,
LUK 24:23 ama nandǝ thlǝwa dza ja wu hu mai, kǝ ndǝ sha shili, ndǝ nar ˈya, abǝr ndǝ lari waladi kǝra na anǝ ˈya abǝr ǝnga pi nga ja.
LUK 24:24 Alenyi nju pama ˈya ndǝ maˈyi a ndar hu ndǝ nda lari abangǝ nga nyi ǝnggǝra mathlǝkǝˈyi ta na, ama nanda ǝnga Kǝrnda nandǝ lari nyi mai.”
LUK 24:25 Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nda, “Əm, nahyi nji kǝra gǝra ǝnga ɗǝnga, aˈyi ɓatsǝ anǝ hyi hya hǝnggǝri ǝnga sǝra nabiˈyar nana mai!
LUK 24:26 A mbari anǝ Kǝrsiti ja sa ɓwaɓwatǝˈyar kau, ja dzǝgwa gu kadakadarkur nyi, aˈyi abangǝ wa?”
LUK 24:27 Kǝ ji cabiya nda sǝra tsǝtsǝfǝ nǝ ndǝr Hyal na ar kǝra ja, mbari ar highiɓǝ Musa baˈanǝ tsǝfǝri nabiˈyar patǝu.
LUK 24:28 Ənggǝra ndǝ dla lǝhǝu wu dzǝri mǝlmǝ kǝra nda vǝr maˈyi a vuwa gwa, kǝ Yesu mǝl ǝnggǝr tǝrabiya a ndumwar nda,
LUK 24:29 ama kǝ ndǝ ciɗǝ nyi nda vǝr na, “Nggya ǝnga ˈya, ara wagǝu a ɗari, kǝ ja pǝci a gya tǝɗǝri.” Kǝ ji nu nda ji nda nggya ǝnga nda.
LUK 24:30 Ənggǝra ndǝ nggya aga sǝm sǝr sǝm, kǝ ji hǝri macikǝl ba ji fǝnggǝr barka, kǝ ji ɓǝɓǝlǝwa ba ji tǝkǝna nda.
LUK 24:31 Ənggau kǝ liya nda pahau, ndǝ tsamǝ ri nyi. Ama kǝ ji sanakǝr wu liya nda.
LUK 24:32 Ndǝ na anǝ kuvwar nda, “Ɗǝm ya, hu ɗa mǝn aˈyi nyinyau ǝnga caguli ar pǝci kǝra ja vǝr ndǝr anǝ mǝn ar lagu wa, ǝnggǝra ja vǝr cabiya mǝn sǝra tsǝtsǝfau wu ndǝr Hyal wa?”
LUK 24:33 Kǝ ndǝ hyaˈari ǝnga kusa ndǝ sha a vu Urshalima. Ndǝ thlǝwa nanda kumo a sǝrtangǝ ta ǝkkǝˈyi alenyi nji a vu na,
LUK 24:34 kǝ ndǝ nar nda, kadzangǝ, “Thlagǝ a hyaˈari! A canǝ nyi ja kǝrnyi anǝ Biturusu!”
LUK 24:35 Ənga tsu nanda mǝthlǝ kǝ nar nda sǝra ɗa ǝnga nda wu lagu ǝnga ǝnggǝra ndǝ tsamǝ ri Yesu ayukuɗa ji ɓǝɓǝlǝwa nda macikǝl.
LUK 24:36 Tsu nda vǝr ndǝr ar kǝra sǝ kau, kukuthlǝ kǝja Yesu taˈyu wu pama nda, kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Jamǝkur ja nggya ǝnga hyi.”
LUK 24:37 Ama kǝ ndǝ gǝrahǝ nda vǝr tsǝdzau, ma ndǝ nggani dǝgur ngǝ canǝ nda kǝr.
LUK 24:38 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Mi ngǝ ɗa hyi gǝrahǝ abanga, ǝnga hyu nggya ǝnga tǝkǝkǝr wu ɗǝfuwa hya?
LUK 24:39 Tsamiya mau tsa yau ǝnga hya yau aga hya lari, nayi ǝnga kǝrɗa ngau. Tsǝkwar ɗa mau, aga hya sǝni abǝr dǝgur aˈyi ǝnga kum ǝnga ɗǝhi, ǝnggǝr kǝ hya vǝr lari ɗa kǝ mai.”
LUK 24:40 Ayukuɗa ji nana abangau, kǝ ji canǝ nda tsa ja ǝnga hya ja.
LUK 24:41 Tsu nda vǝr caguli ara sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝ ɗa kau, ama tsu nda ǝnga tǝkǝkǝr wu ɗǝfuwa nda, kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Sǝr sǝm aˈyi ara hyi nga nyi ya?”
LUK 24:42 Kǝ ndǝ nǝ nyi kalfi kukubwa.
LUK 24:43 Kǝ ji dlǝwuri ji sǝmku, nanda kǝl tsamǝ nyi.
LUK 24:44 Ji na anǝ nda, “Sǝˈyar kǝ ngǝ sǝra yi ndǝr anǝ hyi ar kǝri pǝci kǝra yi tsu ǝnga hyi, abǝr a mbari nja nyabiya sǝra nji tsǝfǝri ar kǝra yau wu dlaɗǝ nǝ lagu Musa, ǝnga tsǝfǝ nǝ nabiˈyar ǝnga Zabura tsu.”
LUK 24:45 Kǝ ji mǝliya ndǝ sǝnbiya sǝra tsǝtsǝfau wu ndǝr Hyal,
LUK 24:46 Ji nar nda, “Abangǝ nga nyi tsǝtsǝfau, abǝr a ɗar tsaˈa anǝ Kǝrsiti ja lari ɓwaɓwatǝu, pǝci makǝrkura nyi ba ja hyaˈari sara vir tau.
LUK 24:47 Ətsu wu thlǝmǝ nyi nga nju nda tǝtǝlna ndǝr Hyal anǝ njir duniya patǝ aga nda tubi nda uya tǝfǝbiya bikǝr nda. Nju nda dzǝguya sǝ kǝ wu Urshalima.
LUK 24:48 Nahyi ngǝ sakida sǝˈyar kau.
LUK 24:49 Kǝja, yu nda sǝwa hyi sǝra dǝɗa mǝliya hyi alkawal abǝr ju sǝwa. Ama hya sǝkǝ wu mǝlmǝ kwatahǝu, kǝl nji nǝ hyi dǝnama sara dǝmǝlmau.”
LUK 24:50 Kǝ ji hǝbiya nda a biyar ya mǝlmau, ndǝ maˈyi ba a vu Bethlani. A ndǝna, ji hyaˈana tsa ja dǝmǝlmau kǝ ji fǝnggǝr nda barka.
LUK 24:51 Ənggǝra ja vǝr fǝ barka anǝ nda, kǝ ji tǝkǝbiya dzǝ ǝnga nda, ji maˈyi a dǝmǝlmau.
LUK 24:52 Nanda tsu ndǝ dzǝgwa dlǝvǝ nyi, ndǝ sha a vu Urshalima, nyinyau ǝnga huɗǝ pǝrtǝu gagaɗau.
LUK 24:53 Ndu shili parangǝ tsu wu ki Hyal nda vǝr fal Hyal.
JOH 1:1 Kadivira Hyal dzǝguya duniya ndǝr aˈyi, ndǝr kǝ ǝnga Hyal nga ja, ǝnga tsu ndǝr kǝ Hyal ngau.
JOH 1:2 Aˈyi ja ǝnga Hyal kadivira ja dzǝguya duniya.
JOH 1:3 Lagu nyi ngǝ Hyal mǝliya sǝ patǝu, ma aˈyi ǝnga ja mai, sǝ aˈyi kǝra Hyal mǝliya wu sǝra ji mǝlna mai.
JOH 1:4 Wu ja ngǝ pi, najaka pi tsu ca ngǝ mbǝmbǝl nǝ nji.
JOH 1:5 Mbǝmbǝla nyi a vǝr mbǝl wu kuthlǝu, ama kuthla nyi aˈyi a sǝn ciya mbǝmbǝla nyi mai.
JOH 1:6 Vanyi ndǝ aˈyi kǝra Hyal sǝwa, thlǝmǝ nyi ca ngǝ Yahwana.
JOH 1:7 Ji shili ar viya sakida ar kǝra mbǝmbǝl kau, aga patǝr nju nda mbǝrsa ǝnga ja lagu nyi.
JOH 1:8 Naja ǝnga kǝrnyi ngǝ mbǝmbǝl kǝ mai, ama ji shili ar viya sakida ar kǝra mbǝmbǝla nyi.
JOH 1:9 Mbǝmbǝl kǝra jiri, kǝra wu nǝ nyi mbǝmbǝlkur anǝ kalar ndǝ a vǝr shili wu duniya.
JOH 1:10 Ji shili wu duniya kǝra naja ngǝ mǝliya ǝnga kǝrnyi, ama alaga abangau, njir duniya aˈyi sǝnbiya nyi mai.
JOH 1:11 Ji shili aga ˈyiˈyi kǝra nǝ nyi, ama nji nyi aˈyi dlǝwuri nyi mai.
JOH 1:12 Ama anǝ patǝr njira dlǝwuri nyi, njira mbǝrsa ǝnga thlǝmǝ nyi, anǝ ndar ja dǝnama nǝ ɗa wazha Hyal.
JOH 1:13 Aˈyi wazha yaya wu ndǝkur mai, alaga lagur cim nǝ ndǝkur mai, ǝnga alaga lagur ɗǝnga nǝ salkur mai, ama yaya sara ara Hyal.
JOH 1:14 Ndǝr kau, ba ji ɗa ndapi, ba ji nggya wu pama mǝn. Naˈya tsu lari kadakadarkur nyi, kadakadarkur nǝ Zǝr Zǝmǝ pathlǝ sara ara Tada, kǝra nyinyau ǝnga mayiwakur ba ǝnga jirkur.
JOH 1:15 Yahwana ngǝ lǝr sakida ar kǝra ja, ji hyaˈana ɗahǝu, ji na, “Naja kǝ ngǝ ndǝra yi ndǝr ar kǝra ja ar pǝci kǝra yi na, ‘Ndǝra wu shili wu yukuɗǝ ɗa, naja ndiya ɗa, ara aˈyi ja kadivira nji ya ɗa.’ ”
JOH 1:16 Sara wu nyinyikur nǝ mayiwakur nyi nga mǝn uya barka, ju lǝ mayiwakur nyi ar kǝr ar kǝr.
JOH 1:17 Arya dlaɗǝ shili lagu tsa Musa, ama mayiwakur ǝnga jirkur shili lagu Yesu Kǝrsiti.
JOH 1:18 Ndǝ aˈyi kǝra saya fǝr li ar Hyal mai, ama kǝl Zǝr Hyal Zǝmǝ pathlǝu, kǝra a vǝr nggya ǝnga Tada, a cabiya mǝnǝr ja Hyal.
JOH 1:19 Kǝja sakida kǝra Yahwana lǝri ar pǝci kǝra njira nggurǝm nǝ Yahudiya sara wu Urshalima sǝwa pubuˈyar ǝnga njir Lawi aga nda yiwabiya tara wa nga ja.
JOH 1:20 Naji nggǝl ara nar nda jiri mai, ama ji nana ar babal abǝr, “Nayi ngǝ Kǝrsiti mai.”
JOH 1:21 Kǝ ndǝ yiwa nyi ndǝ na, “Ya, wa nga ga? Nagǝ ngǝ Iliya ya?” Kǝ ji shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Awau, nayi ngǝ mai.” Əngwar nda, “Ya, nagǝ ngǝ nabiya nyi ya?” Kǝ ji shaɗǝwa, “Awau.”
JOH 1:22 Ayukuɗa nyi patǝu, kǝ ndǝ na, “Wa nga ga? Nar ˈya sǝra ˈya sha ˈya nda nar nyi anǝ njira sǝwa ˈya. Mi nga gu na ar kǝra kǝr nga?”
JOH 1:23 Kǝ Yahwana shaɗǝwa nda lagu ndǝr nabi Əshaya, ji na, “Nayi ngǝ ɗahǝ a vǝr ngga a gwar tagǝu, ja vǝr na, ‘Hya pabǝri nyi lagu anǝ Thlagǝu, hya mǝliya lagu tataˈyi pir wu mwa nyi.’ ”
JOH 1:24 Kǝ alenyi njir Farisi, njira nji sǝwa
JOH 1:25 yiwa nyi, “Ma nagǝ aˈyi Kǝrsiti mai, ǝnga nagǝ aˈyi Iliya mai, ba nagǝ tsu aˈyi nabiya nyi mai, mi ngǝ ɗa gu mǝl baɓǝtizǝma?”
JOH 1:26 Əngwar Yahwana, “Nayau, ya vǝr mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ hyi ǝnga ˈyimi. Ama vanyi ndǝra ndiya ɗa ǝnga dǝnama a vǝr shili, kǝra alaga sǝr mba ɓiɓi nyi nayi aˈyi ɗa tsa aga ya pǝlna mai.
JOH 1:27 Ju sa mǝliya hyi baɓǝtizǝma ǝnga Mambǝl Cicau ba ǝnga uˈu.”
JOH 1:28 Sǝˈyar kǝ patǝ ɗarkǝr wu Bethlani, a biyar ya dǝl Urdǝnu, vira Yahwana a vǝr mǝl baɓǝtizǝma ari.
JOH 1:29 Əzǝgǝkura nyi ba Yahwana lari Yesu a vǝr shili lagu nyi, kǝ ji na, “Kǝja, Zǝr Gamǝ nǝ Hyal, kǝra hǝna bikǝ nǝ njir duniya!
JOH 1:30 Ndǝ kǝ nga ya vǝr ndǝr ar kǝri ta, ta yi na, abǝr ‘Ndǝ aˈyi a vǝr shili ayukuɗǝ ɗa, ama naja dǝgal a ndiya ɗa ara tsu ɗǝɗǝmǝ aˈyi ja kadivira nja ya ɗa.’
JOH 1:31 Nayi ǝnga kǝrɗa sayi sǝni nyi mai, ama yi shili, yi sa mǝl baɓǝtizǝma ǝnga ˈyimi anǝ nji aga ya cabiya nyi anǝ njir Izirayila.”
JOH 1:32 Kǝ Yahwana lǝri najaka sakida abǝr, “Yi lari Mambǝl a vǝr shida sara dǝmǝlmau, a papa mbǝthla, ji sa ndzafau a dar kǝra ja.
JOH 1:33 Nayi ǝnga kǝrɗa yu sǝni nyi mai, ama kǝl ta ndǝra sǝwa ɗa aga sa mǝl baɓǝtizǝma ǝnga ˈyimi nar ɗa abǝr, ‘Ndǝra gǝ lari Mambǝl ndzafau ar ja, naja ngu nda mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ nji ǝnga Mambǝl Cicau.’
JOH 1:34 Nayi tsu a lar yi sǝkǝ nyabiya dzǝ ar kǝra ja, ca ngǝ ɗa yi lǝri sakida abǝr ndǝ kau, Zǝr Hyal ngau.”
JOH 1:35 Əzǝgǝkura nyi Yahwana ǝnga nji mǝthlǝ sara wu pama zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar ar vi ta wayu.
JOH 1:36 Kǝ Yahwana lari Yesu ja vǝr tǝrabiya, kǝ ji na, “Lara mau, Zǝr Gamǝ nǝ Hyal!”
JOH 1:37 Ənggǝra zǝmbǝlmaˈyar kǝ mǝthlǝ nggari sǝra Yahwana na, kǝ ndǝ nu Yesu.
JOH 1:38 Ta Yesu shabiya dzau, ba ji lari nda nda a vǝr nu nyi, kǝ ji yiwa nda, “Mi nga hyu gala?” Əngwar nda, “Rabi” kǝra cabiya Malǝmǝ ngau, “Əmani nga gu nggya?”
JOH 1:39 Kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Anda mau hya sa lari.” A ndu saka foɗǝ nǝ wagǝu, kǝ ndǝ maˈyi ndǝ nda lari viya nyi, ba ndǝ hǝna pǝkǝ ǝnga ja.
JOH 1:40 Andǝrawusu, zamǝya Simanu Biturusu, aˈyi ja pathlǝ wu pama nji mǝthlǝ kǝra nu Yesu ayukuɗa Yahwana nana ndǝr ar kǝra Yesu.
JOH 1:41 Sǝ tanggǝrma kǝra Andǝrawusu mǝliya ca ngǝ, ji maˈyi ji nda thlǝwa zamǝ nyi Simanu, ba ji nar nyi, “A nǝr ˈya Ndǝ Cacaɗau” ndǝra nju ngga ǝnga Kǝrsiti.
JOH 1:42 Kǝ ji shili ǝnga Simanu a shili ara Yesu. Yesu tsamǝ nyi, ba ji na, “Nagǝ ngǝ Simanu zǝr Yahwana. Nju nda ngga ngau ǝnga Kefasu,” kǝra ma nji shabiya ca ngǝ Biturusu.
JOH 1:43 Əzǝgǝkura nyi tsu kǝ Yesu biya ju maˈyi a vu Galili. Kǝ ji thlǝwa Fǝlipǝu, kǝ ji na anǝ nyi, “Nu ɗa.”
JOH 1:44 Fǝlipǝu sara wu Bethlesaida nga ja, mǝlmǝr Andǝrawusu ǝnga Biturusu.
JOH 1:45 Fǝlipǝu maˈyi ji nda thlǝwa Nathlaniyalu, kǝ ji na anǝ nyi, “A nǝr ˈya ndǝra Musa tsǝfǝri sǝ ar kǝri wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ dlaɗau ǝnga nabiˈyar tsu tsǝfǝri, naja ngǝ Yesu ndǝr Nazǝratu, zǝr Yusufu.”
JOH 1:46 Kǝ Nathlaniyalu yiwa ji na, “Sǝ tsapǝu a sǝn biya sara wu Nazǝratu ya?” “A ndǝ ga sa lari ǝnga kǝrngau,” ǝngwar Fǝlipǝu.
JOH 1:47 Ta Yesu lari Nathlaniyalu a vǝr shili ara ja, kǝ ji na ar kǝra ja, “Lara mau ndǝr Izirayila nǝ jijiri, ndǝra gǝra ǝnga nggyabiya fafati.”
JOH 1:48 Kǝ Nathlaniyalu yiwa ji na anǝ Yesu, “Lagu mani nga gǝ sǝn ɗa?” Əngwar Yesu, “Ar pǝci kǝra gǝ ǝgya kiɗa wur martǝndǝm ta nga yi lar ngau, kadivira Fǝlipǝu dzǝgwa ngga ngau.”
JOH 1:49 Kǝ Nathlaniyalu na, “Malǝmǝ, nagǝ ngǝ Zǝr Hyal; nagǝ ngǝ Tǝl nǝ njir Izirayila!”
JOH 1:50 Yesu nar nyi anǝ Nathlaniyalu, “Gǝ mbǝrsa ara yi nar ngǝ abǝr yi lar ngǝ ar pǝci kǝra gǝ ǝgya kiɗa wur martǝndǝm ta ya? Jiri, gu nda lari sǝra a ndiya kau.”
JOH 1:51 Kǝ Yesu ɓǝra nar nyi, “Ənga jiri nga yu na anǝ hyi, hyu nda lari dǝmǝlmǝ a pahǝri, waladiˈyar nǝ Hyal a vǝr di ǝnga gya ar kǝra Zǝr Ndau.”
JOH 2:1 Ar pǝci nǝ makǝrkura nyi, mini nǝ hǝ dzǝ aˈyi wu mǝlmǝ Kana nǝ ˈyiˈyir Galili. Miya Yesu aˈyi ja a ndǝna.
JOH 2:2 Yesu ǝkkǝˈyi zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar ma nji nggǝya nda a shili ar vir mini kau.
JOH 2:3 Ənggǝra ˈyimir wur inabi kuɗau, kǝ miya Yesu na anǝ nyi, “ˈYimir wur inabir nda a kuɗǝri.”
JOH 2:4 Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Ama, mi ngǝ nǝr mǝn wu sǝ ka? Pǝci ɗa ma aˈyi ɗa kwatahǝ mai.”
JOH 2:5 Kǝ miya Yesu nar nyi anǝ njir tǝkǝ sǝr sǝm, “Nahya mau, kalar sǝra ji na anǝ hyi, ca nga hya mǝl.”
JOH 2:6 Lǝha dzǝr viya nyi ha tsǝka aˈyi kwa, kǝra njir Yahudiya wu kǝbǝ kwatǝ ci dzǝ ǝni, ǝnggǝr kǝra mbǝrsar nda cabiya. Kalar ha nyi wu sǝn hǝri ǝgwa kwa kwa ǝnga ˈyimi.
JOH 2:7 Kǝ Yesu nar nyi anǝ njir tǝkǝ sǝr sǝm, “Nyanyana mǝ haˈyar kǝ patǝ ǝnga ˈyimi.” Ba ndǝ nyanyana nda ba ar miya.
JOH 2:8 Kǝ ji na anǝ nda, “Kabangǝkau, gǝri nya mau a nda nǝ tsahwaˈa.” Kǝ ndǝ gǝri ndǝ hǝr nyi a nda.
JOH 2:9 Ta tsahwaˈa ɗahari ˈyimi hyalagǝ kǝra sha aga ˈyimir wur inabi, naji sǝnbiya vira nji uya nyi sara ar mai, ama njir tǝkǝ sǝr sǝm wu sǝni. Kǝ tsahwaˈa nggar salkwanjili a ndumwar sau,
JOH 2:10 kǝ ji na anǝ nyi, “Kalar ndu shili ǝnga ˈyimir wur inabi kǝra ndiya ǝnga mǝsahǝu tsu kaɗǝu, ayukuɗa ndǝ sa, ndǝ nyau, ba nja shili ǝnga kǝra cacaɓǝu, ama, nǝ ngǝ kau, pamǝ nga nyi ara nji, gǝ piyari kǝra mǝsahǝu kǝl kabangǝkau!”
JOH 2:11 Najakǝ ngǝ sǝ dǝdǝgur nǝ tanggǝrma kǝra Yesu mǝliya, ji mǝliya sǝ kǝ wu mǝlmǝ Kana nǝ Galili. Najakǝ ngǝ cabiya kadakadarkur nyi, ǝnga ji mǝliya zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar mbǝrsa ǝnga ja.
JOH 2:12 Ayukuɗa kǝ ngǝ Yesu ǝnga mǝnyi ǝnga zamǝ nyiˈyar ba ǝnga zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar maˈyi a gyiwu Kafarnahumu. A gyina, ndǝ sǝkari nǝ pida ɗiyawu.
JOH 2:13 Ta pǝcir lardur vǝlna nǝ njir Yahudiya ɗa lǝhǝu, kǝ Yesu maˈyi a du Urshalima.
JOH 2:14 Wu huɗa ki Hyal, ba ji thlǝwa nja vǝr ɗǝlna thla, ǝnga tǝmahǝu ǝnga mbǝthlaˈyar aga saɗaka, ba ji thlǝwa alenyi nji tsu nda vǝr bǝla bǝla gǝnnar nda.
JOH 2:15 Kǝ Yesu lǝmiya kurpǝ sara wu ǝpa, ba ji kǝdlǝbiya nda patǝ sara wu Ki Hyal. Ji kǝdlǝbiya tǝmahǝ ǝkkǝˈyi thla, ba ji shashabiya tǝmbǝl bǝla bǝla gǝnnar nda a dǝmǝlmau, ǝnga ji tǝtǝlna gǝnnar nda.
JOH 2:16 Kǝ Yesu nar nyi anǝ njira vǝr ɗǝlna mbǝthlaˈyar kau, “Faˈabiya mau sǝˈyar kǝ ǝnggau! Hya sara shabiya ki dǝɗa aga sugu mai.”
JOH 2:17 Ənggǝra sǝ kǝ ɗarkǝr, kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar ɗǝngari sǝra tsǝtsǝfau, wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ Hyal abǝr, “Huɗǝ hamǝ nǝ ki Hyal a vǝr mbǝ ɗa ǝnggǝr uˈu.”
JOH 2:18 Kǝ njira nggurǝm nǝ Yahudiya yiwa Yesu, ndǝ na, “Ya, mi ngǝ sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝra gu sǝn mǝliya, kǝra wu cabiya ˈya abǝr aˈyi gǝ ǝnga dǝnama nǝ mǝliya sǝˈyar ka?”
JOH 2:19 Kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Hya dlana ki Hyal kau, ba ya sa hyaˈana wu pida makǝru.”
JOH 2:20 Kǝ ndǝ shaɗǝwa nyi, ndǝ na, “Nji hǝri fa foɗǝ kumunyi apǝ kwa a vǝr hǝr ki Hyal kau, ya, abari nga gu sǝn hyaˈana nyi wu pida makǝr ka?”
JOH 2:21 Ama ki Hyal kǝra Yesu wu ndǝr ar kǝri kau, dza ja ngau.
JOH 2:22 Ayukuɗa Yesu hyaˈari sara vir tau, kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar ɗǝngari sǝ kǝ Yesu nar nda kau. Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa mbǝrsa ǝnga sǝra tsǝtsǝfau wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ Hyal ǝnga sǝra Yesu nana.
JOH 2:23 Ar pǝci kǝra Yesu wu lardur nǝ vǝlna wu Urshalima, nji gangǝu mbǝrsa ǝnga ja arya sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝra ndu lari ji mǝl.
JOH 2:24 Ama Yesu aˈyi fiyafǝ ǝnga nda mai, ara ju sǝnbiya nji patǝu.
JOH 2:25 Naja aˈyi wu yiwu nja lǝr sakida ar kǝra nji anǝ nyi mai, arya ju sǝn sǝra wu ɗǝfuwa ndapi.
JOH 3:1 Saya ɗa vanyi ndǝr Farisi aˈyi kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Nikodimosu, naja pathlǝ wu pama njira nggurǝm nǝ Yahudiya.
JOH 3:2 Ji shili ǝgya Yesu uvuˈyi, ji sa na, “Malǝmǝ, ˈyi wu sǝni abǝr nagǝ malǝmǝ ngau, sara ara Hyal, arya ndǝr sǝn mǝliya sǝˈyar kǝ ga vǝr mǝl kǝ aˈyi mai, kǝl ndǝra Hyal ǝnga ja.”
JOH 3:3 Kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Yi wu nar ngau jirkura nyi, ndǝr sǝn gwu tǝlkur Hyal aˈyi mai kǝl ma nji ɓǝra yabiya nyi nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi.”
JOH 3:4 Kǝ Nikodimosu yiwa nyi, ji na, “Lagu mani nga nja ɓǝra sǝn yabiya ndǝra a halǝr ka? Ja ɓǝra sǝn sha a vu huɗa mǝnyi aga nja ɓǝra yabiya nyi nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi ya?”
JOH 3:5 Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Jiri nga yu na anǝ ngau, ndǝr sǝn gwu tǝlkur Hyal aˈyi mai, kǝl nji ɓǝra yabiya nyi nǝ ˈyimi ǝnga nǝ Mambǝl.
JOH 3:6 Sǝra ndapi yabiya ndǝ ngau, ama sǝra Mambǝl yabiya tsu mambǝl ngau.
JOH 3:7 Ja sara ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ ngǝ mai, ara yi na, abǝr, ‘Kǝl nji ɓǝra yabiya ngǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi.’
JOH 3:8 Yambaɗǝ wu sǝ a ndar vira ju yiwu. Gu nggari ǝnggǝra ju sau, ama nagǝ wu sǝn nana vira ji hyaˈari sara ari ǝnga vira ju maˈyi a ndar tsu mai. Abangǝ nga nyi tsu ǝnga ndǝra nji yabiya nyi wu Mambǝl.”
JOH 3:9 Kǝ Nikodimosu yiwa Yesu, ji na, “Abari ngǝ sǝkǝ wu sǝn ɗa?”
JOH 3:10 Kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nyi, ji na, “Ya, nagǝ malǝmǝ dǝgal ngau wu Izirayila, ama nagǝ wu nggabiya sǝˈyar kǝ mai ya?
JOH 3:11 Jiri nga yu na anǝ ngau, ˈyi wu ndǝr ar kǝra sǝra ˈyi wu sǝni, ǝnga ˈyi wu lǝr sakida ar kǝra sǝra ˈyi lari, ama alaga abangau nahyi aˈyi dlǝwuri sakidar ˈya kǝ mai.
JOH 3:12 Ma yu ndǝr anǝ hyi ar kǝra sǝra wu duniya, nahyi mbǝrsa ǝni mai, abari nga hyu sǝn nda mbǝrsa ma yi ndǝr anǝ hyi ar kǝra sǝra a dǝmǝlma?
JOH 3:13 Ndǝ aˈyi kǝra saya maˈyi a dǝmǝlmǝ mai, kǝl naja Zǝr Ndǝ kǝra shida sara dǝna.
JOH 3:14 Ənggǝr kǝra Musa har pabau a dar wu tagǝ mashi ta, abangǝ tsu kǝl nji hyaˈana Zǝr Ndau a dar wu,
JOH 3:15 aga kalar ndǝra mbǝrsa ǝnga ja wu uya pi gǝra kuɗau.”
JOH 3:16 “Arya Hyal ca yiwukur anǝ njir duniya gagaɗau, ca ngǝ ɗa ji lǝri Zǝr nyi zǝmǝ pir, aga kalar ndǝra hǝnggǝri ǝnga ja, naji wu tǝ mai, ama ju uya pi gǝra kuɗau.
JOH 3:17 Arya Hyal aˈyi sǝwa Zǝr nyi a shida wu duniya aga ja sa mǝlna nyi numa anǝ duniya mai, ama aga njir duniya a uya mbǝɗau lagu nyi.
JOH 3:18 Kalar ndǝra mbǝrsa ǝnga Zǝr Hyal, numa aˈyi wu sǝm nyi mai. Ama kalar ndǝra aˈyi mbǝrsa ǝnga ja mai, numa a sǝmku nyi ri tsu kaɗǝ ara naji mbǝrsa ǝnga thlǝmǝr Zǝr Hyal kǝra zǝmǝ pir mai.
JOH 3:19 Kǝja sǝra ju nda mǝl numa ar kǝri, mbǝmbǝl shili wu duniya, ama njir duniya wu yiwu kuthlǝu a ndiya mbǝmbǝl ara sǝr mǝla nda ɗǝmwaˈyu.
JOH 3:20 Kalar njira wu mǝl sǝ ɗǝmwaˈyu, shishir dza nda wu yiwu mbǝmbǝl mai, ara hivǝr sǝr mǝla nda a biyar babal.
JOH 3:21 Ama njir mǝl sǝra tsaˈa ndu shili ar vi mbǝmbǝl, aga nja lari ar babal abǝr sǝra ndu mǝl sǝra Hyal wu yiwu ngau.”
JOH 3:22 Ayukuɗa kau, kǝ Yesu ǝnga zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar maˈyi a ndar ˈyiˈyir Yahudiya. A ndǝna ji nda ɓǝliya sar kushu, ju mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ nji.
JOH 3:23 Yahwana nǝ nyi tsu ja vǝr mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ nju mǝlmǝ Ayinanu kǝra lǝhǝu wu dzǝr mǝlmǝ Salimu, ara ˈyimi aˈyi gangǝu a ndǝna. Nji kǝl shili nga ndu shili ju mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ nda.
JOH 3:24 (Sǝkǝ ɗarkǝr kadivira nji fuwa Yahwana wu fursǝna.)
JOH 3:25 Kǝ zǝmbǝlmaˈyar nǝ Yahwana gu kǝpal ǝnga vanyi ndǝr Yahudiya ar kǝra ci dzǝ kǝra dlaɗǝ nana nja mǝl.
JOH 3:26 Ndǝ shili ǝgya Yahwana, ndǝ sa na anǝ nyi, “Malǝmǝ, ndǝ ta ǝnga gǝ a biyar ya dǝl Urdǝnu ta, ndǝ ta gǝ lǝri sakida ar kǝr ta, kǝja ja vǝr mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ nji ǝnga patǝr nja vǝr sha shili ara ja.”
JOH 3:27 Kǝ Yahwana shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Ndǝr sǝn dlǝwuri sǝ aˈyi mai, kǝl sǝra Hyal nǝ nyi.
JOH 3:28 Nahyi ǝnga kǝrhyi ngǝ sakida ɗa arya yi na anǝ hyi, ‘Nayi ngǝ Kǝrsiti mai, ama Hyal sǝwa ɗa wu mwa nyi.’
JOH 3:29 Ar pǝcir hǝ dzau, kwanjili nǝ sal kwanjili ngau. Bazhiya sal kwanjili kǝra shili ar vir hǝ dzǝ kau, kǝl sǝkǝ nga ja, aga ja nggari ɗaha sal kwanjili. Ju nyi ǝnga huɗǝ pipida ma ji nggari sal kwanjili a vǝr ndǝr. Lagu kǝ tsu ngǝ huɗǝ pipida ɗa a nyabiyar dzau.
JOH 3:30 A ɗari tsaˈa ja cakau, nayi tsu ya gǝnna dzau.
JOH 3:31 “Ndǝra shida sara a dǝmǝlmau, naja nga adabanga nji patǝu. Patǝr njira wu duniya nǝ duniya ngau, ǝnga ndu ndǝr ar kǝra sǝr duniya. Ndǝra shida sara a dǝmǝlmau, naja nga adabanga nji patǝu.
JOH 3:32 Ju lǝri sakida sǝra ji lari ǝnga ji nggari, alaga abangau, ndǝ aˈyi kǝra mbǝrsa ǝnga sakida nyi mai.
JOH 3:33 Ama kalar ndǝra dlǝwuri sakida nyi a cabiyari abǝr Hyal ndǝ jijiri ngau.
JOH 3:34 Ara ndǝra Hyal sǝwa, ndǝr Hyal nga ju na, arya Hyal nǝ nyi Mambǝl nyi nyinyau.
JOH 3:35 Tada wu yiwu Zǝr nyi, ba ji fuwa patǝr sǝ wu tsa ja.
JOH 3:36 Kalar ndǝra mbǝrsa ǝnga Zǝra nyi aˈyi ja ǝnga pi gǝra kuɗau. Ndǝra gǝra ɓǝla sǝra Zǝra nyi nana, naji wu uya pi mai, ama Hyal wu ɗǝfu ǝnga ja.”
JOH 4:1 Njir Farisi nggari abǝr Yesu a vǝr dumwa ǝnga uya nji, ǝnga mǝl baɓǝtizǝma anǝ zǝmbǝlma gangǝu a ndiya Yahwana.
JOH 4:2 Kwalaga kǝ aˈyi Yesu ǝnga kǝrnyi nga vǝr mǝl baɓǝtizǝma kǝ mai, ama zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar ngau.
JOH 4:3 Ənggǝra Yesu nggari abangau, kǝ ji piyari ˈyiˈyir Yahudi ba ji ɓǝra sha a vu ˈyiˈyir Galili.
JOH 4:4 Kabangǝkǝ a mbari kǝl Yesu ja tǝrabiya wu Samariya.
JOH 4:5 Kǝ ji dla wu vanyi mǝlmǝ wu ˈyiˈyir Samariya kǝra nja ngga ǝnga Sayika. Vi kau, lǝhǝ nga nyi a dzǝr vira Yakubu nǝ nyi anǝ zǝr nyi Yusufu.
JOH 4:6 Ar vi kau, mǝla nǝ Yakubu aˈyi. Ar pǝci kǝra Yesu hǝɗa ǝnga ɓau, ba ji ɓǝliya sar a miya mǝla nyi. Sǝkǝ ɗarkǝr ǝnggǝr saka kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ nǝ puci.
JOH 4:7 Kǝ vanyi mala nǝ Samariya shila gwa mǝla. Kǝ Yesu na anǝ nyi, “Usi, gǝr ɗa ˈyimi ya tǝwari.”
JOH 4:8 (Zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar tsu a maˈyir nda a vu huɗa mǝlmǝ aga nda vuwa ɗǝl sǝr sǝm.)
JOH 4:9 Kǝ mala Samariya kǝ na anǝ Yesu, “Abari nagǝ ndǝr Yahudiya a sǝn yiwa ˈyimi ara ya, nayi mala Samariya?” (Ara sǝ aˈyi kǝra wu daɓǝri ndǝr Yahudiya ǝnga ndǝr Samariya mai.)
JOH 4:10 Əngwar Yesu, “Maja abǝr gu sǝni sǝ kurthlǝ nǝ Hyal kǝra ju lau, ǝnga ndǝra na anǝ ngau, ‘Gǝr ɗa ˈyimi ya tǝwari,’ gu sǝn yiwa nyi, ba ja nǝ ngǝ ˈyimi nǝr lǝ pi.”
JOH 4:11 Kǝ mala kǝ na, “Malǝmǝ, kǝja sǝr gǝ ˈyimi aˈyi ara gǝ mai, ya, kǝja mǝla kǝ dzǝgamǝ nga nyi, lagu mani nga gu sǝn gǝr ɗa ˈyimi lǝ pi ka?
JOH 4:12 Ɗǝm ya, naga ndiya dǝrˈya Yakubu, ndǝra labiya ˈya mǝla kǝ ya? Naja ǝnga kǝrnyi ma, ji sa ˈyimi sara a gwa, ǝnga wazha nyi ba maˈwi nyiˈyar.”
JOH 4:13 Yesu na, “Kalar ndǝra sa ˈyimi kau, hili wu ɓǝra nda tǝ nyi wayu.
JOH 4:14 Ama ndǝra sa ˈyimi kǝra yu lǝ kau, naji wu ɓǝra nggar hili mai baˈanuwa. ˈYimi kǝra yu lǝ kau, wu nda ɗa wu ja ǝnggǝr mandǝli ˈyimi kǝra wu huhwi sara wu dza ja kǝra wu nǝ nyi pi gǝra kuɗau.”
JOH 4:15 Əngwar mala kau, “Malǝmǝ, nǝ ɗa ˈyimi kau, ara ya sara ɓǝra nggari hili, ǝnga ya ɓǝra shili ǝnggau ya sa gǝ ˈyimi.”
JOH 4:16 Kǝ Yesu na, “Maˈyi ga nda shili ǝnga sal ngau.”
JOH 4:17 Əngwar ja, “Sal aˈyi ara yi mai.” Əngwar Yesu anǝ nyi, “A nabiyar gǝ jiri ǝnggǝra gǝ na abǝr, ‘Sal aˈyi ara yi mai.’
JOH 4:18 Arya jirkura nyi ca ngǝ a hǝr gǝ shili pamǝpamǝ tǝfu, ǝnga ndǝ kǝ gǝ ǝni kabangǝkǝ kǝ sal ngǝ mai, a nabiyar gǝ jiri.”
JOH 4:19 Əngwar ja, “Ndǝ dǝgalǝu, maya nggani nagǝ nabi ngau.
JOH 4:20 Əjir ˈya dlǝvǝ Hyal ar mǝ kau. Ama ǝngwar hyi njir Yahudiya wu Urshalima ngǝ vira nja kyaga dlǝvǝ Hyal.”
JOH 4:21 Kǝ Yesu na, “Mala, mbǝrsa ǝnga sǝra yu na kau, arya pǝci a vǝr shili kǝra nji tsu wu nda dlǝvǝ Tada ar mǝ kǝ mai, alaga wu Urshalima mai.
JOH 4:22 Nahyi njir Samariya nahyi wu sǝni ndǝra hyu dlǝvǝ mai, naˈya ˈyi wu sǝni ndǝra ˈyi wu dlǝvau, ara mbǝɗau shili sara ara njir Yahudiya.
JOH 4:23 Ama pǝci a vǝr shili, pǝca nyi ma a shiliri, kǝra njir dlǝvǝ Tada ǝnga jiri wu nda dlǝvǝ nyi wu mambǝl ba ǝnga jirkur, ara Tada wu gal culi nji kǝ nga dlǝvǝ nyi.
JOH 4:24 Hyal Mambǝl ngau, njir dlǝvǝ nyi kǝl nda dlǝvǝ nyi wu mambǝl ba ǝnga wu jirkur tsu.”
JOH 4:25 Mala kǝ na, “A sǝn yi abǝr Ndǝ Cacaɗau a vǝr shili ndǝra nju ngga nyi ǝnga Kǝrsiti. Ma ji shili ju sa cabiya ˈya patǝr sau.”
JOH 4:26 Yesu na, “Nayi ndǝra vǝr ndǝr anǝ ngau nayi ngau.”
JOH 4:27 Ar pǝci kǝ ngǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar sha shili, ba ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ nda ǝnggǝra ndǝ thlǝwa nyi ja vǝr ndǝr ǝnga mala. Ama ndǝr sǝn yiwa, “Mi nga ga gal ǝnga mala ka?” Ənga ndǝr sǝn na anǝ nyi, “Mi ngǝ ɗa gu ndǝr ǝnga ja?” aˈyi tsu mai.
JOH 4:28 Kǝ mala kǝ piyari tǝm gwa mǝla nyi, ba ji maˈyi a vu huɗa mǝlmau, ji vuwa nar nyi anǝ nji,
JOH 4:29 “Shila mau, hya sa lari ndǝra nar ɗa sǝra yi saya mǝlna patǝu. Abǝr naja ngǝ Kǝrsiti ya?”
JOH 4:30 Kǝ nji bibiya sara wu huɗa mǝlmau, kǝ ndǝ shili ǝgya Yesu.
JOH 4:31 Ar pǝci kǝ ngǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar a vǝr kǝdi Yesu, “Malǝmǝ, sǝm sau.”
JOH 4:32 Ama kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Sǝr sǝm aˈyi ara yi kǝra yu sǝn sǝm ama nahyi wu sǝn mai.”
JOH 4:33 Kǝ zǝmbǝlma nyiˈyar yiwa kǝrnda, ndǝ na, “Abǝr vanyi ndǝ daɓaga shili ǝnga sǝr sǝm anǝ nyi ya?”
JOH 4:34 Ama kǝ Yesu shaɗǝwa nda, ji na, “Sǝr sǝm ɗa ca ngǝ ya mǝl sǝra ndǝra sǝwa ɗa wu yiwu ǝnga ya nyabiya thlǝr nyi cipǝu.
JOH 4:35 Hyu na abǝr, ‘A hyiri hya foɗǝ aga fwaha ɗa.’ Ama yu na anǝ hyi, hya pahǝna liya hyi mǝnahǝu aga hya tsamǝ vu huɗa fa, ara a nǝr nda patǝ tsaˈa aga gǝm kabangǝkau.
