REV 9:2 Kǝ shashilga nyi pahǝna miya kaˈu kǝra nji gǝra sǝn tǝkǝna ta, kǝ ˈyar biya sara a gwa ǝnggǝr ˈyar kǝra wu biya sara ar vir thlǝ tǝm kǝra dǝgal gagaɗau. Pǝci ǝnga dǝmǝlmau haɗiya dzau ǝnga kuthlǝ ara ˈyar kǝra a vǝr biya sara wu kaˈu kǝra nji gǝra sǝn tǝkǝna ta.
REV 9:3 Sara wu ˈyar ta, kǝ ndzǝkwa shida a shida wu duniya, ǝnga nji nǝ nda dǝnama nǝ da ǝnggǝr ǝdiˈyar.
REV 9:4 Kǝ nji nar nda, abǝr nda sara lǝ ɓwaɓwatǝ anǝ sar ǝnga sǝ tsǝtsǝˈyar, ba wuˈyar mai, ama kǝl njira gǝra ǝnga mǝtsamǝ nǝ Hyal ar huɗǝma nda.
REV 9:5 Nji aˈyi nǝ nda dǝnama nǝ tsa nji mai, ama aga nda takasǝya nda wacu nǝ hya tufu. Ənga ɓwaɓwatǝ kǝra ndǝ lari ǝnggǝr da ǝdi nga nyi, kǝra dǝya ndau.
REV 9:6 Ar pǝci kau, nju gal tau ama nandǝ wu uya mai. Ndu nda cim nda tau ama ba ta hwinakǝr ara nda.
REV 9:7 Ndzǝkwa nyiˈyar ndu pa tagu kǝra nji ɓathlǝr aga gwa pa. A dar kǝra nda, ndǝ hari sǝ ǝnggǝr dara nǝ tǝlkur kǝra nji mǝliya sara wu ǝndzau, bama nda tsu wu pa bama nji.
REV 9:8 Shishir kǝra nda ǝnggǝr shishir kǝra mathlǝkǝˈyi nga nyi, ǝnga hira nda tsu ǝnggǝr hira lǝvari nga nyi.
REV 9:9 Nji haɗiya hathla nda ǝnga lǝgutǝ ha kǝra nji mǝliya sara wu liyangǝ kyakyaru, ǝnga tsǝkir ɓǝga nda ǝnggǝr tsǝkir tagu ǝnga keki tagu kǝra a vǝr hwi a nda miya pa.
REV 9:10 Aˈyi nda ǝnga shiˈwu ǝnga hir da ǝnggǝr nǝ ǝdiyau, wu shiˈwa nda dǝnama aˈyi, nǝ lǝ ɓwaɓwatǝ anǝ nji nǝ hya tufu.
REV 9:11 Aˈyi nda ǝnga tǝl kǝra wu sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra nda, naja ngǝ waladi nǝ kaˈu dzǝgamǝ gagaɗǝ ta, thlǝmǝ nyi wu miya njir Yahudiya ca ngǝ “Abadonu” ba ǝnga miya njir Gǝrikǝu tsu ca ngǝ “Apoliyanu” kǝra cabiya “Ndǝr Ndza Sau.”
REV 9:12 Sǝr tǝhuɗǝ nǝ tanggǝrma a tǝrabiyari, ama kǝja tsu mǝthla nyi a vǝr shili.
REV 9:13 Ta waladi nǝ kwakura nyi mbiɗiya nǝ nyi tǝlǝmǝ tugu, ba yi nggari ɗahǝ a vǝr biya sara ar miya cira bagadi nǝ ǝndzǝ kǝra wu mwar Hyal.
REV 9:14 Kǝ ɗahǝ kǝ na anǝ waladi nǝ kwakura nyi kau, “Pǝlna waladiˈyar kǝ foɗǝ kau, kǝra nji biya nda a gwar dǝl dǝgal nǝ Yifǝratǝsu.”
REV 9:15 Tǝma, kǝ nji pǝliya waladiˈyar kǝ foɗǝ kau, kǝra nji pabǝri nda aga najaka saka ǝnga najaka pǝci, ǝnga najaka hya ǝnga tsu najaka fa aga nda dlǝna cifǝ pathlǝu wu makǝr nǝ ndapi.
REV 9:16 Kǝja sojaˈyar nǝ pa a dar ya tagu. A nar ɗar nji gangǝkura nda, a kari nda njir pa dubu duburam gharu mǝthlǝu.
REV 9:17 Wu mǝtakǝr ɗa, kǝ yi lari tagu ǝnga njir dlǝ nda, ndǝ hari lǝgutǝ liyangǝ kǝra dǝdǝzǝu, ǝnga kǝra ǝnggǝr zaragina, ǝnga tsu kǝra nǝnanǝna. Kalar tagu kau, ǝnga kǝra ja ǝnggǝr nǝ lǝvari, ǝnga sara wu miya nda ngǝ uˈu wu biya ǝnga ˈyar ǝnga uˈu pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni.
REV 9:18 Ənga sǝr kuɗa nji kǝ makǝr kau, ngǝ cifǝ pathlǝu wu makǝr nǝ ndapi kǝra aˈyi wu duniya ngǝ kuɗǝr nda sara ara, nanda ngǝ uˈu ǝnga ˈyar ba ǝnga uˈu pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni kǝra wu biya sara wu miya nda.
REV 9:19 Dǝnama nǝ taguˈyar kau wu miya nda nga nyi ǝnga wu shiˈwa nda. Shiˈwa nda ǝnggǝr nǝ pabǝˈyar, kǝra ǝnga kǝr kǝra ndu lǝ ɓwaɓwatǝ anǝ nji ǝni.
REV 9:20 Alenyi ndapi kǝra hiyau ara tau sara ara sǝr dlǝ nji ta, kǝ ndǝ nggǝl ara tubi ara sǝr mǝla nda. Nanda aˈyi piyari dlǝvǝ mambǝl ɗǝmwaˈyi mai, ǝnga katǝ liyangǝ dǝzǝr nda, ǝnga katǝ liyangǝ mbǝl wilwilu ǝnga liyangǝ kyakyaru, ba sara wu tsǝka ǝnga wu mai. Nanda ngǝ katǝˈyar kǝra gǝra sǝn lar sau, ǝnga nggari ba gǝra sǝn ɓau.
REV 9:21 Nanda tsu aˈyi tubi ara tsa ndǝ mai ǝnga sǝm dǝshakur ba mǝl sǝsukur ǝnga hǝl sǝ ndǝ mai.
REV 10:1 Kǝ yi ɓǝra lari vanyi madiya waladi a vǝr shida sara dǝmǝlmau, kǝra dlama zǝwar nyi, ǝnga shamba adabanga kǝra ja. Bama ja ǝnggǝr pǝci, hiya ja tsu ǝnggǝr shimal uˈu.
REV 10:2 Aˈyi ja ǝnga zǝr lǝkakaɗǝ pǝpǝɗau wu tsa ja kǝra papahau. Kǝ ji fiya hi mazǝma ja a gwar dǝl ǝnga hi matsala ja ar ˈyiˈyi.
REV 10:3 Ji sǝya mala wau kǝra ma gǝ nggari dǝgǝ abǝr nǝ lǝvari. Ənga ǝnggǝra ji wau, ba dlǝɗǝ pamǝpamǝ mǝɗǝfǝ kǝ dlǝwubiya.
REV 10:4 Ənggǝra dlǝɗǝ pamǝpamǝ mǝɗǝfǝ kǝ dlǝwubiya, yu yiwu ya tsǝfǝya, ama ba yi nggari ɗahǝ sara dǝmǝlmǝ a vǝr na, “Ga haɗiya sǝra dlǝɗǝ mǝɗǝfǝ kǝ nana, ga sara tsǝfǝ mai.”
REV 10:5 Kǝ waladi ta yi lari taˈyi a gwar dǝl ǝnga ar ˈyiˈyi ta har tsi mazǝma ja a dǝmǝlmau.
REV 10:6 Ba ji sǝmku fǝla ǝnga thlǝmǝr ndǝra aˈyi baˈanuwa, ndǝra mǝliya dǝmǝlmau ǝnga sǝra a gwa patǝu, ǝnga duniya ǝnga sǝra a gwa patǝu, ǝnga dǝl ǝnga sǝra a gwa patǝu, ji na, “Tsu vanyi sana pǝci aˈyi mai.
REV 10:7 Ama ar pǝci kǝra waladi nǝ mǝɗǝfǝkura nyi wu nda mbǝɗǝ tǝlǝmǝ tugu nyi, sǝra aˈyi ɗǝɗǝwa nǝ Hyal wu nda nyabiya dzau ar babal, ǝnggǝr kǝra ji nana, anǝ njir mǝl thlǝr nyi, nabiˈyar.”
REV 10:8 Kǝ ɗahǝ ta yi saya nggar ta, sara dǝmǝlmǝ ta, ɓǝra ndǝr anǝ ɗa wayu, ji na, “Maˈyi, ga gwa hǝri zǝr lǝkakaɗǝ papahǝ ta, kǝra wu tsa waladi ta, kǝra aˈyi taˈyi a gwar dǝl ǝnga ar ˈyiˈyi.”
REV 10:9 Tǝma, kǝ yi maˈyi a ndǝgya waladiya nyi, yi nda yiwa aga ja nǝ ɗa zǝr lǝkakaɗa nyi. Əngwar ja anǝ ɗa, “Hǝri ba ga ɗǝhu. Ju nda shabiya ta gau ja ɗa ɗǝwatǝu, ama wu miya gau wu nda ɗa nǝnǝmǝu ǝnggǝr ciɗi.”
REV 10:10 Kǝ yi dlǝwuri zǝr lǝkakaɗa nyi, sara wu tsa waladiya nyi, ba yi ɗǝhu. Ta yi fuwa a du miya yau ba ji ɗa nǝnǝmǝu wu miya yau ǝnggǝr ciɗi, ama ta yi tasǝya ba ji ɗa ɗǝwatǝu a gyu ta yau.
REV 10:11 Kǝ nji nar ɗa, “Kǝl ya ɓǝra habiya ndǝr ar kǝra nji pamǝpamǝ gangǝu, ǝnga ˈyiˈyi ˈyiˈyi pamǝpamǝ ǝnga miya pamǝpamǝ ba ǝnga tǝl tǝl pampamǝu.”
REV 11:1 Nji nǝ ɗa zǝwa tǝkǝ sau, kǝ nji na anǝ ɗa, “Maˈyi ga nda tǝkǝri ki Hyal ǝnga bagadi nyi, ba ga dzǝgwa jigabiya njir dlǝvǝ kǝra a gwa gwa.
REV 11:2 Ama ga sara tǝkǝ vi kǝra a biyar ya ki Hyal mai, ga piyari, arya a nǝ nyir nji anǝ njira gǝra sǝn Hyal. Ndu nda lǝr ɓwaɓwatǝ anǝ mǝlmǝ cici nǝ Hyal nǝ hya foɗǝ kumunyi apǝ mǝthlǝu.
REV 11:3 Yu nda sǝwa sakida ɗaˈyar mǝthlǝu, njira har lǝgutǝ sǝˈyinggu, yu nda nǝ nda dǝnama nǝ habiya ndǝr nǝ pida dubu pathlǝu ǝnga gharu mǝthlǝu ǝnga kwakumunyi, ca ngǝ (1,260).”
REV 11:4 Najaka njir lǝ sakida, nanda wur zaitunu mǝthlǝu ǝnga sǝr sǝɓǝ pitǝlla mǝthlǝu kǝra a vǝr taˈyi wu mwar Thlagǝr duniya.
REV 11:5 Kalar ndǝra wu yiwu ja nǝ nda ɓwaɓwatǝu, ba uˈu a biya sara wu miya nda ba ja sana dawar nda ˈyar. Abangǝ tsu ngǝ kalar ndǝra wu yiwu ja nǝ nda ɓwaɓwatǝ wu nda tau.
REV 11:6 Nji kǝ aˈyi nda ǝnga dǝnama nǝ haɗǝ dǝmǝlmau ara par a sara tǝɗau ar pǝci kǝra nda vǝr habiya ndǝr Hyal. Aˈyi nda ǝnga dǝnama nǝ shabiya ˈyimi aga ja sha aga mashi ba aga nda lǝr uˈu ar dza mǝlmǝ pamǝpamǝ gangǝu ar kalar pǝci kǝra ndu yiwu.
REV 11:7 Ayukuɗa ndǝ kuɗana lǝ sakidar nda, ba sǝr tagǝ kǝra biya sara wu kaˈu kǝra nji gǝra sǝn tǝkǝna ta, ka sa pana nda. Ba ja sǝmku tǝlkur ar kǝra nda, ǝnga ja tsǝya nda.
REV 11:8 Nju nda piyari tǝtǝkura nda ar babal wu huɗa mǝlmǝ kǝra nji dlakǝya Thlagǝr nda a gwa. Nju gǝla najaka mǝlmǝ ǝnga Sodomu ba Masaru.
REV 11:9 Nǝ pida makǝr ǝnga reta ngǝ nji sara wu kalar culi ǝnga miya ba ǝnga ˈyiˈyi wu nda tsamǝ dza nji tǝta nyi ama nandǝ wu piyari nja haɗǝna nda mai.
REV 11:10 Njira vǝr nggya wu duniya wu nda gu caguli ara tǝr sakidaˈyar kǝ mǝthlǝu kau. Ndu nda lǝ sǝ wu pamǝ ara caguli, arya sakidaˈyar kǝ mǝthlǝ kau, a lǝri nda ɓwaɓwatǝ gagaɗau anǝ njira wu nggya wu duniya.
REV 11:11 Ama ayukuɗa pida makǝr ǝnga reta, kǝ sǝpi nǝ lǝ pi shida sara ara Hyal, ba ji sa gwu nda, ba ndǝ hyaˈari ar hiya nda, kǝ ndǝ ɓǝra ɗa aˈyi ǝnga pi. Kǝ hivǝr mbar njira lar nda.
REV 11:12 Kǝ sakidaˈyar kǝ mǝthlǝ kǝ nggari ɗahǝ dǝdǝgal sara dǝmǝlmǝ wu na, “Shida mǝ ǝnggau!” Kǝ ndǝ maˈyi a dǝmǝlmǝ wu dlama, wu liya dawar nda ndu tsamǝ nda.
REV 11:13 Ar pǝci kau, kǝ kǝnggǝɗǝ nǝ ˈyiˈyi gagaɗǝ ɗarkǝr, kǝ cifǝ pathlǝu nǝ kumo wu pama mǝlmǝ kǝ dlanakǝr. Nji dubu mǝɗǝfau ngǝ kuɗau arya kǝnggǝɗǝr ˈyiˈyi kau, ba hivǝr mbar njira hyi mbǝmbǝɗau, ba ndǝ dzǝgwa fal Hyal kǝra a dǝmǝlmau.
REV 11:14 Sǝr tǝhuɗǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi a tǝrabiyari, kǝja sǝr tǝhuɗǝ nǝ makǝrkura nyi a vǝr shili ǝnga kusa.
REV 11:15 Kǝ waladi nǝ mǝɗǝfǝkura nyi mbiɗiya tǝlǝmǝ tugu nyi. Kǝ nji nggar ɗahǝ dǝdǝgal sara dǝmǝlmau, a vǝr na, “Tǝlkur nǝ duniya a ɗari tǝlkur nǝ Thlagǝr mǝn ǝnga nǝ Kǝrsiti nyi, ǝnga ju nda sǝm tǝlkur nyi baˈanuwa.”
REV 11:16 Kǝ njira nggurǝm mǝthlǝkumunyi apǝ foɗǝu, kǝra a vǝr nggya ar tsǝkafǝr nda a dumwar Hyal, ndǝ dla ar bama nda a gyu mwar Hyal, ndu dlǝvǝ nyi,
REV 11:17 ndu na, “ˈYu usa ngau, Hyal Thlagǝu, ndǝ dǝgal dǝnama, ndǝra aˈyi ǝnga ndǝra saya ɗa, arya a hǝri gau dǝnama ngau kǝra dǝgalǝu, ba gǝ dzǝguya sǝm tǝlkur ngau.
REV 11:18 Huɗa njir duniya a ndzǝri, ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ ngau a shiliri. Pǝci a shiliri aga ga sa mǝl numa anǝ nji tǝtau, ǝnga ba ga dzǝgwa lǝr akkǝri anǝ njir mǝl thlǝr ngau, nabiˈyar, ǝnga nji cici gǝ Hyal, ba njira vǝr gǝnggǝr sǝli anǝ thlǝmǝ ngau, nji yiɗǝɗǝu ǝnga nji nggunggurǝm. Pǝci a shiliri aga ga dlǝna njira dlǝna duniya.”
REV 11:19 Kǝ ki Hyal a dǝmǝlmǝ pahǝna dzau, a gwu ki Hyal kau, ba nji lar akwati alkawal mbamba nyi. Kǝ mbǝmbǝl sǝm par daɓǝ ǝnga dǝraghi par, ba dlǝɗǝ par ǝnga kǝnggǝɗǝr ˈyiˈyi ba madiya mǝtǝndili.
REV 12:1 Kǝ nji lari vanyi madiya mǝtsamǝ a dǝmǝlmau, vanyi mala nji haɗiya nyi ǝnga pǝci, ǝnga hya a gyi gya kiɗa hiya ja ǝnga dara tǝlkur nǝ shashilga kumou apǝ mǝthlǝu wu kǝra ja.
REV 12:2 Mala kau ǝnga huɗǝ nga ja, ja vǝr wau nǝ ya ara ar tsǝkar ya nga ja.
REV 12:3 Kǝ vanyi mǝtsamǝ ɓǝra cabiya dzau a dǝmǝlmau, vanyi pabǝr vuwa, kǝra dǝzǝu ǝnga kǝr mǝɗǝfau ba tǝlǝmǝ kumou ǝnga dara tǝlkur mǝɗǝfau wu kǝra ja.
REV 12:4 Kǝ shiˈwa ja tsǝkǝna cifǝ pathlǝu wu makǝr nǝ shashilga kǝra a dǝmǝlmau, a gyiwu ˈyi. Kǝ pabǝr vuwa ta taˈyi wu mwar mala huɗǝ kau, aga ja tasǝya zǝr nyi kau, ma ja yari.
REV 12:5 Kǝ mala kǝ yabiya zǝr nyi, zǝr sal, naja ngu nda sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra njir duniya patǝ ǝnga zǝwa liyangǝu. Ama kǝ nji tsǝr zǝr nyi kau a dǝmǝlmau a dǝgya Hyal a dar tsǝkafǝ nyi.
REV 12:6 Kǝ mala kǝ hwinakǝr a ndar tagǝ mashi, vira Hyal pabǝri nyi, vira nju nda nggya ǝnga ja nju ɓǝla nyi nǝ pida 1,260.
REV 12:7 Kǝ pa hyaˈari a dǝmǝlmau. Mayikalu ǝnga waladi nyiˈyar pana pa ǝnga pabǝr vuwa ta, kǝ pabǝr vuwa ǝnga waladi nyiˈyar pa ǝnga nda tsu.
REV 12:8 Ama kǝ ˈyi pabǝr vuwa aˈyi nda ǝnga dǝnama mai, kǝ nji sǝmku tǝlkur ar kǝra nda, tǝma, ba ndǝ tini vir nggyar nda a dǝmǝlmau.
REV 12:9 Kǝ nji vakana pabǝr vuwa ta a gyiwu ˈyi, naja ngǝ pabǝ ɗǝɗǝmǝ kǝra nju ngga ǝnga tǝl shatan, ba ǝnga Shatan, ndǝra nggutana duniya patǝu. Nji vakana nyi a shida wu ˈyi ǝnga waladi nyiˈyar.
REV 12:10 Kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ fwangǝ gagaɗau sara dǝmǝlmau, “Kabangǝkau mbǝɗau ǝnga dǝnama ǝnga tǝlkur nǝ Hyalǝr mǝn a shidari, ǝnga dǝnama tǝlkur nǝ Kǝrsiti nyi. Ara ndǝr cuɗau a miya ndǝla zamǝr mǝn ˈyar, ndǝra wu cuɗǝ ar kǝra nda wu mwar Hyalǝr mǝn vuˈyi ǝnga puci, a vakana nyir nji a gyiwu ˈyi.
REV 12:11 Ndǝ ndiya dǝnama nyi ǝnga mashi Zǝr Gamǝ ba ǝnga ndǝr sakida kǝra wu biya sara wu miya nda, nanda aˈyi yiwu piya nda gagaɗǝ mai nanda aˈyi hwi ara tǝ mai.
REV 12:12 Agabangau, hya caguli nahyi kǝra a dǝmǝlmau ǝnga nahyi njira wu nggya a dǝna! Ama sǝr tǝhuɗǝu anǝ ˈyiˈyi ǝnga dǝl, arya shatan a gyar ja a gya ara hyi! Nyinyi nga ja ǝnga ɗǝfu arya ju sǝni abǝr pǝci nyi gusǝ nga nyi.”
REV 12:13 Ta pabǝr vuwa ta lari abǝr a vakuwa nyir nji a shida wu duniya, tǝma kǝ ji kǝdlǝ mala ta yabiya zǝr sal ta.
REV 12:14 Kǝ nji nǝ nyi ɓǝgǝ mǝthlǝu nǝ madiya mbǝmbǝlǝmǝ anǝ mala nyi, aga ja mau a dar vira nji pabǝr nyi a gwar tagǝ mashi, vira nju nda ɓǝla nyi ari nǝ pǝci ǝnga pǝciˈyar ba ǝnga reta pǝci, ara pabǝ ta a sara tsǝkwar nyi.
REV 12:15 Sara vu miya pabǝr vuwa ta ngǝ ˈyimi wu biya ǝnggǝr nǝ dǝl, aga ja hǝr mala kau ǝnga dǝnama aga ja maˈyi ǝnga ja.
REV 12:16 Ama kǝ ˈyiˈyi dlǝwar mala kau, lagur pahǝna miya ja tǝma, ba ji tasǝya dǝl kǝra biya sara wu miya pabǝr vuwa ta.
REV 12:17 Kǝ pabǝr vuwa ta nyabiya dzǝ ǝnga ɗǝfu ar kǝra mala kau, ba ji maˈyi, ji nda dzǝgwa pa ǝnga alenyi culi mala kǝ patǝu, njira wu ɓǝlari dlaɗǝ nǝ Hyal, ǝnga ndǝ sǝɓiya sakida nǝ Yesu ǝnga jiri.
REV 12:18 Ənggau kǝ pabǝr vuwa ta taˈyi ar mǝshiˈwa nǝ miya dǝla nyi.
REV 13:1 Kǝ yi lari sǝr tagǝu a vǝr biya sara wu dǝl. Sǝr tagǝ kau aˈyi ja ǝnga tǝlǝmǝ kumou, ba ǝtsu ǝnga kǝr mǝɗǝfau. Aˈyi ja ǝnga dara tǝlkur kumou ar tǝlǝma nyiˈyar, ǝnga ar kalar kǝr, sǝr diɗa thlǝmǝr Hyal aˈyi ari.
REV 13:2 Sǝr tagǝ kǝra yi lari kau, wu pa ufwa wula, ama aˈyi ja ǝnga hi ǝnggǝr nǝ cimjigǝl, ǝnga miya tsu ǝnggǝr miya lǝvari. Pabǝr vuwa ta nǝ nyi dǝnama nyi, ǝnga tsǝkafǝ nyi ba ǝnga dǝnama nǝ tǝlkur nyi.
REV 13:3 Pathlǝu wu pama kǝra sǝr tagǝ ta ɗa ǝnggǝr ji uya mbǝlgǝ nǝ tau, ama mbǝlgǝ nǝ tǝ kau, ba shilǝgǝbiya dzau. Kǝ sǝkǝ ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ duniya patǝ ba ndǝ dzǝgwa nu sǝr tagǝ ta.
REV 13:4 Nju gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli anǝ pabǝr vuwa ta, arya ji nǝ nyi dǝnama anǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, ǝnga nji tsu ndǝ gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli anǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, ndu yiwa ndu na, “Wa ngǝ ǝnggǝr sǝr tagǝ ka? Wa nga sǝn pa ǝnga ja?”
REV 13:5 Nji nǝ nyi miya anǝ sǝr tagǝu, aga ndǝr nǝ ɓwadzau ǝnga ndǝr nǝ diɗa Hyal, ǝnga nji piyari nyi ja ca dǝnama nyi nǝ hya foɗǝ kumunyi apǝ mǝthlǝu.
REV 13:6 Kǝ ji pahǝna miya ja aga diɗa Hyal, ju diɗa thlǝmǝr Hyal ǝnga vir nggya Hyal ǝnga njira vǝr nggya a dǝmǝlmau.
REV 13:7 Nji nǝ nyi dǝnama nǝ pa nji cici gǝ Hyal ǝnga ja sǝmku tǝlkur ar kǝra nda. Kǝ nji nǝ nyi dǝnama ar kǝra kalar culi, ǝnga nji, ǝnga miya ba ˈyiˈyi pampamǝu.
REV 13:8 Patǝr njira wu duniya wu gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli anǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, kǝl njira thlǝmǝr nda aˈyi tsǝtsǝfau divira duniya a dzǝguya dzau wu lǝkakaɗǝ pi nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ kǝra nji thlana.
REV 13:9 Ndǝra ǝnga himi ngga bǝgǝ ja nggari.
REV 13:10 Ma ndǝra wu kyaga ɗa mafa, mafakur nga ju nggya. Ma ndǝra nju kyaga tsǝya nyi ǝnga katsakǝr, ǝnga katsakǝr nga ju tau. Culi sǝˈyar kau, wu yiwu nji cici gǝ Hyal nda nggya ǝnga sǝsu sau ba ǝnga mbǝrsa.
REV 13:11 Kǝ yi ɓǝra lari vanyi sǝr tagǝu kǝra biya sara wu ˈyiˈyi. Aˈyi ja ǝnga tǝlǝmǝ mǝthlǝu ǝnggǝr nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ, ama ju ndǝr ǝnggǝr nǝ pabǝr vuwa ta.
REV 13:12 Ji mǝl thlǝr ǝnga patǝr dǝnama nǝ tǝlkur nǝ sǝr tagǝ tanggǝrma ta anǝ nyi. Ənga ji mǝliya duniya ǝnga njira a gwa gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli anǝ sǝr tagǝ nǝ tanggǝrma ta, kǝra mbǝlgǝ nǝ tǝ nyi ta a shilǝgǝbiyar dzau.
REV 13:13 Ji mǝliya madiya mǝtsamǝ gangǝu, kǝlta ji mǝliya uˈu a shida sara a dǝmǝlmau wu liya nji patǝu.
REV 13:14 Arya dǝnama kǝra nji nǝ nyi aga mǝl mǝtsamǝ nǝ sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝra ji mǝliya ar viya sǝr tagǝ nǝ tanggǝrma ta, ba ji nggutana njira wu duniya. Ji ciwa nda aga nda hǝriya sǝra a papa sǝr tagǝ ta nji uya nyi ǝnga mbǝlgǝ nǝ katsakǝr ama naja aˈyi tǝ mai ta aga nda gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli.
REV 13:15 Nji nǝ nyi dǝnama nǝ lǝ sǝpi anǝ sǝra nji hǝriya kǝra a papa sǝr tagǝ nǝ tanggǝrma ta, aga ja sǝn ndǝr, ǝnga ja tsǝya patǝr njira nggǝl ara gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli.
REV 13:16 Naja tsu kǝ ji ciwa kalar ndau, ndǝ kushu ǝnga ndǝ dǝgalǝu, ndǝr gǝnna ǝnga ndǝra gǝra gǝnna, kambau ǝnga mafa, aga nda dlǝwuri mǝtsamǝ kau ar pǝl mazǝma nda ma aˈyi mai ar huɗǝma nda.
REV 13:17 Ji mǝl abangau ara ndǝ a sara ɗǝlbiya ǝnga ɗǝlna sau, kǝl ndǝra ǝnga mǝtsamǝ kau, ca ngǝ ndaliya thlǝmǝr sǝr tagǝ kau, ǝnga lamba nǝ thlǝmǝ nyi.
REV 13:18 Sǝ kau wu yiwu hahangǝkur. Ma ndǝ aˈyi ǝnga sǝnbiya, bǝgǝ ja jigabiya lamba sǝr tagǝ kau, ara lamba nǝ ndapi ngau, lamba kau, ca ngǝ 666.
REV 14:1 Ta yi tsamau, ba yi lari Zǝr Gamǝ taˈyi ar mǝ nǝ Sǝhiyona. Ənga ja, nji aˈyi, nji duburam gharu ǝnga duburam foɗǝ kumunyi apǝ foɗǝu (144,000) kǝra ǝnga thlǝmǝ nyi ǝnga thlǝmǝr dǝnyi tsǝtsǝfau ar huɗǝma nda.
REV 14:2 Kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ sara dǝmǝlmau ǝnggǝr huhwir ˈyimi ǝnga dlǝɗǝr par. Ɗaha nyi a papa ɗaha sǝmbǝl.
REV 14:3 Nda vǝr thlǝ na mafǝliyangǝu a dumwar tsǝkafǝ Hyal ǝnga a dumwar sǝ ǝnga pi foɗǝ kau ba ǝnga njira nggurǝm mǝthlǝkumunyi apǝ foɗǝ ta. Ndǝ aˈyi kǝra wu sǝn highiɓǝri thlǝ na kǝ mai, kǝl nji 144,000 kau, kǝra Zǝr Gamǝ bǝliya nda sara wu tsa duniya.
REV 14:4 Nji ngau kǝra gǝra diyaɓǝna dza nda ǝnga zawarkur, ndǝ nggya wu cicikur. Ndu nu Zǝr Gamǝ kalar vira ji maˈyi a ndari. A bǝliya ndar nji, nanda ngǝ ɗaramwa kǝra nju lǝ anǝ Hyal ǝnga nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ.
REV 14:5 Fati aˈyi wu miya nda mai, ǝnga nanda aˈyi vavazǝ mai.
REV 14:6 Kǝ yi ɓǝra lari vanyi waladi a vǝr mau a dǝmǝlmau. Aˈyi ja ǝnga ndǝshigu nǝ baˈanuwa kǝra ju nda pǝzau anǝ njira wu duniya. (Nanda ngǝ culi pampamǝu, ǝnga miya pampamǝu ǝnga nji pampamǝu.)
REV 14:7 Ji na ǝnga ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu, “Hya hivǝr Hyal ǝnga hya gǝnggǝr nyi sǝli, arya pǝcir mǝl numa nyi a ɗari. Dlǝvǝ nya mau ndǝra mǝliya dǝmǝlmau, ǝnga gyiwu ˈyi, ǝnga tsadu ba ǝnga mandǝli.”
REV 14:8 Waladi nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi nu nyi, ji sa na, “A dla ja! Madiya Babilanu a dlari, kǝra mǝliya njir duniya nyabiya dzau wu sǝsukur nyi ǝnggǝr nyi padlau.”
REV 14:9 Waladi nǝ makǝrkura nyi nu nda, kǝ ji na, ǝnga ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu, “Ma njira dlǝvǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, ǝnga sǝ a papa nyi kau, alaga njira dlǝwuri mǝtsamǝ nyi ar huɗǝma nda, ǝnga alaga ar tsa nda,
REV 14:10 ju nda tǝwari ˈyimir wur inabi nǝ huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal, kǝra nyinyau wu kyakiwa nǝ huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal kǝra ǝzaˈu. Nju nda nǝ nda ɓwaɓwatǝ nǝ uˈur kǝtsa kǝra pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni a dumwar waladi cici ˈyar ǝnga Zǝr Gamǝu.
REV 14:11 ˈYar nǝ uˈu ɓwaɓwatǝr nda kau, hyaˈari a dǝmǝlmǝ baˈanuwa. Ɓǝlsar aˈyi ara njira wu dlǝvǝ sǝr tagǝ ǝnga sǝ kǝra wu pa nyi vuˈyi ǝnga pǝci mai, alaga njira dlǝwuri mǝtsamǝ nǝ thlǝmǝr sǝr tagǝ kau.”
REV 14:12 Sǝ kau, a cabiyari abǝr nji cici gǝ Hyal, njira wu ɓǝlar ndǝr Hyal ǝnga jirkur wu Yesu kǝl nda nggya ǝnga mba ɗǝfu.
REV 14:13 Kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ sara dǝ mǝlmau a vǝr na, “Tsǝfǝya, barka anǝ njira tǝ wu Thlagǝu, mbar kabangǝkau.” Əngwar Mambǝl Hyal, “Pakatǝu, a nggyar nda njir barka, arya ndu nda uya ɓǝlsar sara wu thlǝr kwakwaɗǝkur nda, ara sǝr mǝla nda kǝra mǝnahǝu wu nu nda.”
REV 14:14 Ta yi tsamau, tǝma, kǝ yi lari a dumwa ɗa dlama pǝrtǝu, a du dlama kau, vanyi ndǝ aˈyi kǝra vir nggya “A papa Zǝr Ndau” ǝnga dora tǝlkur nǝ ǝndzǝ wu kǝra ja ba mǝkalǝ sǝsǝm wu tsa ja.
REV 14:15 Kǝ vanyi waladi shida sara vu ki Hyal, ji sa ngga ndǝra aˈyi nggya wu dlama kau ǝnga ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu, “Hǝri mǝkalǝ ngau, ga faˈa sǝ ǝni, arya pǝcir faˈa sǝ asi a ɗari, ara sǝr duniya a nǝri.”
REV 14:16 Ndǝra aˈyi nggya a du dlama kau, kǝ ji sǝr mǝkalǝ nyi a shida wu duniya, kǝ ji kwafǝri sǝ ǝni a di.
REV 14:17 Kǝ vanyi waladi ɓǝra biya tsu sara du ki Hyal kǝra dǝmǝlmau, ǝnga vanyi mǝkalǝ sǝsǝmau, wu tsa ja.
REV 14:18 Vanyi waladi tsu kǝra dǝgala gǝra uˈu biya sara dar bagadi, kǝ ji ngga ǝnga ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu, ndǝra ǝnga mǝkalǝ sǝsǝm ara ja kau, “Hǝri mǝkalǝ sǝsǝm ngǝ kau, ga sǝri ga kwafǝya yayar wu kǝra dar wuˈyar kǝra wu duniya patǝu, arya a nǝr nda.”
REV 14:19 Kǝ waladi ta sǝwa mǝkalǝ nyi a shida wu duniya, kǝ ji kwafǝya kalar yayar wur inabi ˈyar nǝ duniya, kǝ ji tsǝmiya nda a gwu vir ɓǝci yayar wur inabi nǝ huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal
REV 14:20 Nji ghighiraɓǝna yayar wa nyi a biyar ya mǝlmau, a biyar vir ɓǝci yayar wur inabi, kǝ mashi biya sara wu nda, wu dzǝgwa ndǝɗǝ dzau a gwar tagǝu, dzǝgamkura nyi pa kǝra tagu, ǝnga tugukura nyi tsu melu gharu ǝnga cisu kumunyi (180).
REV 15:1 Kǝ yi lari vanyi madiya mǝtsamǝ a dǝmǝlmau. Mǝtsamǝ kau, ca ngǝ waladi mǝɗǝfau ǝnga ɓwaɓwatǝ mǝɗǝfau. Ɓwaɓwatǝ kau, ca ngǝ nǝ jomǝ ndǝl, arya ǝnga nda nga nju nda nyabiya huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal.
REV 15:2 Tǝma, kǝ yi lari vanyi sǝ a papa tsadau kǝra wu pa dǝl kwalaba dadaɓǝ ǝnga uˈu. Tataˈyi a biyar ya tsadǝ kau, ngǝ njira sǝmku tǝlkur ar kǝra sǝr tagǝ ta, ba sǝr papa nyi ba ǝnga lamba thlǝmǝ nyi. Ndǝ sǝɓiya sǝmbǝl wu tsa nda kǝra Hyal nǝ nda.
REV 15:3 Nda vǝr thlǝ na nǝ Musa, mafa Hyal ǝnga thlǝ na nǝ Zǝr Gamǝu. “Sǝr mǝla gau, dǝdǝgal nga nda gagaɗau ǝnga sǝ dǝdǝgur nga nda, Ya, Hyal Thlagǝu Ndǝ Dǝgal Dǝnama! Tandar ǝnga jiri ngǝ lagu ngau, tǝl nǝ baˈanuwa.
REV 15:4 Wa ngǝ gǝra hivǝr nga, Thlagǝu? Wa ngǝ gǝra dlǝvǝ dǝgalkur nga? Kǝl nagǝ ngǝ ndǝ cicau. Patǝr ndapi wu nda shili, ndu sa dlǝvǝ ngau arya thlǝr tsapǝkur ngau a biyari ar babal.”
REV 15:5 Ayukuɗa sǝˈyar kǝ patǝu, tǝma, yi tsamǝ a dǝmǝlmau, tǝma, kǝ yi lari ki Hyal ca ngǝ kwapatǝ nǝ sakida, papahau.
REV 15:6 Sara vu ki Hyal kau, ngǝ waladi mǝɗǝfǝ ǝnga ɓwaɓwatǝ mǝɗǝfǝ kǝ biya. Ndǝ hari kar lilinu kǝra wu mbǝl wilwilǝu, ǝnga ndǝ thlaˈubiya hathla nda ǝnga takulagǝ ǝndzǝ dlaɓǝu.
REV 15:7 Pathlǝ wu pama sǝ ǝnga pi foɗǝ ta, nǝ nyi anǝ waladi mǝɗǝfǝ ta ǝgwa ǝndzǝ mǝɗǝfǝ kǝra nyinyi ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal ndǝra aˈyi ja baˈanuwa.
REV 15:8 Ki Hyal kau, nyinyi nga nyi ǝnga ˈyar kǝra shida sara du kadakadarkur nǝ Hyal ǝnga dǝnama nyi. Ndǝ aˈyi kǝra wu sǝn gwu ki Hyal kǝ mai, kǝl ma ɓwaɓwatǝ waladi mǝɗǝfǝ kǝ jomǝya dzau.
REV 16:1 Tǝma, kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝ sara wu ki Hyal kǝra a vǝr na anǝ waladi mǝɗǝfǝ ˈyar kau, “Maˈya mau, hya biya pǝna ǝgwa huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ Hyal mǝɗǝfǝ kau, a gyu duniya.”
REV 16:2 Kǝ waladi nǝ tanggǝrma kǝ biya, kǝ ji biya pǝna nǝ nya ǝgwa a gyu duniya. Kǝ mbǝlgǝ pǝziya dzǝ ar dza njira ǝnga mǝtsamǝ nǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, ǝnga nda vǝr dlǝvǝ sǝra a papa nyi.
REV 16:3 Minu nyi, tǝma waladi nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi shabiya ǝgwa nyi a gwar tsadau, tǝma ˈyimi kǝra a gwa sha aga mashi ndǝ tǝtau, ba sǝra a gwagwa kuɗǝ patǝu.
REV 16:4 Kǝ nǝ makǝrkura nyi tsu biya, kǝ ji biya shabiya nǝ nya ǝgwa a gu dǝlˈyar ǝnga mandǝliˈyar, kǝ ˈyimi kǝra a gwa sha aga mashi.
REV 16:5 Kǝ yi nggari waladi kǝra ǝnga dǝnama ar kǝra ˈyimi a vǝr na, “Tsatsaˈa ngǝ numa gau, Nagǝ ndǝ cicau, ndǝra saya ɗa, naja ngǝ ǝshina,
REV 16:6 Arya nja nyi a pǝnar nda mashi, mashi nji cici gǝ Hyal ǝnga mashi nabiˈyar. Kǝja ga nǝ ndari mashi aga nda sa, akkǝra nyi ngǝ kǝja.”
REV 16:7 Kǝ yi nggari ɗahǝu sara dar bagadiya nyi, a vǝr na, “Hyal Thlagǝu, ndǝ dǝgal dǝnama! Numa ngau, jijiri ǝnga tsatsaˈa nga nyi.”
REV 16:8 Kǝ waladi nǝ foɗǝkura nyi pǝna ǝgwa nyi a dar pǝci, kǝ ji cakǝr nyi dǝnama nǝ titiˈwa nji ǝnga uˈur pǝci.
REV 16:9 Ndǝ titiˈwanakǝr arya kwakwaɗǝkura pǝca nyi, ba ndǝ gu diɗa thlǝmǝr Hyal, ndǝra ǝnga dǝnama ar kǝra ɓwaɓwatǝˈyar kǝ patǝu, ama kǝ ndǝ nggǝl ara tubi ǝnga fal Hyal.
REV 16:10 Waladi nǝ tǝfukura nyi pǝna nǝ nya ǝgwa a dar tsǝkafǝ nǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, tǝma, kǝ tǝlkur nyi haɗiya dzǝ ǝnga kuthlǝu. Nji tsu nda vǝr ɗǝ hira nda ara ɓwaɓwatǝu.
REV 16:11 Ndǝ dumwa ǝnga diɗa Hyal arya ɓwaɓwatǝ kǝra nda a gwa ǝnga shilǝgǝ kǝra ar dza nda, ama kǝ ndǝ nggǝl ara tubi.
REV 16:12 Waladi nǝ kwakura nyi shabiya sǝra a gu ǝgwa nyi a gwu dǝl dǝgal Yifǝratǝsu, tǝma, kǝ ˈyimi kǝra a gwa shiˈwau, aga tǝlˈya r sara dǝ wu sǝbiyar pǝci uya lagur shida.
REV 16:13 Kǝ yi lari mambǝl ɗǝmwaˈyiˈyar makǝr kǝra a papa bwanja, biya sara wu miya pabǝr vuwa kau, ǝnga sara wu miya sǝr tagǝ kau, ba ǝnga sara wu miya nabi fati.
REV 16:14 Nanda mambǝl ɗǝmwaˈyiˈyar ngau, kǝra a vǝr mǝl sǝ dǝdǝgur. Nda vǝr biya aga nda maˈyi a ndǝra tǝltǝlˈyar nǝ patǝr duniya, aga nda tsǝmiya dzǝ aga sa pa ar pǝci dǝgal nǝ Hyal Dǝgal Dǝnama.
REV 16:15 Hya ɗǝngari sǝra Yesu nana, abǝr, “Kǝja ya vǝr shili ǝnggǝr ndǝr hǝl! Ndǝr barka ngǝ ndǝra pabǝr kǝrnyi ju vǝr sǝkǝ shili ɗa ǝnga ji hari kari nyi camǝu, ara ja sara nggya turusu, nja lari tursukura ja.”
REV 16:16 Tǝma, kǝ ndǝ tsǝmiya tǝl tǝlˈyar kǝ patǝ a shili ar vi zǝmǝu, vira nju ngga ǝnga miya njir Yahudiya Amagidanu.
REV 16:17 Waladi nǝ mǝɗǝfǝkura nyi shabiya sǝra gu ǝgwa nyi a dǝmǝlmau. Kǝ ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu, hyaˈari sara ndar tsǝkafǝ wu ki Hyal ju na, “A ɗari!”
REV 16:18 Kǝ sǝm par ǝnga dǝraghi par ǝnga dlǝɗǝ par ǝnga madiya kǝnggǝɗǝr ˈyiˈyi kǝra gǝra saya ɗa ǝnggǝra ndǝ shili wu duniya. Kǝnggǝɗǝ kau, madiya madiya kǝnggǝɗǝr ˈyiˈyi ngau.
REV 16:19 Najaka madiya mǝlmau, ba ji tǝkǝbiya dzǝ bwata makǝru, kǝ madiya mǝlmǝ nǝ ˈyiˈyi pamǝpamǝ dlanakǝr. Kǝ Hyal ɗǝngari ǝnga Babilanu madiya mǝlmau, ba Hyal nǝ nyi kyakiwa nyinyau ǝnga huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal aga ja sa.
REV 16:20 Kalar dzǝgu dǝl sanakǝr ǝnga kalar mǝˈyar sanakǝr, nji aˈyi ɓǝra lar nda mai.
REV 16:21 Sara dǝmǝlmau, kǝ madiya mǝtǝndili tǝtǝɗau a shidar kǝra nji. Kǝ ndǝ dzǝgwa diɗa Hyal arya ɓwaɓwatǝ nǝ mǝtǝndili kau. Ɓwabwata nyi dzadzau gagaɗau.
REV 17:1 Kǝ pathlǝ wu pama waladi mǝɗǝfǝ kǝra nda ǝnga ǝgwa mǝɗǝfǝ ta, shida ara yau, kǝ ji nar ɗa, “A ndau, aga ya sa canǝ ngǝ ɓwaɓwatǝ kǝra nju nda lǝri anǝ madiya zawar kǝra a vǝr nggya ar kǝra ˈyimi kǝra gangǝu.
REV 17:2 Naja ngǝ ndǝra tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya mǝl sǝsukur ǝnga ja. Njir duniya patǝ a nyir nda ǝnga sǝsukur nyi ǝnggǝr njira padlǝ wu tsa nda.”
REV 17:3 Kǝ waladi ta hǝr ɗa wu mambǝl a ndar tagǝ mashi, a ndǝna tǝma, kǝ yi lari vanyi mala a vǝr nggya ar sǝr tagǝ dǝzǝu. Sǝr tagǝ kau, aˈyi ja ǝnga thlǝmǝ nǝ diɗa Hyal tsǝtsǝfǝ ar dza ja. Aˈyi ja tsu ǝnga kǝr mǝɗǝfau ǝnga tǝlǝmǝ kumou.
REV 17:4 Mala kǝ hari kar ɗǝdla ɗǝdla ǝnga maggǝdi maggǝdi, ǝnga ji hari ǝndzǝ kǝra wu mbǝl, ǝnga tsǝka dǝdur ba ǝnga handzǝlkwa. Tasau ǝndzǝ ngu tsa ja, nyinyau ǝnga kalar sǝra gǝra cicau ǝnga sǝr mǝl sǝsukur nyi.
REV 17:5 Kǝja thlǝmǝ ɗǝɗǝwa kǝra tsǝtsǝfǝ ar huɗǝma ja: “Babilanu madiya mǝlmau Mǝya zawarˈyar Ənga sǝ zhizhigǝrˈyar nǝ duniya.”
REV 17:6 A lari yi mala kǝ a nyir ja nyi papadlau, ǝnga mashi nji cici gǝ Hyal, mashi njira lǝri sakida ar kǝra Yesu. Ta yi lari nyi ba ɗa sǝr dǝdǝgur anǝ ɗa.
REV 17:7 Kǝ waladi na anǝ ɗa, “Ara mi sǝ kǝ ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ nga? Yu cabiya ngǝ sǝra ar ɗǝwa ar kǝra mala kau, ǝnga sǝr tagǝ kǝra ja vǝr dlǝ kau, kǝra ǝnga kǝr mǝɗǝfau ba ǝnga tǝlǝmǝ kumou.
REV 17:8 Sǝr tagǝ kǝra gǝ lari ta, aˈyi ja ɗǝɗǝmǝu, ama tsu ja aˈyi mai. Ju nda biya sara wu kaˈu kǝra nji gǝra sǝn tǝkǝna ba ja maˈyi a ndar vira nju nda tsǝya nyi ari. Njira vǝr nggya wu duniya, njira gǝra ǝnga thlǝmǝr nda tsǝtsǝfǝ wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ pi, mbari ar dzǝguya duniya wu nda ɗa sǝ dǝdǝgur anǝ nda, ma ndǝ lar sǝr tagǝ kau, kǝra aˈyi ɗǝɗǝm ama tsu ja aˈyi mai ama tsu ju ɓǝra nda sha shili.
REV 17:9 “Sǝ kau, wu gal hahangǝkur, Kǝr mǝɗǝfǝ kau, madzǝgamǝ mǝɗǝfǝ ngau, kǝra mala kǝ a vǝr nggya a dari.
REV 17:10 Nanda tsu ar viya tǝlˈyar mǝɗǝfǝ ngau. Tǝfwa nda a dlanar nda kǝr, tsu pathla nda vǝr sǝm tǝlkur, ǝnga pathla nda tsu ji gǝra shili, ama ma ji nda shili, ju sa sǝm tǝlkur nǝ pǝci kushu.
REV 17:11 Sǝr tagǝ kǝra aˈyi ɗǝɗǝmǝu, ama aˈyi ja tsu mai, naja ngǝ tǝl nǝ cisǝkura nyi. Pathlǝ ja wu pama nda mǝɗǝfǝ kau, ǝnga ja vǝr maˈyi a ndar vira nju nda tsiya nyi ari.
REV 17:12 “Tǝlǝmǝˈyar kǝ kumo kǝ gǝ lari kau, nanda ngǝ tǝlˈyar kumou kǝra gǝra dlǝwuri vir sǝm tǝlkur nda kwatahǝu, ama ndu nda dlǝwuri zǝwa tǝlkur nǝ saka pathlǝ daɓǝ ǝnga sǝr tagǝ kau.
REV 17:13 Tǝlˈyar kau, ɗǝngar nda zǝmǝ nga nyi, dǝnamar nda patǝ ǝnga sǝm tǝlkur nda ndu nda nǝ nyi anǝ sǝr tagǝ kau.
REV 17:14 Ndu nda par pa ǝnga Zǝr Gamǝ kau, ama ba Zǝr Gamǝ kǝ a sǝmkur tǝlkur ar kǝra nda arya naja ngǝ Thlagǝr thlagǝˈyar ǝnga Tǝlǝr tǝlˈyar, ǝnga njira aˈyi ǝkkǝˈyi ja, nanda ngǝ njira nji ngga, ǝnga njira nji caɗǝbiya ǝnga njir nu kǝra ji fǝr kǝr ǝni.”
REV 17:15 Tǝma, kǝ waladi kǝ na anǝ ɗa, “ˈYimi kǝra gǝ lar ta, vira mala zawar ta a vǝr nggya ari ta, nanda ngǝ nji ǝnga dlamir nji ǝnga ˈyiˈyi ˈyiˈyi ˈyar ba ǝnga miya pampamǝu.
REV 17:16 Sǝr tagǝ ǝnga tǝlǝmǝ kumo kǝra gǝ lari ta, ndu nda piyari shishir dza zawar kau. Ndu nda faɗiya kar nyi ba nda piyari nyi turusu. Ndu nda ɗǝhu kumǝr dza ja ba nda nggyina sǝra hyau ǝnga uˈu.
REV 17:17 Arya Hyal nǝ nda ɗǝfu aga nda nyabiya sǝra ju yiwu lagur mǝliya aga nda nǝ nyi dǝnamar nda anǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, aga ja sǝm tǝlkur, kǝl pǝcira ndǝr Hyal wu nda nyabiya dzau.
REV 17:18 Mala ta gǝ lari ta naja ngǝ madiya mǝlmǝ kǝra a vǝr sǝm tǝlkur ar kǝra tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya.”
REV 18:1 Ayukuɗa sǝˈyar kǝ patǝu, ba yi lari vanyi waladi a vǝr shida sara a dǝmǝlmau. Aˈyi ja ǝnga dǝnama nǝ sǝm tǝlkur, ǝnga kadakadarkur nyi a vǝr mbǝl ar kǝra duniya patǝu.
REV 18:2 Ji ngga ǝnga ɗahǝ dǝgalǝu, ji na, “A dlar ja, madiya Babilanu a dlari! A ɗar ja vir nggya anǝ mambǝl ɗǝmwaˈyiˈyar pampamǝu, Ənga vir nggya anǝ kalar mambǝl diyadiyaɓǝˈyar, ǝnga vir nggya anǝ ˈyagǝ dǝgur ǝnga diyadiyaɓǝˈyar, ǝnga vir nggya anǝ kalar sǝr tagǝu, kǝra dǝgur ǝnga diyadiyaɓǝu.
REV 18:3 Ara patǝr ˈyiˈyi ndǝ wathliya dzau wu nggyabiya nǝ sǝsukur nyi. Tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya patǝ a mǝliyar nda sǝsukur ǝnga ja. Njir shafǝli a mǝliyar nda gǝnna wu ja lagur yiwu nggyabiya wawahǝ nyi.”
REV 18:4 Kǝ yi ɓǝra nggari vanyi ɗahǝ sara a dǝmǝlmǝ a vǝr na, “Biya mau, nahyi nji ɗa, sara wu ja! Ara hya sara gu bikǝ nyi ara ɓwaɓwatǝ nyi a sara uya hyi.
REV 18:5 Ara bikǝ nyi a vuyar dzǝ ba a dǝmǝlmau. Kǝ Hyal ɗǝngari ǝnga bikǝ nyi.
REV 18:6 Mǝliya nya mau ǝnggǝr kǝra ji mǝliya. Kibiya nya mau aga mǝthlǝu sǝra ji mǝliya. Wathliya nya mau aga mǝthlǝu kyakiwa ɗǝmwaˈyikur kǝra ji wathliya hyi a gwa.
REV 18:7 Nǝ nya mǝ ɓwaɓwatǝ ǝnga huɗǝ kyakyaru ǝnggǝr kǝra ji hana kǝrnyi ǝnga nggya wawahǝ nyi. Wu ɗǝfuwa ja, ja vǝr ɓwakǝr nyi, ‘Yi wu nggya ǝnggǝr kwatam, aˈyi yi mala tǝsal mai, ǝnga aˈyi yiwu sǝˈyinggu mai.’
REV 18:8 Agabangau, wu pǝci pathlǝu ɓwaɓwatǝ wu nda nyabiya dzau, tau, ǝnga sǝˈyinggu ba wuɓau. Uˈu wu nda nggyina nyi, arya Hyal Thlagǝu ndǝ dǝgal dǝnama ngu sa thlana nyi numa.”
REV 18:9 Ma tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya kǝra mǝl sǝsukur ǝnga nggyabiya wawahǝ nyi ǝnga nda lari ˈyar nǝ uˈu kǝra wu nggyi nyi, ndu nda tiwi ǝnga sǝˈyinggu nyi.
REV 18:10 Maja wu ɓwaɓwatǝu, ndu taˈyi tsalǝu ara ndu hivǝr nja sara daɓǝr nda wu ɓwaɓwatǝ nyi, ǝnga ndu tiwi nyi. “Sǝr tǝhuɗǝu! Sǝr tǝhuɗǝu, madiya mǝlmau, Babilanu, mǝlmǝ kǝra ǝnga dǝnama! Wu saka pathlǝu numa ngau a shiliri!”
REV 18:11 Njir shafǝli nǝ duniya wu nda tiwi ǝnga jiga tiwi arya ja, ara tsu ndǝr nda ɗǝl kar nda aˈyi mai.
REV 18:12 Tsu ndǝr nda ɗǝl ǝndzau, ǝnga thladla ǝnga tsǝka dǝduru ǝnga handzǝlkwa ǝnga yadi lilinu ǝnga yadi ɗǝdla ɗǝdla ǝnga yadi pǝrapǝraɗǝu ba ǝnga kar maggǝdi maggǝdi, patǝ ǝkkǝˈyi alenyi wu la ki ǝnga alenyi sǝ kǝra nji mǝliya sara wu hira ciwar ǝnga wu dǝduru ǝnga liyangǝ shishiˈwu ba alenyi liyangǝ ǝnga tsǝka pǝzi mai.
REV 18:13 Ətsu ndǝr nda ɗǝl kar nǝ sǝ kisǝu ǝnga yaji ǝnga sǝr ɗǝzǝ huɗa umbwa ǝnga ɓurdi dza wu ǝnga ɓurdi dǝdǝgau ǝnga ˈyimir wur inabi ǝnga mal wur zaitunu ǝnga ǝpou ǝnga uhi, ǝnga thla ǝnga tǝmahǝu ǝnga tagu ǝnga keki tagǝu ǝnga mafaˈyar ba ǝnga alenyi nji aˈyi mai.
REV 18:14 Ndu na anǝ nyi, “Kalar sǝ mǝnahǝu, kǝra gu cim a tǝrabiyari, tsu gu ɓǝra uya nda mai. Patǝr bǝrbakur ngau a tǝrabiyari, tsu gu ɓǝra nda uya mai.”
REV 18:15 Njir shafǝli kǝra ɗǝlna nyi sǝˈyar kǝ uya akkǝri a gu bǝrbakur nyi ndu nda taˈyi tsalǝu, ara ndu hivǝr nja sara daɓǝr nda wu ɓwaɓwatǝ nyi. Ndu tiwi ndu sǝˈyinggu,
REV 18:16 ndu wau, ndu na, “‘Sǝr tǝhuɗǝu! Sǝr tǝhuɗǝu, madiya mǝlmau, ndǝra ɗǝɗǝmǝu, a vǝr mba kadǝmbul lilinu ǝnga lǝgutǝ ɗǝdla ɗǝdla ǝnga lǝgutǝ maggǝdi maggǝdi. Ndǝra ɗǝɗǝmǝu, a vǝr ha ǝndzǝ wilwilu ǝnga tsǝka dǝduru ba ǝnga handzǝlkwa.
REV 18:17 Wu saka pathlǝu kalar bǝrbakur nyi kau wu nda sa!’ “Kalar njir dlǝ kwambwal, ǝnga njira wu ɓǝ a gwa, ǝnga njir mǝl thlǝr a gwu nda ǝnga kalar njira vǝr mǝl gǝnnar nda a gwar ˈyimi, ndu nda taˈyi tsatsalǝu.
REV 18:18 Ma ndǝ lari ˈyar uˈu kǝra a vǝr nggyi nyi, ndu sǝya mala wau, “Mǝlmǝ aˈyi saya ɗa dǝgala abangǝ nga nyi ya?”
REV 18:19 Ndu nda tǝwa ˈyiˈyi wu kǝra nda, ndu tiwi ǝnga jiga tiwi, ndu na, “ ‘Sǝr tǝhuɗǝu, madiya mǝlmau, vira njira ǝnga kwambwal ar tsadau, ǝnga ndǝ mǝliya gǝnna lagur bǝrbakur nyi! Wu saka pathlǝu, kǝja nja sana nyi ri!
REV 18:20 Caguli mau ar kǝra ja, dǝmǝlmau! Caguli mau nji cici gǝ Hyal ǝnga cama sǝsǝˈyar ba ǝnga nabiˈyar! Hyal a cabiya nyi ri numa nǝ shishikur nyi kǝra ji mǝl anǝ hyi.’ ”
REV 18:21 Kǝ madiya waladi hǝri vanyi madiya tsǝka kǝra ǝnggǝr bǝra, kǝ ji vakuwa a gwar tsadau, kǝ ji na, “Ənga gwazhi vi ǝnggǝr kau, ngǝ madiya mǝlmǝ Babilanu, nga nju nda vakana nyi a gya, tsu nju ɓǝra lari nyi mai.
REV 18:22 Njir tsa sǝmbǝl ǝkkǝˈyi njir thlǝ na ǝnga njir mbiɗǝ mbǝlaˈwu, ǝnga aligata aˈyi kǝra nju ɓǝra nggari wu gǝ mai. Ndǝ aˈyi kǝra wu ɓǝra mǝl thlǝr tsi kǝra aˈyi nju uya wu gǝ mai. Ɗahǝ nǝ au ar bǝra nju ɓǝra nggari wu gǝ mai.
REV 18:23 Tsu nju ɓǝra lari mbǝmbǝl nǝ pitǝlla wu gǝ mai. Ɗaha sal kwanjili ǝnga kwanjili nju ɓǝra nggari wu gǝ mai. Njir sugu ngau, ca ngǝ nji nggunggurǝm nǝ duniya. Lagur shavi ngau, nga gǝ nggutana ˈyiˈyir duniya.
REV 18:24 A gu ja ngǝ mashi nabiˈyar ǝnga nǝ nji cici gǝ Hyal, ǝnga kalar njira nji tsǝya wu duniya.”
REV 19:1 Ayukuɗa kau, tǝma, kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ a papa ɗaha dlamir nju wau a dǝmǝlmau, a vǝr na, “Fal Hyal! Mbǝɗau ǝnga kadakadarkur ǝnga dǝnama a nggyari anǝ Hyalǝr mǝn,
REV 19:2 arya jiri ǝnga tsatsaˈa ngǝ numa nyi. A thlana nyir ja numa anǝ madiya zawar ta ndǝra diyaɓǝna duniya ǝnga sǝsukur nyi. A kibiyar ja ar ja mashi mafa nyi kǝra nji tsǝya.”
REV 19:3 Wayu kǝ ndǝ ɓǝra wau, ndǝ na, “Fal Hyal! ˈYar kǝra a vǝr biya wu ja vǝr ɗǝzǝ a dǝmǝlmǝ baˈanuwa.”
REV 19:4 Njira nggurǝm mǝthlǝkumunyi apǝ foɗǝu ǝnga sǝ ǝnga pi foɗǝ ta dla a gyu mwar Hyal ndu dlǝvǝ nyi, naja kǝra a vǝr nggya ar tsǝkafǝu. Ndu dzǝgwa tiwi, ndu na, “Amina, Fal Hyal!”
REV 19:5 Kǝ ɗahǝ hyaˈari sara ar tsǝkafǝu, kǝ ji na, “Fal Hyalǝr mǝn, nahyi mafa nyi patǝu, nahyi njira vǝr hivǝr nyi, nji dǝdǝgal ǝkkǝˈyi njira kukushu!”
REV 19:6 Kǝ yi nggar vanyi ɗahǝ a papa ɗaha dlamir nji, ɗahǝ ǝnggǝr dǝl shida shida, ǝnggǝr ɗaha madiya dlǝɗǝr par, a vǝr wau, “Fal Hyal! Arya Hyal Thlagǝr mǝn Ndǝ Dǝgal Dǝnama a vǝr sǝm tǝlkur.
REV 19:7 Taˈyi mǝna caguli mǝna ɗa ǝnga huɗǝ pipida mǝna nǝ nyi kadakadarkur! Arya hǝdzau nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ kau, a shiliri, kwanjili nyi a ɓathlǝri dzau.
REV 19:8 Lilinu mbǝmbǝl camǝ nga nji nǝ nyi aga ja hari.” (Lilinu mbǝmbǝl camǝ ngǝ cabiya sǝr mǝla nji cici gǝ Hyal kǝra tsapǝu.)
REV 19:9 Kǝ waladi kǝ nar ɗa, “Tsǝfǝya, ‘Barka anǝ njira nji nggǝya aga mini hǝdzǝ nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ kau!’ ” Ji ɓǝra cakǝri na, “Najakǝ ngǝ ndǝr Hyal kǝra jijiri.”
REV 19:10 Ta yi nggari abangau, tǝma, kǝ yi dla a gyu huɗǝ nyi, aga ya dlǝvǝ nyi. Ama kǝ ji na anǝ ɗa, “A sara ga mǝl abangǝ mai! Ndǝ nga yi ǝnggǝr nagau, ndǝr mǝl thlǝr kuvwar ngau ba ǝnga zamǝr hyi kǝra lǝri sakida ar kǝra Yesu. Dlǝvǝ Hyal! Arya lǝri sakida ar kǝra Yesu ca ngǝ ndǝrhaha.”
REV 19:11 Kǝ yi lari dǝmǝlmau papahau, ǝnga a dumwa ɗa vanyi tagu pǝrtǝu, kǝra ndǝr dla nyi nju ngga nyi ǝnga Ndǝra nju fǝr kǝr ni ǝnga Ndǝ jijiri. Ənga ju mǝl numa tsatsaˈa ǝnga pa tsatsaˈa.
REV 19:12 Liya ja ǝnggǝr kyara uˈu. A du kǝra ja ngǝ dora nǝ tǝlkur gangǝu. Thlǝmǝ aˈyi kǝra tsǝtsǝfau ar ja, kǝra ndǝ gǝra sǝni kǝl naja.
REV 19:13 Kar kǝra ar dza ja dzǝdzǝgu nga nyi ǝnga mashi. Thlǝmǝ nyi ca ngǝ Ndǝr Hyal.
REV 19:14 Sojaˈyar kǝra a dǝmǝlmau a vǝr nu nyi, ar tagu pǝpǝrtǝu, ǝnga ndǝ hari lilinu pǝrtǝ camǝ mǝnahǝu.
REV 19:15 Sara vu miya ja ngǝ vanyi katsakǝr sǝsǝm wu biya aga dliya duniya nǝ ˈyiˈyi pampamǝu. “Ju sǝm tǝlkur ǝnga zǝwa liyangǝu.” Ju nda ghighiraɓǝna vir ɓǝci ˈyimi wur inabi nǝ huɗǝ ndzǝndzǝ nǝ Hyal, Ndǝ Dǝgal Dǝnama.
REV 19:16 Ar lǝgutǝ nyi ǝnga ar ˈya ja thlǝmǝ aˈyi tsǝtsǝfau: Tǝl nǝ tǝlˈyar ǝnga Thlagǝ nǝ thlagǝˈyar.
REV 19:17 Kǝ yi lari vanyi waladi taˈyi a dar pǝci, ju ngga ǝnga ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝ anǝ kalar ˈyagǝˈyar kǝra a vǝr mau, “Shila mau, hya kaɓiya dzǝ ǝnggau aga madiya sǝm sǝr sǝm nǝ Hyal.
REV 19:18 Hya sa sǝm kumǝr dza tǝlˈyar ǝnga madiya sojaˈyar ǝnga madiya nji ǝnga taguˈyar ǝnga njir dlǝ nda ǝnga kumǝr nji patǝu, mafa ǝnga kambǝr nji, nji dǝdǝgal ǝnga nji kukushu.”
REV 19:19 Kǝ yi lari sǝr tagǝ ta ǝnga tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya ǝnga njir par nda kaɓiya dzǝ aga pa ndǝr dlǝ tagu kau ǝnga soja nyiˈyar.
REV 19:20 Ama kǝ ji mbari sǝr tagǝ kau ǝnga nabi fati kǝra a vǝr mǝl sǝ dǝdǝgur wu thlǝmǝ nyi. Ənga sǝ dǝdǝgur kǝra ji mǝl kau, ǝnga ji nggutana njira dlǝwuri mǝtsamǝ nǝ sǝr tagǝ kau, ǝnga ndǝ dlǝvǝ sǝra a papa nyi. Gyapǝ nda nga nji vakuwa a gu faˈa uˈur kǝtsa kǝra pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni ǝnga pi.
REV 19:21 Alenyi njira hyau, kǝ ndǝr dlǝ tagu kau, tsǝya nda ǝnga katsakǝr kǝra wu biya sara wu miya ja. Patǝr ˈyagǝˈyar kaɓiya dzǝ aga nda sa nyabiya dzau ǝnga kumǝr dza nda.
REV 20:1 Ba yi lari vanyi waladi sara a dǝmǝlmǝ a vǝr shida ǝnga sǝr pahǝ miya kaˈu kǝra nji gǝra sǝn tǝkǝna ǝnga ǝpa nǝ liyangǝ wu tsa ja.
REV 20:2 Kǝ ji mbari pabǝr vuwa ta, naja ngǝ pabǝ ɗǝɗǝmǝ ta, naja ngǝ tǝl nǝ mambǝl ɗǝmwaˈyiˈyar kǝra nju ngga ǝnga Shatan, ba ji mbiya nyi ǝnga ǝpa liyangǝ nǝ fa duburam.
REV 20:3 Ji vakuwa nyi a gyu kaˈu dzǝgam gagaɗǝ ta ba ji haɗiya, tǝma, kǝ ji dzǝgwa kuɓǝlǝri ba ji fǝr mǝtsamǝ ari aga ja kari nyi ara ɓǝra ngguta nji kǝl ma fa duburam kǝ tǝrabiya. Ayukuɗa kau, nju ɓǝra siya nyi nǝ pǝci kushu.
REV 20:4 Ba yi lari tsǝkafǝˈyar ǝnga njira vǝr nggya ar nda, nji nǝ nda dǝnama nǝ tǝlkur aga nda numa anǝ duniya. Kǝ yi lari mambǝl njira nji thlana kǝra nda arya sakidar nda ar kǝra Yesu ǝnga ndǝr Hyal. Nanda aˈyi dlǝvǝ sǝr tagǝ kǝ mai ǝnga sǝra wu papa nyi mai, ǝnga nandǝ dlǝwuri mǝtsamǝ nyi ar huɗǝma nda alaga ar tsa nda mai. Ndu ɓǝra ɗa aˈyi ǝnga pi ba nda sǝm tǝlkur ǝnga Kǝrsiti nǝ fa duburam.
REV 20:5 Alenyi nji tǝtǝ wu ɓǝra shili wu pi mai kǝl ma fa duburam kǝ kuɗau. Najakǝ ngǝ hyaˈari sara vǝr tǝ nǝ tanggǝrma.
REV 20:6 Barka ǝnga cicikur anǝ njira uya hyaˈari sara vǝr tǝ nǝ tanggǝrma, arya tǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi aˈyi ǝnga dǝnama ar kǝra nda mai. Ndu ɗa pubuˈyar nǝ Hyal ǝnga nǝ Kǝrsiti, ndu sǝm tǝlkur ǝnga ja nǝ fa duburam.
REV 20:7 Ayukuɗa fa duburam kau, nju nda siya Shatan sara ar vira nji mbiya nyi ari.
REV 20:8 Ba ja biya maˈyi a nda ngguta nju huɗa duniya ǝnga dǝla duniya patǝu. Ju tsǝmiya Gogu ǝnga Magogu aga nda sa pa. Gangǝkura nda ndu ɗa ǝnggǝr mǝshiˈwa nǝ miya dǝl.
REV 20:9 Ndǝ ɓau, ba ndǝ zǝwari miya cira duniya patǝu, ǝnga ndǝ zǝwar mǝlmǝ kǝra Hyal wu yiwu, ca ngǝ kaɓǝ nji gǝ Hyal wu kwapatǝu. Ama kǝ uˈu shida sara dǝmǝlmau ba ji sa sǝmku nda.
REV 20:10 Shatan kǝra nggutana nda ba nja vakuwa nyi a gu faˈa nǝ uˈur kǝtsa kǝra pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni, vira nji vakuwa sǝr tagǝ ǝnga nabi fati ta a gwa gwa. Nju nda nǝ nda ɓwaɓwatǝ vuˈyi ǝnga pǝci baˈanuwa.
REV 20:11 Tǝma, kǝ yi lari madiya tsǝkafǝ pǝrtǝu ǝnga ndǝra vǝr nggya a dari. Dǝmǝlmau ǝnga gyiwu ˈyi wu hwi ara ja, tsu vir nggya aˈyi ara nda mai.
REV 20:12 Kǝ yi lari njira kuɗau, nji yiɗǝɗǝu ǝnga nji nggunggurǝm tataˈyi wu mwar tsǝkafa nyi. Kǝ nji pahǝna lǝkakaɗǝˈyar. Kǝ nji ɓǝra pahǝna vanyi lǝkakaɗau, ca ngǝ lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ pi. Nji mǝliya nyi numa anǝ njira kuɗau tsaˈa aga sǝra mǝla nda wu pǝci kǝra nda wu duniya ǝnggǝr kǝra nji tsǝfǝya a gu lǝkakaɗǝˈyar kau.
REV 20:13 Kǝ tsadǝ lǝri njira kuɗau wu nda ba tau ǝnga nji gǝ mambǝl tsu lǝri njira tau wu nda. Kǝ kalar ndǝ, nju mǝliya nyi numa tsaˈa aga sǝra ji mǝliya.
REV 20:14 Kǝ tau ǝnga nji gǝ mambǝl kǝ nji vakuwa nda a gu faˈa nǝ uˈur kǝtsa ca ngǝ tǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi.
REV 20:15 Kalar ndǝra nji gǝra uya thlǝmǝ nyi wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ pi kau, ba nja vakuwa nyi a gu faˈa nǝ uˈur kǝtsa.
REV 21:1 Kǝ yi lari dǝmǝlmǝ mafǝliyangǝ ǝnga gyiwu ˈyi mafǝliyangǝu, arya dǝmǝlmǝ ǝnga gyiwu ˈyi nǝ tanggǝrma a tǝrabiyari, tsu tsadu aˈyi tsu mai.
REV 21:2 Kǝ yi lari Mǝlmǝ Cicau, Urshalima mafǝliyangǝ a vǝr shida sara a dǝmǝlmau, sara dara Hyal ǝnggǝr kwanjili kǝra ɓathlǝr dzǝ mǝnahǝu aga sǝkǝ salkwanjili.
REV 21:3 Kǝ yi nggari vanyi ɗahǝ dzǝdzǝgamǝu sara dar tsǝkafǝ kau, wu na, “Vir nggya Hyal a ɗari ǝkkǝˈyi nji, ju nggya ǝkkǝˈyi nda, ndu ɗa nji nyi ba Hyal ǝnga kǝrnyi wu nggya ǝkkǝˈyi nda ba ja ɗa Hyalǝr nda.
REV 21:4 Ju nda ɗana nda sǝlǝm wu liya nda. Tsu nju ɓǝra tǝ mai, sǝˈyinggu aˈyi alaga tiwi ǝnga kwakwaɗǝkur nggyabiya aˈyi mai, ara sǝ ɗǝɗǝmǝ a tǝrabiyari.”
REV 21:5 Ndǝra vǝr nggya ar tsǝkafǝ kǝ na, “Kǝja ya vǝr mǝl kalar sǝ ja ɗa mafǝliyangǝu!” Kǝ ji ɓǝra na, “Tsǝfǝya sǝˈyar kǝ patǝu, arya sǝˈyar kǝ gu sǝn fǝr kǝr ǝnga nda ǝnga jiri nga nda.”
REV 21:6 Kǝ ji nar ɗa, “A ɗari. Nayi ngǝ Alǝfa ǝnga Omega, Dzǝguya ǝnga Kuɗiya. Anǝ ndǝra ǝnga hili yu nǝ nyi ˈyimir sa kurthlǝu, sara a vu mandǝli ˈyimi nǝ pi.
REV 21:7 Ndǝra sǝmku tǝlkur ju ɗa ndǝr faˈa ki ɗa. Ba ya ɗa Hyal nyi ǝnga ba ja ɗa zǝr ɗa.
REV 21:8 Ama njir hivǝr ǝnga njira gǝra hǝnggǝri ǝnga njir mǝl sǝ dedeɓǝu ǝnga njir tsa ndau ǝnga nji sǝsu ǝnga njir pipitima ǝnga njir nu katǝu ba ǝnga njir fati, vir nggyar nda wu nda ɗa wu faˈa nǝ uˈur kǝtsa kǝra pǝrtǝ pwahǝu wu shuni. Najakǝ ngǝ tǝ nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi.”
REV 21:9 Pathlǝ wu pama waladiˈyar mǝɗǝfǝ ta kǝra ǝnga ǝgwa mǝɗǝfǝ nyinyi ǝnga ɓwaɓwatǝ mǝɗǝfǝ shida ka sa na anǝ ɗa. “Shili, yu canǝ ngǝ kwanjila nyi, mala Zǝr Gamǝ kau.”
REV 21:10 Kǝ ji hǝri ɗa wu mambǝl a dar vanyi madiya mǝ dzǝgamǝu, kǝ ji canǝ ɗa Urshalima Mǝlmǝ Cici kau, a vǝr shida sara a dǝmǝlmau sara dara Hyal.
REV 21:11 Ju mbǝl ǝnga kadakadarkur nǝ Hyal, ju mbǝl ǝnggǝr tsǝka dudur kǝra wu mbǝl ǝnggǝr doragalu.
REV 21:12 Aˈyi ja ǝnga madiya mahwal dzǝgam kǝra zǝwuya nyi ǝnga miyar gwa kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu ǝnga waladiˈyar kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu ǝnga ar kalar miyar gwa waladi pathlǝu. Ar kalar miyar gwa kau, nji tsǝfǝya thlǝmǝr culi nǝ njir Izirayila pathlǝ pathlǝu.
REV 21:13 Miyar gwa makǝr a dǝ Sǝbiyar Pǝci ǝnga miyar gwa makǝr a yi Gya Vuya ǝnga miyar gwa makǝr a gwa Dǝ Fwahǝu ǝnga miyar gwa makǝr a yi Gwa Tǝɗǝ Pǝci.
REV 21:14 Nji hǝriya mahwal kau ar fǝhi nǝ tsǝka kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu, ar tsǝka fǝhi kau nga nji tsǝfǝya thlǝmǝr cama sǝsǝˈyar kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ nǝ Zǝr Gamǝu.
REV 21:15 Waladi kǝra ndǝr anǝ ɗa kau, sǝr tǝkǝ sǝ aˈyi ara ja nǝ ǝndzǝ aga ja tǝkǝri mǝlmǝ kau ǝnga miyar gwa ba ǝnga mahwala nyi.
REV 21:16 Mǝlmǝ kau, tugukura nyi ǝnga dlaɓǝkura ja ghǝragǝ nga nyi. Ji tǝkǝri ǝnga sǝr tǝkǝ sǝ nyi, tugukura nyi melu 1,400 ǝnga dzǝgamǝkura nyi ba ǝnga dlaɓǝkura nyi abangǝ tsu.
REV 21:17 Dzǝgamǝkura mahwala nyi a kari hi 200, sǝr tǝkǝ sǝ nǝ nji kǝra waladi kǝ a vǝr tǝkǝ sǝ ǝni.
REV 21:18 Nji hǝriya mahwal kau ǝnga tsǝka jaspa ǝnga mǝlma nyi nji hǝriya ǝnga ǝndzau, kǝra camǝ ǝnggǝr kwalaba.
REV 21:19 Fǝ hiya mahwal kǝ nji ɓathlǝri ǝnga kalar tsǝka duduru. Nǝ tanggǝrma tsǝka jaspa ǝnga nǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi tsǝka safayasu ǝnga nǝ makǝrkura nyi tsǝka kalsidoni ǝnga nǝ foɗǝkura nyi tsǝka imiralǝdu
REV 21:20 ǝnga nǝ tǝfukura nyi tsǝka sardonisu ǝnga nǝ kwakura nyi tsǝka karneliyanu ǝnga nǝ mǝɗǝfǝkura nyi tsǝka kǝrisolatu ǝnga nǝ cisǝkura nyi tsǝka bǝryalu ǝnga nǝ ǝdlǝkura nyi tsǝka topasu ǝnga nǝ kumokura nyi tsǝka krisofǝresu ǝnga nǝ kumo asǝrtangǝkura nyi tsǝka jasinthlǝu ba ǝnga nǝ kumo apǝ mǝthlǝkura nyi tsǝka amithliyasu.
REV 21:21 Miyar gwa kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ kau, ca ngǝ handzǝlkwa kumo apǝ mǝthlǝu. Kalar miyar gwa kau, nju mǝliya nyi ǝnga handzǝlkwa pathlǝu. Lagu dǝdǝgal nǝ huɗa mǝlmǝ kau, nji mǝliya nda ǝnga ˈyimir ǝndzau, kǝra wu mbǝl wilwilu ǝnggǝr kwalaba.
REV 21:22 Nayi aˈyi lar ki Hyal wu mǝlmǝ kǝ mai, arya Hyal Ndǝ Dǝgal Dǝnama ǝnga Zǝr Gamǝ nanda ngǝ ki Hyal nǝ mǝlmǝ kau.
REV 21:23 Mǝlmǝ kǝ aˈyi wu yiwu pǝci ǝnga hya nda mbǝl a gya gwa mai arya kadakadarkur nǝ Hyal ǝnga kǝrnyi ngu lǝ mbǝmbǝl anǝ nyi ǝnga Zǝr Gamǝ tsu naja ngǝ pitǝlla nyi.
REV 21:24 Ənga mbǝmbǝl nyi ngǝ njir duniya wu nda ɓǝr nda ǝnga tǝlˈyar nǝ duniya wu nda shili ǝnga dlǝdlǝvǝkur nda a vuwa gwa.
REV 21:25 Pǝci aˈyi kǝra nju nda haɗiya miya miyar gwaˈyar nǝ mǝlmǝ kǝ mai, ara vuˈyi aˈyi a ndǝna mai.
REV 21:26 Nju nda shili ǝnga kadakadarkur ǝnga dlǝdlǝvǝkur nǝ njir duniya a vu mǝlmǝ kau.
REV 21:27 Saˈyi kǝra gǝra cicau, kǝra wu nda gwa gwa mai, alaga ndǝr mǝl sǝ gǝra sǝli ǝnga ndǝr ngguta nju nda gwagwa mai, kǝl njira nji tsǝfǝya thlǝmǝr nda wu lǝkakaɗǝ pi nǝ Zǝr Gamǝu.
REV 22:1 Kǝ waladi kǝ canǝ ɗa dǝl nǝ ˈyimi nǝ pi, kǝra wu mbǝl wilwilu ǝnggǝr doragalǝu, kǝra a vǝr huhwi sara dar tsǝkafǝ nǝ Hyal ǝnga nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ
REV 22:2 a gyar hada lagu nǝ hada mǝlmau. Wu nǝ pi kau, dadakǝ ngǝ nggilanga ja ar ghimbila dǝl kau. Wu kau, wu ya yayar wu kumo apǝ mǝthlǝ wu fa, ju ya wazha kalar hya. Hyali wu kau kundzǝgǝ ngau aga shilǝgǝ ˈyiˈyi pampamǝu.
REV 22:3 Tsu shiˈwu nǝ Hyal wu ɓǝra ɗa wu mǝlmǝ kǝ mai. Tsǝkafǝ nǝ Hyal ǝnga nǝ Zǝr Gamǝ wu nda ɗa wu mǝlmǝ kau. Njir mǝl thlǝr nyi wu nda dlǝvǝ nyi.
REV 22:4 Ndu nda lari bama ja. Thlǝmǝ nyi tsu wu nda ɗa tsǝtsǝfǝ ar huɗǝma nda.
REV 22:5 Tsu vuˈyi wu nda ɗa mai. Tsu nju ɓǝra nda yiwu vanyi mbǝmbǝl pitǝlla alaga mbǝl pǝci kǝra wu shili ǝnga mbǝmbǝl mai, arya Hyal ǝnga kǝrnyi ngu nda ɗa mbǝmbǝl anǝ nda. Ndu nda sǝm tǝlkur baˈanuwa.
REV 22:6 Kǝ waladi kǝ nar ɗa, “Ndǝr kau, ndǝr kǝra ndu sǝn fǝr kǝr ǝni ngau ǝnga ndǝr jiri ngau. Hyal Thlagǝu, thlagǝr mambǝlˈyar nǝ nabiˈyar, ngǝ sǝwa waladi nyi aga ja cabiya anǝ njir mǝl thlǝr nyi sǝra wu nda ɗa kajangǝkau.”
REV 22:7 “Nggara mau, kǝja ya vǝr shida kajangǝkau! Barka anǝ ndǝra ɓǝlari ndǝrhaha kau, kǝra wu lǝkakaɗǝ kau.”
REV 22:8 Nayi Yahwana, Nayi ngǝ nggari ǝnga lari sǝˈyar kau. Ama ta yi lari, kǝ yi nggari, kǝ yi ɓǝliya undi aga ya dlǝvǝ waladi kǝra canǝ ɗa sǝˈyar kau.
REV 22:9 Ama kǝ ji nar ɗa, “Ga sara mǝl abangǝ mai! Nayi ndǝr mǝl thlǝr kuvwar hyi ngau, nagǝ ǝnga zamǝ ngǝˈyar nabiˈyar ǝnga kalar njira ɓǝlari ndǝr lǝkakaɗǝ kau. Ga dlǝvǝ Hyal!”
REV 22:10 Kǝ ji nar ɗa, “Ga sara ghiɗǝna ndǝr nǝ ndǝrhaha nǝ lǝkakaɗǝ kǝ mai, arya pǝci a ɗari lǝhǝu.
REV 22:11 Taˈyi njir mǝl sǝ ɗǝmwaˈyu nda dumwa ǝnga mǝl sǝ ɗǝmwaˈyir nda, njir mǝl sǝ gǝra tsatsaˈa tsu nda dumwa ǝnga mǝl sǝra gǝra tsatsaˈa, njir mǝl sǝ tsapǝu nda dumwa ǝnga mǝl sǝra tsapǝu, nji cicau nda dumwa ǝnga mǝl sǝra cicau.”
REV 22:12 “Nggara mau, kǝja ya vǝr shili kajangǝkau! Akkǝri ɗa aˈyi ǝnga yau, ba ya nda nǝ nyi anǝ kalar ndǝ tsaˈa aga sǝr mǝla ja.
REV 22:13 Nayi ngǝ Alǝfa ǝnga Omega, Tanggǝrma ǝnga Jomǝ ndǝl, Dzǝguya ǝnga Kuɗiya.
REV 22:14 “Barka anǝ njira cina kar har nda aga nda uya lagur sǝm Wu Nǝ Pi, ba nda gwu huɗa mǝlmǝ lagu miyar gwa.
REV 22:15 Abiya ngǝ hyaˈyar ǝnga njir pipitima ǝnga nji sǝsu ǝnga njir tsa ndau ǝnga njir nu katǝu ba ǝnga kalar njir yiwu fati ǝnga mǝl thlǝr fati.
REV 22:16 “Nayi Yesu, a sǝwari yi waladi ɗa aga ja nǝ ngǝ sakida kau aga ga nǝ nyi anǝ daɓǝr njir nu. Nayi ngǝ culi ǝnga nggyilanga Dawuda ǝnga nayi ngǝ shashilga vǝlang.”
REV 22:17 Mambǝl ǝnga kwanjili kǝ na, “Shila mau!” Kalar ndǝra nggar ɗa, taˈyi ja na, “Shila mau!” Kalar ndǝra ǝnga hili, taˈyi ja shili ǝnga kalar ndǝra wu yiwu aga ja uya ˈyimi nǝ pi, bǝgǝ ja dlǝwuri kurthlǝu.
REV 22:18 Yu tǝɗǝ himiya kalar ndǝra wu nggar ndǝr nǝ lǝkakaɗǝ ndǝrhaha kau, ma ndǝra cakǝri a dagǝri, Hyal wu nda cakǝr nyi ɓwaɓwatǝ kǝra Hyal nana wu lǝkakaɗǝ nyi kau.
REV 22:19 Ma ndǝra gǝnna ndǝr sara wu lǝkakaɗǝ nǝ ndǝrhaha kau, Hyal wu nda hǝbiya nǝ nya nubwa nǝ mǝsahǝkur sara wu wu nǝ pi ǝnga sara wu mǝlmǝ cici nǝ Hyal, ǝnggǝr kǝra nji tsǝfǝri wu lǝkakaɗǝ kau.
REV 22:20 Ndǝra lǝr sakida sǝˈyar kǝ na, “Angǝ, ya vǝr shili kajangǝkau.” Amina, Shili, Thlagǝ Yesu.
REV 22:21 Taˈyi mayiwakur nǝ Thlagǝ Yesu a nggya ǝkkǝˈyi nji cici gǝ Hyal patǝu. Amina.
